A kipat cil in Pasian in vantung le leitung a piangsak hi.
Pasian in, “Khuavak om hen,” ci hi; tua ciangin khuavak om pah hi.
Nitak hong bei in zingsang hong tung a, ni thum ni ahi hi.
Nitak hong bei in zingsang hong tung a, ni li ni ahi hi.
Nitak hong bei in zingsang hong tung a, a ni nga ni ahi hi.
Tua ahih ciangin vantung, leitung, le a sunga omte khempeuh kiman khin hi.
Tua ciangin leitung panin meiilum kaaito in, lei maitang khempeuh a buah hunin
Tua gam a khamte hoih hi. Tua munah bedolak singnai le onik suang om hi.
A nihna gun min Gihon hi a, Kush gam kimkotah a luang pen ahi hi.
Topa Pasian in mipala in, Eden huan kho in a kem dingin a koih hi.
Mipa le a zi a guaktangin om uh a, maizum lo uh hi.
Tu in gulpi pen, Topa Pasian' bawlsa gamlak ganhing dangte khempeuh sangin ngiansiam zaw hi. Amah'n numei kiangah, “Pasian in, ‘Huan sung singgah khat peuhpeuh ne loding,' hong ci ahi hiam?” ci hi.
Numei in gulpi kiangah, “Huan sung singgahte ka ne theiding uh hi.
Ahih hangin gulpi in numei kiangah, “Na si keiding uh hi.
Ahih hangin Topa Pasian in mipa samin ama kiangah, “Koi laiah om na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n, “Na guaktanga na omna kua in hong gen ahi hiam? Na nek loh dinga kong thupiak singgah ne kha na hi hiam?” ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa Pasian in numei kiangah, “Bangci a hici gamtat na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Numei in, “Gulpi in kei hong khem a, ka ne hi,” ci hi.
Tua hun sungin Kain in lei pana pianggah piakna Topa' tungah paipih a,
Topa'n Kain tungah, “Bang hangin nang heh a, bang hangin na mai sia ahi hiam?
Limtakin hih lecin, nang hong kisang loding ahi hiam? Limtakin na hih kei le nang hong hih nuamin mawhna in hong buk a, nang hong uk nuam hi. Ahih hangin nang in tua mawhna na zawhding ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Kain tungah, “Na sanggampa Abel koiah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Ka thei kei hi. Kei, ka sanggam a kempa ka hi hiam?” ci hi.
Topa'n, “Bang hangin hici gamtat na hi hiam? Na sanggampa' sisan, leilak panin kei tungah hong kiko hi.
Kain in Topa' tungah, “Keimah gim hong kipiakna, ka thuak zawhding hi lo hi.
Enosh kum sawmkua a phak ciangin, amah in Kenan kici tapa khat nei hi.
Kenan kum sawmsagih a phak ciangin, Mahalalel kici tapa khat nei hi.
Mahalalel kum sawmguk le kum nga a phak ciangin Jared kici tapa khat nei hi.
Enok kum sawmguk le kum nga a phak ciangin, Methuselah kici tapa khat nei hi.
Lamek kum za le kum sawmgiat le nih a phak ciangin tapa khat nei a,
Leitungah mite tam dingin hong kipanin, amau' sung panin tanute hong suah ciangin,
Ahih hangin Noah in Topa' maipha mu hi.
Noah in tapa thum, Shem, Ham, le Jafeth a nei hi.
Tu in Pasian' muhnaah leitung sia a, leitungah ngongtatna kidim hi.
Teembaw a dingin kongkhak khat bawl inla, tua tungpi khat le alang ciangah zawh bawl in. A pangah teembaw kongkhak bulh in. A dawl nuainung, a dawl nihna le a dawl thumnate bawl in.
Noah zong tua bangmahin gamta a, Pasian' thupiak khempeuh a hih hi.
Ganhing siangtho nupa kop sagih, ganhing a siang lo nupa kop khat,
huih lak vasate zong nupa kop sagih, leitungah amau' nam a manthan loh nadinginla in.
Noah in zong Topa' thupiak khempeuh a hih hi.
Leitungah tuiciin a tun lai in Noah kum zaguk pha hi.
Ganhing siangthote, a siang lo ganhingte, vasate, leitung aa bokvak peuhmah,
A ni sagih ni in leitungah tuiciin tung hi.
Sun sawmli le zan sawmli sung leitungah guah zu hi.
Tui khangto in leitungah tam mahmah hi. Tui tungah teembaw laam hi.
Leitungah tui khangkhang ahih manin mual lian a sangte khempeuh tuumcip hi.
Leitungah a om, nuntakna hu a nei peuhmah a si uh hi.
Ni za le ni sawmnga sung leitungah tui om hi.
Tui thukte le vantung tawlette kikhak a, vantung pana guahte kikhawlsak hi.
Kha sagihna, tua kha ni sawm le sagih ni in Ararat mualtungah teembaw kinga hi.
Ni sawmli a cin ni ciangin Noah in ama bawlsa teembaw tawlet hong a,
va-ak khat khah hi. Leitung panin tuite a keu mateng leeng kawikawi hi.
Amah'n ni sagih sung ngakin, teembaw panin a vakhu khah leuleu hi.
A kha nihna, tua kha ni sawmnih le sagih ni in leitung keu hi.
Tua ciangin Pasian in Noah kiangah,
“Nang le na zi, na tapate le na tapate' zite, teembaw sung panin paikhia un.
Note pen leitung ganhing khempeuh, huih lak vasa khempeuh, leilakah a bokvak khempeuh le tuipi ngasa khempeuh in hong kihta in hong zahtakding uh hi. Note' khut sungah tuate hong kipia hi.
Tua ciangin Pasian in Noah le amah tawh a om a tapate kiangah,
“En un, note le note' khit a na suanlekhakte uh le,
note tawh a om nuntakna a nei peuhmah, vasate, innsate, note tawh a om leitung gamsa peuhmah, teembaw sung panin a paikhia zahzah peuhmah tawh ka thuciamna ka kipsak hi.
Vantungah meii kong kaisak ciangin meii sungah sakhituihup a kimuh leh,
Teembaw sung panin a paikhia Noah' tapate, Shem, Ham, le Jafeth ahi hi. Ham pen Kanaan'pa ahi hi.
Hih Noah' tapa thumte panin leitung buppi mi tawh hong kidim hi.
Noah pen lo kho masapa hi a, amah in leenggui lo khat a bawl hi.
Amah'n leenggahzu ne in kham a, a puanbuk sungah bangmah silh loin a lum hi.
Noah a zukhamna panin a pilvan' ciangin ama tungah a tapa Ham' gamtatna thei a,
amah in, “Kanaan in samsiatna ngahta henla, a sanggamte' sila hi tahen.
Topa ka Pasian in Shem thupha pia henla, Kanaan, ama sila hisak hen.
Tuiciin a tun khit ciangin Noah kum zathum le kum sawmnga nungta hi.
Jafeth' tapate: Gomer, Magog, Madai, Javan, le Tiras ahi hi.
Gomer' tapate: Ashkenaz, Rifath, le Togarmah ahi hi.
Javan' tapate: Elishah, Tarshish, Kittim, le Dodanim ahi hi.
Ham' tapate: Kush, Egypt, Put, le Kanaan ahi hi.
Tua gam panin Assiria gam sungah amah pai in Nineveh, Rehoboth-Ir, Kalah, le
Egypt pen Lud mite, Anam mite, Lehab mite, Naftuh mite,
Pathru mite, Kasluh mite (Filistia mite' pianna), le Kaftor mite' pianna pupi ahi hi.
Kanaan pen ama sung pan a suak masa Sidon, Heth,
le Jebus mite, Amor mite, Girgash mite,
Hiv mite, Arki mite, Sin mite,
Hihte pen a innkuan, a kam pau, a leitang, a minamin Ham' suanlekhakte ahi hi.
Eber mi khempeuh' pianna pupi, Jafeth' u, Shem' sung panin zong tate hong piang hi.
Shem' tapate: Elam, Asshur, Arpakshad, Lud, le Aram ahi hi.
Aram' tapate: Uz, Hul, Gether, le Mash ahi hi.
Joktan pen Almodad, Shelef, Hazarmaveth, Jerah,
Hadoram, Uzal, Diklah,
Obal, Abimael, Sheba,
Ofir, Havilah, le Jobab' piannapa ahi hi. Hihte khempeuh Joktan' tapate ahi hi.
Amau' tenna gam pen Mesha panin kipanin Sefar lamah nisuahna gam mualtung dong ban hi.
Tua laitakin leitung buppi in kampau khat le kammal tawmno bek nei hi.
Tua ciangin mihingte' lamsa khuapi le tausangpi a en dingin Topa hong paisuk hi.
Shelah kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin Eber kici tapa khat nei hi.
Peleg kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin amah in Reu kici tapa khat nei hi.
Serug kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin amah in Nahor kici tapa khat nei hi.
Terah a suah khit ciangin Nahor kum za le sawm le kua nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang neilai hi.
Terah kum sawmsagih a phak khit ciangin amah in Abram, Nahor, le Haran a nei hi.
Tu in Sarai ciing a,ta nei lo hi.
Terah in ama tapa Abram le Haran' tapa, ama tupa ahi Lot, le a tapa Abram' zi ahi a monu Sarai samin, Kanaan gam sungah a pai dingin Khaldea gam Ur khua panin amaute a paikhia khawm uh hi. Ahi zongin amaute Haran a tun uh ciangin tua munah a teng uh hi.
Terah' khansung kum zanih le kum nga hi a, Haranah Terah a si hi.
Abram in a khualzin zom lai a, Negeb gam lam manawhin a pai lai hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Faro in Abram samin, “Bang hangin hih bangin kei hong bawl na hi hiam? Amah na zi ahihna bang hangin kei kiangah hong gen lo na hi hiam?
Ka zi dingin amah ka lak theih nadingin, ‘Amah ka sanggamnu hi,' bang hangin hong ci na hi hiam? Tu in hih laiah na zi om hi. Amahla inla pai un,” a ci hi.
Abram in ganhing, ngun, le kham hau mahmah hi.
Abram tawh a paikhawm Lot in zong tuuhon, ganhon, le puanbukte nei hi.
Na maiah gam buppi om hi lo ahi hiam? Kei' kiang panin nangmah paikhia tawm in. Nang in veilam na lak leh, kei taklamah ka paiding hi. Tua ahih kei leh zong, nang in taklam na lak leh, kei veilamah ka paiding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua laitakin Sodom mite migi lo hi a, Topa' tungah nakpitakin a khialte ahi hi.
le amau' gam Seir Mual tunga Hori mite hong zo uh hi.

Amah'n a pualamah paipih a, “Vantung lam enin aksite sim in; na sim thei hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Na suanlekhakte, tua mah bangding hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin amah in, “Topa Pasian aw, keimah in tua leitang ka neih nading bangci theihding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Sasialne vasate tua sate tungah hong tuk suk ciangin Abram in tuate a hawlkhia hi.
Ken mite, Kenaz mite, Kadmon mite,
Hit mite, Perez mite, Refaim mite,
Amah'n, “Sarai' sila numei Hagar aw, koi pan hong pai a, koiah paiding na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Ka tonu Sarai' kiang panin a taikhia ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin ama tungah thu a gen Topa pen, “Nang, a mu thei Pasian khat na hi hi,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Keimah in Pasian mu khin taktakin, amah ka muh khit ciangin hing lai hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.

Nang tawh thuciamna ka bawlding a, nang tampi tak kong phasakding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Abram mai kunsuk hi. Pasian in ama kiangah,
Note' vun dawn ki-atding a, tua pen kei le note' kikalah thuciamna lim khat hiding hi.
Note' lak panin ni giat a pha peuhmahpa a vun ki-atding hi. Note' khang tawntungin pasal peuhmah, note' inn sunga suak hitaleh, noteta ahi lo, gamdang mi khatpeuh kiang panin na sum uh tawh na lei uh hitaleh
Tua ciangin Abraham mai kun sukin nui a, amahmah tungah, “Kum za a pha pasal khat inta neiding ahi hiam? Kum sawmkua a pha Sarah inta neiding ahi hiam?” kici hi.
Abraham in Pasian' kiangah, “Ishmael hong nungtasak peuh lecin,” a ci hi.
Amah tawh a kiho a man khit ciangin Abraham' kiang panin Pasian paikhia to hi.
Ama vun dawn a ki-atin Abraham kum sawmkua le kua phata hi.
Ama vun dawn a ki-atin a tapa Ishmael kum sawm le thum a pha hi.
Tua ni mahmahin Abraham le a tapa Ishmael a vun uh ki-at hi.
“Ka tote aw, nong hehpihna-un na sempa hong kheng kei un.
Amaute'n ama kiangah, “Na zi Sarah koiah om ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amah'n, “Puanbuk sungah om hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Sarah amahmah nui in, “Kei ka teek khit, ka topa zong a teek khitin tua bang hi thei nawnding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Topa'n Abraham' tungah, “Bang hangin Sarah nui in, ‘Tu in kei teek ka hih cianginta nei takpiding ka hi hiam?' ci ahi hiam?
Na khat peuhpeuh Topa a dingin haksa lua ahi hiam? A kisehsa tuzawh kha kua ciangin nang kiangah kong paikikding a, Sarah in tapa khat neiding hi,” a ci hi.
Topa'n a lungsimah, “Abraham a lian a thahat minam suakin, leitung minam khempeuh in ama thupha ngah bangin thupha a ngah nadingun hong ngending hi, ci in thei ahih manin, tu-a ka hihding thu Abraham' tungah imding ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Abraham in hong naihin, “Thuman mite, migilote tawh susia khawm takpiding na hi hiam?
Tua khuapi sungah thuman mi sawmnga bang om leh, tua sunga om thuman mi sawmngate' hangin khah loin tua khua susia teiteiding na hi hiam?
Thuman mite, migilote tawh a kibat nadingin migilote tawh thuman mite thahkhawmding, hi theiding ahi hiam? Tua pen hi thei loding hi. Leitung khempeuh Thukhenpa a manin gamta loding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Thuman mi sawmnga sung panin nga om kei leh? Tua nga a om loh manin khuapi buppi na susia veveding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Tua sungah sawmli le nga ka muh nakleh ka susia keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Amaute'n Lot sam uh a, “Tu nitak a nang kiangah hong tung mite koiah om ahi hiam? Amau' taw ka luk theih nadingun ko kiangah amaute hong paikhiatpih in,” a ci uh hi.
Lot, kongkhak puaah mite kiangah pai in kong lehkhak a,
“Ka sanggamte aw, tua banga na gitloh gamtat loh nading uh kong thum hi.
Ahih hangin amaute in, “Taikhia in. Kote kiangah hong peem pak a, tu in nang thukhen hong kineihding na hi hiam? Tu in amaute sangin nang kong siatbawl zawding uh hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amaute in nakpitakin Lot' lam hong neh uh a, kongkhak a phukham zah dongin hong neh uh hi.
Tua ciangin mi nihte in Lot kiangah, “Hih laiah tanau dang na nei hiam? Makte, tapate, ahih kei leh khua sunga nang' mi peuhpeuh hih mun panin paikhiatpih in.
Ahi zongin Lot in amaute tungah, “Hi lo hi, ka tote aw;
En un, gal-a om khuapi, tai nadingin nai a, khuapi neu khat ahi hi. Tua laiah hong taisak un - khuapi neu khat hi lo ahi hiam? tua hileh ka suaktading hi,” a ci hi.
Zoarah Lot a tun ciangin tua laiah ni suak khinta hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n vantung panin Sodom le Gomorrah khuate tungah kaat le meikuang zusak hi.
Ahih hangin a nunga om Lot' zi nunghei a, amah ci khuam a suak hi.
Topa' mai-a a dinnasa munah zingsang tungin Abraham va pai hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Lot' tanu tegel in apa uh tawh naupaii uh hi.
Ahi zongin Abimelek in amah zuan nai lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in, “Topa aw, nang in midikpa thatding na hi hiam?
Amahmah in kei kiangah, ‘Amah, ka sanggamnu ahi hi,' hong ci hi lo ahi hiam? A numei mahmah in zong, ‘Amah, ka sanggampa ahi hi,' hong ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin lungsim kisuang hetloin a gamta ka hi a, khial ka kisa kei hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Abimelek in Abraham samin ama kiangah, “Bang hangin ko tungah hong hici gamtat na hi hiam? Kei le ka kumpi gam sungah khialhna lianpi khat nong tut nadingin nang' tungah bang khialhna nei ka hi uh hiam? Hih dinga kilawm lo nate kei' tungah nong hih hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Abimelek in Abraham' kiangah, “Hih banga na gamtat nadingin bang ngaihsun na hi hiam?” ci lai hi.
Abraham in Sarah tawh a neih ama tapa' min dingin Isaac a phuak hi.
A tapa Isaac a suah ciangin Abraham kum za pha hi.
Amah'n, “Sarah in nau nawi piading ci in kua in Abraham' tungah gen ngeiding ahi hiam? Ahi zongin a teek khitin amah tawh tapa khat ka nei hi,” a ci hi.
Ama tapa' hangin Abraham' tungah thu nuam het lo hi.

Pasian in naupang' kahna aw a za hi. Pasian' vantungmi in vantung panin Hagar sam a, ama kiangah, “Hagar aw, bang in hong lungkhamsak ahi hiam? Lau kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh naupang a omna munah a kahna awging Pasian in za hi.
Abraham in, “Ka kiciamding hi,” a ci hi.
Abraham in a tuuhon sung panin tuununo sagih tuam koih hi.

Filistia mite' leitangah Abraham, sauveipi sung peemta in a om hi.

khuapi kulhkongpiah a kikhawm mite khempeuh' mai, Hit mite' omnaah Abraham' neih dingin kipia hi.

Esau in, “Amah Jakob kici mah hi lo ahi hiam? Amah'n kei nihvei hong suankhia khin hi. Amah'n ka innluahza hong sut hi. En in, tu in amah in ka thupha hong sut leuleu hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Kei a dingin thupha siit lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Isaac in Esau dawngin, “En in, amah nangma' topa in ka bawl khin a, a sanggamte khempeuh ama tungah nasemin ka pia khin a, an le leenggahzu tawh amah ka hingsak hi. Tua ahih ciangin kata aw, nang a dingin bang hih thei nawnding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Esau in a pa' kiangah, “Pa aw, thupha khat beek nei nawn lo na hi hiam? Kei thupha hong pia in, kei zong, kapa aw,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Esau a kap hi.

Bang hang hiam cih leh tangvalpa kei tawh hong ton kei leh kapa kiangah bangci ciahkik theiding ka hi hiam? Ka pa' tungah a tungding siatna ka thuakzo keiding hi,” a ci hi.

Gad' tapate: Zifion, Haggi, Shuni, Ezbon, Eri, Arodi, le Areli ahi hi.
Jakob' zi Rachel' tapate: Josef le Benjamin ahi hi.
Benjamin' tapate: Bela, Bekher, Ashbel, Gera, Naaman, Ehi, Rosh, Muppim, Huppim, le Ard ahi hi.
Dan' tapa Hushim ahi hi.
Naftali' tapate: Jahzeel, Guni, Jezer, le Shillem ahi hi.
Faro in note hong samin note kiangah, ‘Na nasep uh bang ahi hiam?' hong cih ciangin,
A sanggamte' lak panin amah in mi ngala in Faro' kiangah va paipih hi.
Faro in a sanggamte kiangah, “Na nasep uh bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute'n Faro' kiangah, “Ka pate uh mah bangin na nasem kote pen gankemte ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
Faro in Jakob kiangah, “Na nuntak kum bangzah phata ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Jakob in Faro thupha pia in tua lai panin a paikhia hi.
Egypt gam sung le Kanaan gam sunga sum a bei khit ciangin Egypt mite khempeuh Josef kiangah hong pai in, “Kote an hong pia in. Bang hangin na muhnaah siding ka hi uh hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh ka sum uh beita hi,” a ci uh hi.
Bang hangin kote si in ka leitang uh nangma muhnaah maimawkding ahi hiam? Kote le ka leitang uh an tawh hong lei in. Kote, Faro' sila ka hiding uh a, ka leitang uh zong ama a' hiding hi. Leitang mawkval loin, kote si loin ka hin theih nadingun khaici hong pia in,” a ci uh hi.
Mihingte ahihleh, Egypt mongkhat panin a mongkhat dongin amah in sila in bawl hi.
Israel in Josef' tapate a muh ciangin amah in, “Hihte kua ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
“Jakob' tapate aw, hong kikhawmin za unla, napa Israel' thugen ngai un.
“Simeon le Levi, unau hi a, a hiam uh ngongtat nadingin a zang uh hi.
Judah pen humpinelkai tawh kibang a, a sa matsa a nek khit ciangin a kuaah a ciahkik tawh kibang hi. Humpinelkai bangin kizia in a lumsuk hi. Kua'n amah phawng ngamding hiam?
“Issakhar, a hatla tawh kibang a, vangik nih kikalah a lum hi.
“Dan in Israel minam dangte mah bangin a mite thu khending hi.
“Nong hotkhiatding ka ngak hi, Topa.
“Gad pen a buluhte in buluhding a, ahih hangin amah in amaute sulzuih kikding hi.
“Asher' loah an tampi piangding a, amah in kumpi anlimte bawlding hi.
“Naftali, a kikhah sakhipi hi a, sakhino suakkhiasak hi.
Tua ciangin Josef a pa' tungah pukin, ama tungah kap a, amah a nam hi.
Ahih hangin Josef in amaute kiangah, “Lau kei un. Kei, Pasian' zaah om ka hi hiam?
Note'n ahihleh, kei' tungah a sia dingin na ngaihsun uh hi. Ahih hangin Pasian in tuhuna mah bangin mi tampite a nuntak theihna a pian nadingin a hoih dingin a ngaihsut ahi hi.
Jakob tawh Egyptah a hong pai, amau' innkuan ciat tawh ahi Israel' tapate' minte:
Reuben, Simeon, Levi, le Judah,
Issakhar, Zebulun, le Benjamin,
Dan le Naftali, Gad le Asher ahi hi.
Jakob' suanlekhakte khempeuh mi sawmsagih hi a, Josef pen Egyptah na om khinzo hi.
Tua ciangin Josef le a sanggamte le tua khangmi khempeuh si uh hi.
Tu in Josef a thei lo kumpi thak khat Egypt gamah hong khang hi.
Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Israel mite a gim mahmahin na semsak uh a,
Tua ahih ciangin Egypt kumpipa in naudomte samin amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin hih bangin gamta a, nau pasalte nungtasak na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in naudomte limbawl hi. Mite khangin pawlcing semsem uh hi.
Naudomte in Pasian zahtak uh ahih manin amah in amaute tungah suanlekhak a pia hi.
Tu in Levi' suante khat in Levi numei khat mah zi inla hi.
Tua ciangin a sanggamnu in Faro tanu kiangah, “Keimah pai in Hebru numeite lak panin nang a dingin naupang hong khoisak dingin naucing khat ka va sapsakding hiam?” a ci hi.
A zing ciangin amah paikik a, Hebru mi nih na kilai uh hi. Amah'n a gamta khial mipa kiangah, “Bang hangin na lawm sat na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n dawngin, “Kote' tungah ulianding le thukhen dingin kua in nang hong koih ahi hiam? Egypt mipa na thah bangin kei thahding hong sawm na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Moses lau a, “A thu hong kithei taktak hi,” ci in ngaihsun hi.
Apa uh kiangah amaute a tun ciangun amah in, “A bangci-a tuni-a hong hici ciah baih na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n a tanute kiangah, “Amah koi laiah om ahi hiam? Bang hangin tua mipa nusia na hi uh hiam? Amah'n an hong nek theih nadingin va sam un,” a ci hi.
Pasian in Israel mite mu a, amaute' omzia zong a thei hi.
Ahih hangin Moses in Pasian kiangah, “Faro' kiangah pai in Egypt panin Israel mite a paikhiatpih dingin kei, kua ka hi hiam?” ci hi.
Tua ciangin Moses in Pasian kiangah, “Israel mite kiangah kei va pai in amaute kiangah, ‘Na pate uh' Pasian in note' kiangah kei hong sawl hi,' va ci leng, amaute in, ‘Ama min bang ahi hiam?' ci in hong dong leh, amaute' tungah bang ciding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin keimah in ka khut zanin na lamdangte tawh Egypt ka vatgawpding hi.
Topa'n ama kiangah, “Na khut sungah bang om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Ciangkhut,” ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n ama kiangah, “Kua'n mipa' kam bawl ahi hiam? Kua'n amah pau thei losak, bilngongsak, musak, mittawsak ahi hiam? Topa ahi keimah hi lo ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Moses tungah Topa heh a, amah in, “Levi mi na sanggampa Aaron om hi lo ahi hiam? Amah'n hoihtakin thu a gen theihna ka cian theih hi. En in, nangmah a dawn dingin amah hong paikhia a, amah in nang hong muh ciangin a lungsim sungah amah kipakding hi.
Lampiah a giahna khatah Topa'n Moses dawntuahin thah a sawm hi.
Tua ciangin Moses le Aaron pai in Israel upate khempeuh a kaikhawm uh hi.
Ahih hangin Faro in, “Ama thu mangin Israel mite ka paisakna dingin Topa na cih uh kua ahi hiam? Topa na cih uh ka thei kei hi. Tua tham loin Israelte ka paisak keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Egypt kumpipa in amaute kiangah, “Moses le Aaron aw, bang hangin amau' nasepna panin mite paikhiasakding na hi uh hiam? Na nasepnate uhah pai un,” a ci hi.
Tua ni mahin Faro in nasem ukte le a nasem mapite thu pia a,
Note pai unla, na muhna peuhpeuh uhah na buhtuding uh va zong tawm un. Ahih hangin na nasep ngeizah uh themkhat zong hong kikhiam loding hi,' ci hi,” a ci uh hi.
Israel mi nasem mapi, Faro' nasem ukte in amaute a uk dingin a koih sawn mite kisatin, “Bang hangin tu ciang dong, leiseek bawlding na nasep khempeuh uh hih khin nai lo na hi uh hiam?” ci in kidong hi.

Topa'n Moses le Aaron' kiangah,

Faro' nasemte in ama kiangah, “Eite tungah hih mipa bang tanvei thangzak hong hi nilohding ahi hiam? Amaute'n amau' Pasian, Topa a biak theih nadingun mite paisak in. Egypt a siatna theitel nai lo na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.

Egypt gam sungah Topa'n Moses le Aaron kiangah,
Note' omna inn tunga sisan pen note a dingin lim hiding hi. Sisan ka muh ciangin note kong paisanding a, Egypt leitang ka vatgawp ciangin note hong susiading gimna note' tungah hong tung loding hi.
Note'n silngo sawh loh anlum pawi na bawlding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih ni teekteekin Egypt leitang panin na mihonte uh ka paikhiatpih hi. Tua ahih ciangin note in na khan tawntungun hih ni pen biakna ngeina kip khatin na nei tawntungding uh hi.
Note le na tapate un hih pen biakna ngeina kipin na nei tawntungding uh hi.
Na tate un note kiangah, ‘Hih banga hihna pen bang a cih nopna ahi hiam?' hong cih ciangin,
note in, ‘ Topa' Paisanna hangin biakpiakna ahi hi. Amah'n eite' innkuante hong khawi in Egypt mite a thah lai in Egypt gam sungah Israel innkuante paisan hi,' na ciding uh hi,” a ci hi. Mite'n a lu uh kunin Pasian a bia uh hi.

Abib kha, tuni in note a paikhia na hi uh hi.
Note'n silngo sawh loh anlum ni sagih sung na neding uh a, a ni sagih ni in Topa pahtawina pawi khat omding hi.
note in naubu a hong masa khempeuh Topa a dingin na tuam koihding uh hi. Na ganhing uh a tacil apa khempeuh zong Topa a' hiding hi.
Hong paiding hunah na tapa in, ‘Hih pen bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?' ci in nang hong dot ciangin, nangmah in ama kiangah, ‘Salsuahna, Egypt panin Topa'n vangliatna tawh kote hong paikhiatpih hi.
Sukkoth panin amaute pai lai uh a, sehnel gam nawl, Ethamah giahphual sat uh hi.

‘Kote hong hici omsak inla, Egypt mite' na hong semsak in,' ci in Egyptah nang' tungah hong gen hi lo ka hi uh hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh sehnel gamah sih sangin Egypt mite' na sepding kote a dingin hoihzawding hi,” a ci uh hi.

Na taklam khut na zan a, leitung in amaute nawmvalh hi.

Moses in, “Ama tungah na phunnate uh Topa'n a zakna hangin, Topa'n note' tungah nitak an nekding sa, zingsangin na kham tak uha na nekding uh an hong piak ciangin - kote pen a bang hi mawk ka hi uh hiam? Note' phunnate pen kote' tung hi loin Topa' tung ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Israel mite in a muh uh ciangin amaute khatlekhat in, “Bang ahi hiam?” kici uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in tua pen bang hiam cih thei lo uh hi. Moses in amaute' kiangah, “ Topa'n nek dinga note' tungah hong piak an ahi hi.

Pasian in hih thute khempeuh gen a,
“Keimah longal pasian dang na bia keiding uh hi.

“Mi na that keiding uh hi.
“Nulepa mawhna na bawl keiding uh hi.
“Na na gu keiding uh hi.

Pasian' omna meii sah naiah Moses a pai laitakin mite a gamlaah ading uh hi.
Note'n kei tawh nong biakkhop dingun ngun pasiante le kham pasiante na bawl keiding uh hi.
Note'n keima a dingin lei tawh biakna tau khat bawl unla, tua tungah na meihal biaknate uh le thunuama na biaknate uh, na tuute uh le na bawngtalte uh pia un. Keima min a kiphawk nading munin ka bawlna peuhmahah note kiangah keimah hong pai in note thupha kong piading hi.
Note'n keima a dingin suang tawh biakna tau na bawl uhleh, a kiseek suang tawh na bawl keiding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na nazatte uh tawh na va suk uhleh a ninsak na hi uh hi.
“Tu in hihte pen amaute' tungah na piakding biakna ngeina kipte ahi hi.

“Amapa hitaleh ama nu hitaleh a sat peuhmah kithatding hi.

“Amapa hitaleh ama nu hitaleh a samsia mi peuhmah kithatding hi.

mit tangding mit, ha tangding ha, khut tangding khut, khe tangding khe,

Meigong numei ahi a, tagah ahi zongin na gimsak keiding uh hi.
Note'n amaute na gimsak uh a, amaute keima tungah hong kiko leh, keimah in amau' kikona ka za taktakding hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh ama silhding tua bek hi a, tua pen ama pumpi a dingin a puan neihsun ahi hi. Amah bang dang tawh lumding ahi hiam? Amah kei tungah hong kiko leh ke'n ka zading hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh keimah in hehpihna ka nei hi.
Ama thu neihnaah mizawngpa na langneih keiding uh hi.
“Ama thu neihnaah mizawngpa a thutang kimlai na lelsak keiding uh hi.
“Note'n na leitang uhah kum guk sung khai tuhin a piangte na kaikhawmding uh hi.
Note' tunga kong gente khempeuh thudon un; pasian dangte' min genin nei kei unla, na kam sung panun zong tua bangte kizasak kei un.
“Kum khatin thumvei, keima a dingin pawi na bawlding uh hi.
Topa Pasian ' maiah pasal khempeuh kum khatin thumvei kilaakding uh hi.
Note'n Topa na Pasian uh nong biading uh a, keimah in na an uh le na tui uh thupha ka piading hi. Keimah in note' lak panin cinatna kala khiading hi.
Note' leitangah kuamah nausia om loding a, a ciing zong om loding hi. Note kong teeksihsakding hi.
Note' mai panin Hiv mite, Kanaan mite, le Hit mite a hawlkhia dingin note' maiah tunpi ka sawlkhiading hi.
Note khangin tampi pha in leitang na luah matengun note' mai panin tawm tawmin amaute ka hawlkhiading hi.
Amaute ahi a, amau' pasiante tawh ahi zongin thuciamna na bawl keiding uh hi.

Amaute' tung panin na sanding biakna hih bang ahi hi: Kham, ngun, sumngo,
a kisansak tuutal vunte, keelvunte, singkha sing,
meivakte ading sathau, nilh sathauding le paknamtui dingin a namtui nate,
siampipuan le awmdal a bulh dingin onik suangte ahi hi.
Amaute' lakah kei ka om theih nadingin kei a dingin biakbuk khat amaute bawlsak in.
Nangmah in singkha singzawl na suiding a, tuate kham tawh na zutding hi.
Singkuang puak nadingin singkuang panga kualte sungah a zawlte na khumding hi.
Singkuang' kualte sungah a zawlte omsuakding a, tuate kilakhia loding hi.
Nang' tunga kong piakding thuciamna nangmah in singkuang sungah na koihding hi.
Kham citak tawh na zutding a, a kimkotah a geihual kham tawh na bawlding hi.
Sabuai puak nading zawlte a len dingin a zawl peek geiah a kualte omding hi.

meivakkhuam panin hiang guk a kopte' bulah tua tawh sakhat ahi nun khat omding hi.
A taitehte le a kuangte kham citak hiding hi.

Dalna puan ngate khatlekhat kikhuituahding hi.
Puanbuk puan a val khia, puan alang a val pen, biakbuk nungah kaisukding hi.
“A kisansak tuutal vunte le keelvunte tawh puanbuk khuhna khat na bawlding hi.
“Biakbuk a dingin a po toding khuampeekte singkha sing na bawlding hi.

Amah'n biakna tau tungah khialhna hanga biakna sathau halding hi.
Note na tenna uh Egypt gamah amaute a gamtat bangin note na gamta keiding uh a, note kong paipihna Kanaan gamah zong amaute a gamtat bangin note na gamta keiding uh hi. Note'n amau' gamtatnate na zui keiding uh hi.
Note'n keima biakna ngeina kipte semin ka thukhamte lenin tuate na zuiding uh hi. Kei pen Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi.
Na ni na mawhpih keiding hi; tua nu pen na pa' sanggam numei ahi hi.
Na sanggampa' zi na mawhpih keiding hi; tua pen na sanggampa' mindai nading ahi hi.
Na vengpa' zi tawh na lumkhawm keiding a, tua nu tawh na kininsak keiding hi.
Note a kuamah peuh in na nu le napa uh zahtakin, note in ka Sabbathte na tangding uh hi; kei pen Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi.
Note'n na leenggui lo uh hawkmai loin, leenggah a kiate zong na leenggui lo panun na tawm keiding uh hi. Note'n mizawngte le peemtate a dingin tuate na nusiading uh hi; kei pen Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi.
Note'n a man lopi in keima min tawh na kiciam keiding uh a, tua bangin na Pasian uh' min na daisak keiding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
Note'n bilngongte phuisam loin, mittawte' maiah a puk theih nading nana koih keiding uh a, note in na Pasian uh na zahtakding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
Note'n na mipihte lak uhah mi gensia in vaksuk vakto loin, na vengpa uh a sih nadingin na langpang keiding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
Note'n nomau' mipihte tungah phula loin, amau na lungsim neih keiding uh a, nomau na ki-it uh bangin na vengte uh na itding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
A kum lina ciangin amau'gah khempeuh siangtho in, Topa' tungah phatna biakna hiding hi.
Note'n na baa samte uh met loin na khamul mongte uh zong na tan keiding uh hi.
Note'n mi site' hangin dahna limin na ci tung uh liamsak loin note' tungah ciaptehna khat peuhpeuh zong na sun keiding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
Note'n ka Sabbath ni tangin keimah hong kibiakna mun na zahtakding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
Note lakah a hong peem khualmite tualsung mi mah bangin na ngaihsunding uh a, nomau mah bangin amaute na itding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh note pen Egypt gam sungah khualmi na hi ngei uh hi; kei pen Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi.
Note'n tawi khaina man, tawisuang man, seu man, bung man, na zangding uh hi. Kei pen Egypt gam panin a hong paikhiatpih Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi.
Note'n ka thukhamte khempeuh le ka biakna ngeina kipte khempeuh zui in tuate na semding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Pasal khatpeuh ganhing khat tawh a mawh leh amah le a ganhing kithatding hi.
Note' maiah keimah in ka paihkhiat minamte' ngeinate na zui keiding uh hi. Amaute'n hih nate khempeuh hih uh ahih manin amaute ka kih hi.
Note pen keima a dingin na siangthoding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa ahi keimah ka siangtho a, note pen keima-a' na hih theih nadingun mite kiang panin note kong tuamkoih zo hi.
Amah'n a zi dingin nungaklading hi.
Topa'n Moses tungah,
Bang hang hiam cih leh poina a nei, mittaw, khelbai, maihem, le khutlekhe saulua,
khut liam, khe liam,
Amah'n ama Pasian' anlum, a siangthopen le a siangtho ante ne theiding hi.
Note'n a sitbaang khat peuhpeuh na pia keiding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh hong kisang zo loding hi.
Note'n Topa' tungah lungdam koh biakna na piak uh ciangin, note hong kisan' theih nadingin na piading uh hi.
Note'n keima min siangtho na daisak keiding uh a, Israel mite lakah kei hong kisiangthosakding hi. Kei pen note a hong siangthosak Topa,
note' Pasian ahi dingin Egypt gam panin note a hong paikhiatpihpa ka hi hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
“A kha masa, a ni sawm le li nitak pen Topa' Paisan Pawi ahi hi.
Note hong kisan' theih nadingin amah in Topa' maiah anlom veiding a, Sabbath ni a zing ciangin siampipa in tua anlom veiding hi.
Note'n anlom na vei ni-un, Topa' tungah meihal biakna in a sitbaang lo kum khat a pha tuuno apa khat na piading uh hi.
Note'n na Pasian uh biakna na paipih ma, hih ni matengin anlum hitaleh a ki-em an hitaleh a sial hitaleh na ne keiding uh hi; tua pen note' khang tawntungin na tenna khempeuh uhah ngeina khat hi tawntungding hi.
Note'n na tenna uh panin vei dingin an lawh nih a kibawl anlum nih nong paipihding uh hi. Tuate pen annel a kibawl, silngo sawhin a ki-em, Topa' tungah anpalin a kipia hiding hi.
Note'n anlum tawh, a sitbaang lo kum khat a pha tuuno sagih, le bawngtalno khat, le tuutal nih na piading uh hi. Tuate, Topa' tungah a gim namtui mei tawh kihal biak nadingin an tawh biakna le leenggahzu tawh biaknate tawh Topa' tungah meihal biakna hiding hi.
Note'n khialhna hanga biakna in keel apa khat le thunuama biakpiakna in kum khat a pha tuuno apa nih na piading uh hi.
Note'n tua ni mahin thu zaksakna na bawlding uh a, a siangtho kikhop khat na neiding uh hi. Note'n thatang nasep na sem keiding uh hi; tua pen note' tenna khempeuhah na khang tawntungun ngeina khat hi tawntungding hi.
Note'n thatang nasep na sem keiding uh a, Topa' tungah meihal biakna na paipihding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Note'n tua ni in nana sem keiding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh tua pen Topa note' Pasian' maiah note a dingin kilemna bawl nadingin kilemna bawl ni ahi hi.
Note'n nana sem keiding uh hi. Tua pen na khang tawntungun na tenna khempeuh uhah ngeina khat hi tawntungding hi.
Note'n Topa' tungah na piak uh Topa' Sabbathte, note' letsongte, thuciamna hangin na biaknate khempeuh uh le utthu-a na biaknate khempeuh uh banah piakding ahi hi.
Note'n a ni masa ni in singkung hoih gahte, nisuh hiangte, a teh tam singhiangpite, le lui a gialhektela in, Topa na Pasian uh pahtawina, ni sagih sung pawi na bawlding uh hi.
Note'n tua pen kum simin ni sagih sung pawi in na neiding uh a, note' khang tawntungin ngeina khat hi tawntungding hi. Note'n kha sagihna sungah na bawlding uh hi.
No Israel mi khempeuh ni sagih sung buk sungah na tengding uh hi.
Tu-a bangin Moses in Israel mite tungah Topa' pawi a kisehte a gen hi.
Amah'n kham citak meivakkhuam tungah meivakte a ngeina bangin Topa' maiah omsak tawntungding hi.
Topa' deihna amaute tungah a kigen mateng amaute in tua mipa khumcip uh hi.
“Mi a thatpa kithatding hi.
Ganhing a thatpa in lohding a, mi a thatpa kithatding hi.
Note'n peemta le tualsung mi a dingin ngeina a kibang khat na neiding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh kei pen Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Topa'n Sinai Mual tungah Moses kiangah,
Note'n a kum sawmngana siangthosakin, gam sunga a teng mi khempeuh tungah suahtakna thu na zasakding uh hi. Note'n nomau' neihsa ciat ngahkikin, sila in a kizuak mite nomau' innkuanpihte ciat kiangah na ciahkik uh ciangin note a dingin jubilee hiding hi.
“Hih jubilee kum sungin note khempeuh in nomau' neihsa ciat na ngahkikding uh hi.
Note'n na vengte' tungah na zuak uh ahi zongin na vengte' kiang panin na lei uh ahi zongin note khatlekhat na kikhem keiding uh hi.
Note khatlekhat kikhem loin na Pasian uh na zahtakding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
“Note'n, ‘Lo lah pawi loin, an lahla kei lehang, a kum sagihnaah bang neding ihi hiam?' na cih uhleh
“Note'n na neih uh leitang khempeuh na kitanhkiksak theiding uh hi.
Note'n ama tungah a meetin sum leitawi pia loin, ama tungah a meetin na an uh zong na pia keiding uh hi.
Note'n hih gawpgawpna tawh amah na uk keiding uh a, na Pasian uh na zahtakding uh hi.
Note'n na neih theihding uh sila numei le sila pasalte hih bang ahi hi: Na kimkot uha om minam dangte lak panin sila numei le sila pasal na lei theiding uh hi.
Note'n na gam sung uhah a suak, note lakah a hong peem khualmite leh note tawh a om amau' innkuante lak panin zong na lei theiding uh a, amaute pen nomau a' hi theiding uh hi.
Note'n amaute pen note' khit ciangin na tapate uh tungah amau' neih tawntung dingin a luah dingin na pia theiding uh hi. Note'n sila in amaute na nei theiding uh a, ahih hangin na sanggam uh Israel mite khatlekhat hih gawpgawpna tawh na ki-uk keiding uh hi.
Note'n ka sabbathte tangin keimah hong kibiakna mun na zahtakding uh hi; kei pen Topa ka hi hi.
“Note'n ka thukham zui in, ka thupiaknate mangin tuate na sep uhleh,
Note'n na galte uh na delhding uh a, note' maiah namsau in amaute puksakding hi.
Note nga in zakhat zo in, note zakhat in tul sawm na zoding uh hi. Note' maiah namsau in na galte uh puksakding hi.
Note'n sauveipi a kikhol anluite ne in, a thak koih nadingin a lui na hahsiang masading uh hi.
Keimah in note lakah omna ka bawlding a, keimah in note kong kih keiding hi.
Note pen amau' sila na hihloh nadingun Egypt gam panin note a hong paikhiatpih Topa na Pasian uh ka hi hi. Keimah in note' gimna hakkolte kuaitanin note a dingtangin kong paisak hi.
“Hih banga hihna tawh note hong kihei tuan loin, kei na hong demlai uhleh,
“Tua bang hinapi in note in keima thu ngai loin, kei na hong demlai uhleh,
note ka hong heh ngawh bawlding a, note' khialhna hangin a zah sagih vei in kong thuhilhding hi.
Note na gil uh kial luading ahih manin na tapate uh le na tanute uh' sa na neding uh hi.
Note' sung panin galte' leitangah a omlaite amau' mawhna hangin kiamding uh a, amau' pute pate a mawhna uh hangin a kiam bangun amau zong a kiamding uh hi.

Giahphual panin a dinkhiat peuhmah uh ciangin sunin amaute' tungah Topa' meii a om hi.
Manna pen nannan tang tawh kibang a, a mel pen bedolak singnai tawh kibang hi.
Zanin giahphual tungah daitui a kiat ciangin manna tawh kia khawm hi.
Moses in Topa' kiangah, “Bang hangin na nasempa hong hici bawlsiat na hi hiam? Bang hangin na maipha hong musak loin, hih mi khempeuhte' tavuan kei' tungah hong suan na hi hiam?
Keimah in hih mite khempeuh paii ka hi hiam? Nangmah in kei' kiangah, ‘Nau cingnu in nawine naungek a puak bangin, nangmah in amau' pate piak dingin ka ciam leitangah amaute ang puakin paipih in,' nong cih theih nadingin kei' sunga piang ahi uh hiam?
Hih mite khempeuh piakding koiah sa ngahding ka hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh ka maiah amaute kapin, ‘Ka nekding uh sa hong pia in,' hong ci uh hi.
Mite tungah, ‘Zing cianga dingin note ki-ap pha un, sa na neding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa' zakin na kap uh a, “Sa nekding kua in hong piading ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh Egypt gamah nuam i sa hi,” na ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin note' tungah Topa'n sa hong piading a, note in sa na neding uh hi.
Note'n ni khat sung, ahih kei leh ni nih sung, ahih kei leh ni nga sung, ahih kei leh ni sawm sung, ahih kei leh ni sawmnih sung bek ne loin,
na ikkhiat dong uh le na kih dong matengun kha khat sung tawntung sa na neding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh note' lakah a om Topa nialin a maiah na kap uh a, “Bang hangin Egypt panin paikhia ihi hiam?” na ci uh hi,' ci in,” a ci hi.
Amaute' khamzah dingin tuuhonte le bawnghonte amau a dingin kigozoding ahi hiam? Tua ahih kei leh tuipi ngasate khempeuh amau' khamzahding kimanzoding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Topa'n Moses kiangah, “ Topa' hih theihding zah kiciangtan sa na hi hiam? Ka thugen a manin hong tun leh hong tun loh tu in na muding hi,” a ci hi.

Tua ciangin Moses le Israel upate giahphualah a ciahkik uh hi.

Tua ciangin Balak in Balaam kiangah, “Kei bang hong cih na hi hiam? Ka galte a samsia dingin nang kong sam a, ahi zongin amaute bangmah cih loin, amaute thupha na pia zawsop hi,” a ci hi.
Amah'n, “ Topa'n ka gen dingin hong sawl thu, don loding ka hi hiam?” ci in a dawng hi.
Balak kiangah a paikik ciangin a meihal biakna geiah amah nading a, Moab uliante tawh na om uh hi. Balak in ama kiangah, “ Topa'n bang hong gen ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
A zuau dingin Pasian pen mihing hi lo a, a kisik dingin mihing' tapa hi lo hi. Amah'n gen khin hi; a gen bangin hih loding ahi hiam? Amah'n ci khin hi; a cih bangin tungsak loding ahi hiam?
Ahih hangin Balaam in Balak kiangah, ” Topa' cih khempeuh keimah in ka hihding hi,' hong ci hi lo ka hi hiam?” ci in a dawng hi.
Jakob mite aw, na puanbukte uh bangzahin hoih ahi hiam? Israel mite aw, na giahphual uh bangzahin hoih ahi hiam?
Amaute bok a, humpinelkaipa bangin lumsuk uh hi. Humpinelkaipi bangin lumsuk uh hi. Kua'n amaute phong ngamding ahi hiam? Note thupha hong piate in thupha ngah henla, note hong samsiate in samsiatna ngahta hen,” a ci hi.
Balaam in Balak kiangah, “Kei kiangah nong sawl na kamtaite kiangah,
‘Balak in kham le ngun tawh a kidim ama inn hong piading hitaleh zong, Topa' thu banah keima thu in a pha bawlding ahi a, a sia bawlding ahi zongin bangmah ka hih thei kei hi. Topa' gente bek keimah in ka gending hi,' ci in gen khin hi lo ka hi hiam?
Israel gualzoding a, Edom mite kisuankhiading a, a galte ahi Seir zong, kisuankhiading hi.

Note lakah, zan sungin ama tungah thupiang hangin a siang lo mi a om leh giahphual pualamah amah paikhiading a, giahphual sungah hong pai loding hi.
“Giahphual puaah awnghawh nading mun khat na neiding uh hi.
Ahih hangin thuciamna bawlding pan na kikep uhleh note' sungah khialhna om loding hi.
amah pai in midang khat' zi va suak a,
Amah mizawng ahihleh ama hong khap puan na zantaamsak keiding uh a,
“Bawng in an a cil laitakin a muk na tuam keiding uh hi.
Israel mite lakah ama innkuan pen, ‘A khedap a kikaih khiatsak mipa' innkuan,' kiciding hi.
tua nu' khut na sattansakding uh a, amah na hehpih keiding uh hi.
“Egypt panin nong paikhiat lai-un lampiah Amalek mite in note hong bawlna,
note gimin lungkhamin na om laitakun lampiah a hong simna, le note' nungah a nunung khempeuh hong thahna uh phawk un; amaute in Pasian kihta lo uh hi.
Moses in tua ni mahin mite thuhilhin,
Levi mite in awging lianpi tawh Israel mite khempeuh tungah hih bangin ciding uh hi.
“Na seengte uh le na annel mekna kuangte uhah thupha omding hi.
“Na sepna khempeuh uhah thupha na ngahding uh hi.
Note piak dingin na pu na pate uh tungah Topa'n a ciamsa gam sungah note' sung pana piangte, na gan khawi pan uha piangte, le na leitang pan uha piangteah Topa'n note nakpitakin hong hausakding hi.
Note' leitangah ama hunin guah a zusakding le na sepna khempeuh uh thupha a pia dingin Topa'n a na hoih kholna vantung note hong honding hi. Note'n minam tampite tungah leitawi na piading uh a, ahih hangin note in leitawi nala keiding uh hi.
Note'n tuni-a kong thugente limtakin zuihna tawh Topa na Pasian uh thupiaknate mangin, tuni-a no kong thupiakna kammalte panin, pasian dangte' na semin a bia dingin na pial kei nak-uhleh, Topa'n a makai in note hong bawlding a, mi' nung zui in hong bawl loding hi. Tunglam bekah na kahding uh a, na nuaikiat ngei keiding uh hi.
“Khuapi sungah hong kisamsiading a, loah zong hong kisamsiading hi.
“Na lawhte uh le na annel mekna kuangte un zong samsiatna ngahding hi.
“Na sep na bawlna khempeuh uhah hamsia na ngahding uh hi.
Note' luanghawmte pen huih lak a leeng vasate khempeuh le leitung a ganhingte khempeuh' an hiding a, tuate a bengkhiading mihing om loding hi.
Topa'n haina, mittawtna, le lungsim buaina tawh note hong vatgawpding hi.
Tua ahih ciangin na mit un a muhding nate in note hong hehsak mahmahding hi.
Topa'n note hong paikhiatpihna mite lakah a cikzethuai, paunak, le gentehna na suakding uh hi.
Note'n leenggah lo zuanin na puahding uh a, ahih hangin leenggahzu dawn loin, leenggah zong na ne keiding uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh lung in tuate neding hi.
“Note lakah a om peemtate lian semsemding uh a, note na neu semsemding uh hi.
Note le na suanlekhakte uh tungah a tawntungin tuate pen lim le nalamdang hiding hi.
note na sih matengun amaute in na ganhon note uh le na leitang panun a piang gahte hong neksakding uh hi. Amaute'n note hong beisak matengun note a dingin an, leenggahzu, ahih kei leh sathau, na ganhingte uh ahih kei leh na tuuhon note uh zong hong nusiat loding uh hi.
Note lakah a ngeksuak, a cithei pen mipa in a sanggampa, a it a zi, le amah tawh a om a tate a nunung pen' tungah an pia nuam loding hi.
Note lakah a om a ngeksuak, a cithei pen numei, amah ngekin a ci neel lua ahih manin a khenuai tawh lei sikding a ngaihsun ngei vet lo nu in a it a pasal, a tanute le a tapate a dingin ama sung panin a piang a tate le ama sung panin a paikhia a nau-nungzuite phal loding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh hong umcihna le na galte un na khuapite uhah note hong lungkhamsak nading lungkhamna sungah bangmah neih lohna hangin amah in tuate nesimding hi.
Note na siat matengun hih thukham laibu sungah a kiciamteh lo natna le gimna khempeuh zong Topa'n no tungah hong tungsakding hi.
Note, vantung aksite zahin a tam na hihna sung uhah tawmno bek na phading uh hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa na Pasian uh thu na mang kei uh hi.
Note na zin kik ngei nawn keiding uh hi, ci in kong ciam khualzinna, Egypt gamah teembaw tawh Topa'n note hong paipih kikding hi. Tua laiah sila numei le sila pasal dingin na galte uh tungah na kizuakding uh a, ahih hangin kuamah in note hong lei loding hi,” a ci hi.
note' mit in a muhsa ze-etna lianpite, limte, tua nalamdang liante khempeuh na thei khin uh hi.
Hih kiciamna note bek tawh a bawl hi lo a,
Note lakah numei ahi a, pasal ahi a, innkuan ahi a, minam khat ahi zongin, tua minamte' pasian a bia dingin Topa i Pasian kiang panin tuni in a lungsim a heikhia a omkhakding kidawm un. Tua hikeileh note lakah gu a neigah kha agah singkung hong bangding a, hih kiciamna kammalte za napi in a lungsimah amah thupha kipia tawmin, ‘Ka lungsim khauhna tawh ka gamta zongin ka suakta veveding hi,' a ci hong om khading hi. Hih in mihoih le misia, a kibangin phiatkhiatna hong suaksakding hi.
Minam khempeuhte in, ‘Bang hangin Topa'n hih bangin hih gam bawl ahi hiam? Hih hehna lian, bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?' ci takpiding uh hi.
Note'n na neih theih nadingun, na pu na pate uh neih leitangah, Topa na Pasian un hong paipihding a, na pu na pate uh sangin a citheizaw a tamzaw in note hong bawlding hi.
Note'n na lungsim khempeuh uh le na nuntakna khempeuh uh tawh Topa na Pasian uh itin na hintheih nadingun, Topa na Pasian un note le na suanlekhakte uh tungah thu man' nopna lungsim hong guanding hi.
Note'n Topa' thu mangkikin, tuni-a kong gen ama thupiaknate khempeuh na zuiding uh hi.
Note'n hih thukham laibu sunga kigelh ama thupiaknate le ama thukhamte zui in, Topa na Pasian uh thu na man' uh a, na lungsim khempeuh uh le na nuntakna khempeuh uh tawh Topa na Pasian uh lamah na kihei uhleh, Topa na Pasian un na sepna khempeuh uh, note' suanlekhakte, na ganhingte uh panin a piangte, le na leitang panun a piang khempeuhah nakpitakin hong daupaisakding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh na pu na pate uh tungah amah a lungkim mah bangin note tungah Topa hong lungkim kikding a, note hong daupaisakding hi.
Note'n, ‘Eite in a thu za in i sep theih nadingin kua in vantungah eite a dingin hong paisakin hong laksakding ahi hiam?' na cih theih nadingun vantung a om hi lo hi.
Tua ciangin Moses in Israelte khempeuh tungah a thugen zomlai hi.
Tua hun ciangin amaute tungah ka sin so in, amaute nusia in ka mai ka seelding a, amaute beimangding uh hi. Tua ni ciangin amaute in, ‘Eite' lakah i Pasian a om loh manin hih siatnate i tungah hong tung hi lo ahi hiam?' a cih theih nadingun amaute tungah siatna le gimna tampi tungding hi.
Moses in a bei dongin hih Thukham kammalte laibu sungah a gelh a man ciangin,
Moses in Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang a pua Levi mite thu pia a,
Bang hang hiam cih leh a lehdo mite le a lungkhauh thei mite na hihna uh ka thei hi. En un, note tawh kei a nungta khawm laipi mahin, tuni in Topa na lehdo khin uh hi. Ka sih khit ciangin bangzah takin lehdozaw laiding na hi uh hiam!
“Vantungte aw, ngai un, thu kong gending hi. Ka thugente leitung in za hen.
A hai, ngaihsutna nei lo mite aw, tua bangin Topa thukding na hi uh hiam? Amah pen, note a hong piangsak, note hong bawlin a hong kipsak, napa uh hi lo ahi hiam?
Topa bek mah in amaute makaih a, amaute kiangah gamdang pasian om lo hi.
Note a hong Honkhiapa na phawk kei uh a, note a hong suaksak Pasian na mangngilh uh hi.
“‘Amaute' tungah siatna ka kholding a, amaute' tungah ka thaltangte ka zangding hi.
Amaute a pil hileh, hih thu theitelding uh a, amau' thu tawpna muding uh!
Amau a Honkhiapa in amaute zuakin, Topa'n amaute piakhia kei leh bangci in mi khat in mi tulkhat delh mangin, mi nih in mi tul sawm taisakzoding ahi hiam?
Amau' leenggahzu pen gulpi gu le a gupha gul gunei gu tawh kibang hi.
“Hihte kei kiangah kikholin, ka vankoihna sungah kisiincip hi lo ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Amau' pasiante, a bukna uh suangpi,
amaute' biakpiakna thau ne in, leenggahzu tawh a biakna uh a dawnte koiah om ahi hiam? Amaute thosakin note kihuhsak unla, amaute, na kidalna uh hisak un!
Moses in Israelte khempeuh tungah hih thute a gen a man ciangin
Tua ni mahmahin Topa'n Moses kiangah,
Hi taktak hi; amah in a mite it a, ama tungah a ki-ap mi khempeuh a khut sungah om hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in na kalsuanna hong zui uh a, nang tung panin lamlahna ngah uh hi.
Jakob mihonte' neih dingin Moses in kote tungah ngeina khat hong pia hi.
ni hangagah a hoihpente, le kha hanga piang a hoihpente tawh,
tanglai mualte tunga piang a hoih a limci pente le tawntung mualte' hauhna tawh,
Tua ahih ciangin Israel mite lungmuangin omding uh hi. Jakob suante bek an le leenggahzu gamah om hi. Hi taktak hi, a vantungte in daitui hong khiatsuk hi. Israel aw, mi nuamsa na hi hi. Nang hong kihuhna lum le na gualzawhna lum le na gualzawhna namsau ahi Topa'n nang banga a hotkhiat mi kua om ahi hiam?
Naftali gam khempeuh, Efraim le Manasseh gam, Judah gam khempeuh Nitumna Tuipi dong,
Tua ahih ciangin Topa' thugenna bangin Topa' nasem Moses pen Moab gamah si a,
Topa' nasem Moses a sih khit ciangin Topa'n Moses' nasem, Nun tapa Joshua kiangah,
Thu hong pia khin hi lo ka hi hiam? Thahat inla hang in. Lau kei inla lungkia kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh na paina peuhpeuhah Topa na Pasian nang tawh hong om hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Joshua in mi makaite thu pia in,
Tua ciangin Joshua in Reuben mite, Gad mite, le Manasseh minam a langte tungah,
note hong piak bangin Topa'n na sanggamte uh tungah tawlngakna pia in, Topa na Pasian un amaute a piak leitang amaute in zong a luah mateng uh na huhding uh hi. Tua ciangin note' neih leitangah ciahkikin, Topa' nasem Moses in Jordan gal ni a suahna lamah note hong piak leitang na luahding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Amaute a lup ma in innkhum zanga amaute kiangah Rahab paito in
Ni thum a cin ciangin giahphualah uliante pai in
En un, leitung buppi' Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang note' mai Jordan lamah paiding hi.
A minam bupin Jordan a galkah khit uh ciangin Topa'n Joshua kiangah,
“Nam khat pan mi khat, mite lak panin mi sawm le nih teel inla,
Hong tungding hunah na tate un, ‘Hih suangtumte bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?' ci in hong dot ciangin note' lakah lim khat hiding hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Joshua kiangah,
Tua ciangin amah in Israel mite kiangah, “Hong tungding hunah na tate un, ‘Hih suangte bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?' ci in hong dot uh ciangin,
Jerikho khua kiangah Joshua a tun ciangin a khuadaktoh leh, a khut sungah namsau dawhsa tawh mi khat a maiah nading hi. Ama kiangah Joshua pai in, “Ko' pawl na hi hiam, ahih kei leh ka langte' pawl na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n, “Hilo hi; Topa' galkapte a ukpa in tu in kong pai hi,” a ci hi. Joshua zong bok sukin bia in ama kiangah, “Ka topa in a nasempa bang hong sawl nuam ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin zingsangin Joshua tho baih a, siampite in Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang ala uh hi.
Tua bangin Topa'n Joshua ompih a, gam khempeuhah ama min a thang hi.
Tua ciangin Joshua in, “Ala, Topa Pasian , kote a hong susiading Amor mite' khut sungah a hong pia dingin bang hangin hih mite Jordan galkhatah hong paipih peuhmah na hi hiam? Jordan galkhatah tending a lungkim hi hohta le-ung!
Topa aw, Israelte a galte uh maiah a nungkik uh ciangin bang gen theiding ka hi hiam!
Bang hang hiam cih leh Kanaan mite le hih gam a teng mi khempeuh in hih thu zading uh a, kote hong umcihin leitung panin kote hong phiatkhia mangding uh hi. Tua ciangin a lian mahmah nangma min bang cihding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Topa'n Joshua kiangah, “Tho in, bang hangin tua bangin leiah bok na hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Joshua in, “Bang hangin kote tungah gimna hong tun na hi hiam? Tuni in Topa'n nang tungah gimna hong pia hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Israelte khempeuh in suang tawh Akhan a denglum uh hi. Amaute'n a innkuanpih dangte le a neihsate uh zong suang tawh denglumin a hal uh hi.
Ahih hangin amaute in Ai kumpipa hingmatin Joshua kiangah a paipih uh hi.
Joshua le Israel mite a do dingin lungsim kikhatin kikhawm uh hi.
Ahih hangin Israel mite in tua Hiv mite kiangah, “Kote' maiah a teng mite na hi khatheiding uh hi. Tua hileh note tawh thuciamna hong bangci bawltheihding ka hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Amaute'n Joshua kiangah, “Kote, nangma nasem ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin Joshua in amaute kiangah, “Kuate na hi uh hiam? Koi lai panin hong pai na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Joshua in amaute samin amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin kote' nai hih laiah a teng hinapi in, ‘Note' kiang panin gamla mahmah ung,' cihna tawh kote hong khem na hi uh hiam?
Tua ciangin Joshua, amah tawh a om Israelte khempeuh tawh Gilgal-a giahphualah a ciahkik hi.
Hih kumpi ngate tai in Makkedah leihawm sungah bu uh hi.
Tua ciangin Joshua, Israelte khempeuh tawh Debir lamah kihei kikin tua khua a sim hi.
Hih kumpite khempeuh le Joshua sauveipi sung a kido hi.

Note'n leitang khen sagihin hong ciamteh unla, na ciaptehna uh hih mun kei kiangah nong paipihding uh hi. Tua ciangin keimah in Topa i Pasian' maiah note ading ai ka sanding hi.

Kedemoth a lonona gamte tawh, le Mefaath a lonona gamte tawh, khuapi li kipia hi.
“ Topa' mihon buppi in, ‘ Topa lehdonaah tuni in note a dingin biakna tau khat lamna tawh Topa zuihna panin tuni in kihei in Israel Pasian' tungah na gamtatnasa uh ahi hih khemna pen bang ahi hiam?
Topa' mihonte tungah gimna khat a hong tungsak ahi, eite i kisiansuah nai beek lohna ahi, Peor-a i khialhna hawmthawhin, tuni in Topa zuihna panin kiheikhiading na hi uh hiam? Note'n tuni in Topa lehdo le-uhcin zing ciangin Israel mihon buppi tungah amah hehding hi.
Zerah' tapa Akhan, a ki-ap nateah a khialh manin Israel mihon khempeuh tungah hehna hong tung hi lo ahi hiam? Ama mawhna hangin amah bek si lo hi,' ci uh hi,” ci in a gen uh hi.
Tua ciangin Reuben mite, Gad mite, le Manasseh minam alangte in Israel beh lutangte dawngin,
Tua bang hi het lo hi. Hong tungding hunteah na tate un ko' tate tungah, ‘Israel Pasian, Topa tawh no bang kisai na hi uh hiam?
Note' hangin Topa na Pasian un hih minam dangte khempeuh tungah a bawlnate na mu khin uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh note a dingin hong dosakpa pen Topa na Pasian uh ahi hi.
Note tungah hong ciamsa bangin note a dingin hong dosakpa pen Topa na Pasian uh ahih manin note khat in mi tulkhat na taikeeksak zo uh hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Topa na Pasian uh na itding uh hoihtakin ngaihsun un.
Note'n na sep loh uh leitang, na sat loh uh khuapite, note tungah kong pia a, tuate sungah na teng uh hi. Na suan loh uh leenggui lo pan agah leh oliv huan pan agah na ne uh hi,' ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Joshua in a milipin amau' gamh ciatah, mite a ciahsak hi.
Joshua a sih khit ciangin Israel mite in Topa tungah thu dong uh a, “Kanaan mite a sim dingin kua kuanto masading ka hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua nu tawh a kiten ciangin apa kiang panin lo khat a nget nading a zi hahsawl hi. A zi zong ala tung panin kum a, Kaleb in ama kiangah, “Bang ut na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Josef minamte zong Bethel a sim dingin kuanto uh a, Topa'n amaute a huh hi.
Amor mite' gamgi pen Akrabbim kahtohna, Sela leilu lam pan kipan hi.
hih gam a teng mite tawh thuciamna na bawl keiding uh hi. Amau' biakna taute na susiading uh hi,' ka hong ci hi. Ahih hangin note in ka thupiakna na mang kei uh hi. Bang hangin lehgamtat na hi uh hiam?
Tua ciangin Israel mite, Topa' muhnaah a sia gamta in Baalte' na sem uh hi.
Amaute'n Topa nusia uh a, Baalte le Ashtaroth pasiante bia uh hi.
Ehud in a siahsun' a man khit ciangin siah a puak mite ciahsak hi.
Amau' zia kikalin Ehud tai in suang milimte kheng a, Seirahah a tai hi.
Ehud a sih khit ciangin Topa' muhnaah Israel mite a sia gamta kik uh hi.
Tua hun lai in Lappidoth' zi kamsang numei Deborah in Israelte thu khen hi.
Amah'n mi sawlin Naftali gam Kedesh panin Abinoam' tapa Barak samsakin ama kiangah, “ Topa, Israelte' Pasian in nang thu hong pia in, ‘Pai in, Tabor Mualah na mite khawm inla, Naftali minam le Zebulun minam panin mi tul sawm bangla in hong ci hi lo ahi hiam?
Abinoam' tapa Barak, Tabor Mualah paito khin, ci in Sisera kiangah a kigen ciangin,
Tua ciangin Deborah in Barak kiangah, “Pai in! Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa'n na khut sungah Sisera hong piak ni ahi hi. Na maiah Topa pai hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin mihing tul sawm bang in zui in Tabor Mual panin Barak a paisuk hi.
Amah'n tua nu kiangah, “Puanbuk kongahding inla, mi khatpeuh hong pai in na kiangah, ‘Hih laiah mi khatpeuh a om hiam?' hong cih leh, ‘Om kei,' na ci in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Deborah le Abinoam' tapa Barak in tua ni inla sa uh a,
Topa' maiah mualte kiling hi, Israel Pasian, Topa' mai Sinai galkhatah.
A thak pasiante a kiteel ciangin, kulhkongpi sungah gal om pah hi. Lum ahi a, tei ahi zongin, Israel tul sawmlite lakah kimu ahi hiam?
Bang hangin tuukhawkte lakah tuuhonte a dingin tamngai kitum a ngai dingin zekai na hi hiam? Reuben behte lakah nakpi taka lungsim ngaihsutna a om hi.
Jordan galkhatah Gilead om hi. Dan minamte bang hangin teembaw tawh om ahi hiam? Asher minamte, tuipi geiah tu lai a, leilak a tunna geiah a teng uh hi.
Vantung panin aksite in do uh a, amau paina ciat panin Sisera do uh hi.
Tua ciangin sakol khe, a kop taina, a sakol hangte' koptaina a ging hi.
“Tawlet panin Sisera' nu khuadak a, a kikalh simsiam kawm panin Sisera' nu khuadak hi: ‘Bang hangin a leeng hong ciahding hih tanvei sawt ahi hiam? A leeng khegingte bang hangin hici zekai ahi hiam?' a ci hi.
‘Amaute'n vankinusiate mu in hawm hi lo ahi hiam? Mi khat ciangin nungak khat ahih kei leh nih pai; a kinusia puan kinimte Sisera ading, a kinusia puan kinim a kizemte, a kinim a kizem puan nihte ka ngawng ading maw?' a ci hi.
Midiante' hangin Israel mite Topa' tungah a kiko uh ciangin,
Gideon in ama kiangah, “Kong thum hi, sia aw, Topa'n kote hong ompih ahihleh, bang hangin hih thu khempeuh ko tungah hong tung ahi hiam? Ka pate un kote tungah hong genin, ‘ Topa'n Egypt panin eite hong paipih hi lo ahi hiam?' a cih uh a lamdang ama sepnate khempeuh koiah omta ahi hiam? Ahih hangin tu in Topa'n kote hong paaikhia in Midiante' khut sungah hong pia khin hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin ama lamah Topa kihei in, “Hih nangma thahatna tawh pai inla, Midiante' khutsung panin Israelte honkhia in. Nangmah hong sawl khin hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Gideon in ama kiangah, “Kong thum hi, Topa aw, Israelte bangci hotkhiat zawhding ka hi hiam? En in, Manasseh minam sungah keima behte a hat lo pen hi a, ka innkuan sung panin kei a neupen ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Amaute khatlekhat kiangah, “Hih na kua in hih ahi hiam?” kici uh hi. Amaute'n a thu kanin a dot uh ciangin, “Joash' tapa Gideon in hih hi,” kici uh hi.
Ahih hangin Joash in ama langkhatah a pang mite khempeuh tungah, “Baal panpihding a, ama tupna hutpihding na hi uh hiam? Amah a panpih peuhmah zingsang ciangin kithatding hi. Amah pasian ahihleh amahmah kihu tawm tahen. Bang hang hiam cih leh ama biakna tau a kiphelsak ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Efraim mite in Gideon kiangah, “Midiante a do dingin na kuancil lai in kote nong sap loh, kote hong bangci ngaihsut na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n nakpitakin amah mawhsak uh hi.
Amah'n amaute kiangah, “Note tawh teh dingin kote bang hi lel ka hi uh hiam? No Efraim minamte' sep a themno khat pen ko minam bup khempeuhte' sep sangin thupizaw hi lo ahi hiam?
Pasian in note' khut sungah Midian uliante Oreb le Zeeb hong piazo hi. Note tawh teh dingin kote in bang hihzo ka hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Amah hih bangin kam a pau ciangin ama tunga amau' hehna a bei hi.
Tua ciangin Sukkoth uliante in, “Na galkapte tungah anlum ka piak dingun Zebah le Zalmunna na khut sungah omkhin ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Joash' tapa Gideon a galsimna panin Heres kahtohna lam tawnin ciahkik hi.
Tua ciangin Sukkoth mite kiangah amah tungin, “Kei tungah hong kisialin, ‘A gim na mite tungah anlum ka piak dingun Zebah le Zalmunna na khut sungah omkhin ahi hiam?' na cih uh Zebah le Zalmunna en un,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in Penuel tausang supai in tua khua mite a that hi.
Tua ciangin amah in Zebah le Zalmunna kiangah, “Taborah na thah uh mite koiah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute'n, “Amaute, nangmah bang uh hi; amaute in kumpipa' tapate suun uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
Joash' tapa Gideon pai in ama aituam innah a teng hi.
Tu in Jerubbaal' tapa Abimelek, Shekhem aa nu' tanaute kiangah pai in amaute khempeuh kiangah,
“Shekhem khuami khempeuh huau in gen un, ‘Jerubbaal' tapa sawmsagihte a vekpi in note hong ukding le khat in note hong ukding, note a dingin koi hoihzaw ahi hiam?' a ci hi. Kei pen note' guh note' sa ka hihna zong phawk un,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin oliv kung in amaute kiangah, ‘Keimah in pasiante le mite a kipahtawina ahi ka thaunate nusia in singkungte a uk dingin hong paiding ka hi hiam?' ci hi.
Ahih hangin theikung in amaute kiangah, ‘Keimah in ka khumna le kagah hoihte nusia in singkungte a uk dingin hong paiding ka hi hiam?' ci hi.
Ahih hangin leenggui in amaute kiangah, ‘Keimah in pasiante le mite a lungnuamsak ka leenggahzu nusia in singkungte a uk dingin hong paiding ka hi hiam?' ci hi.
“Tua ahih ciangin tu in Abimelek kumpi in na bawl uh ciangin lungsimtak le thumantak mah tawh a gamta na hi uh hiam? Jerubbaal le a innkuan tungah thuman takin gamta in ama sepna tawh a kituakin amah a bawl mah na hi uh hiam?
Note'n tuni in Jerubbaal le a innkuanpihte tungah lungsimtak le thumantak tawh a gamta takpi mah na hih uhleh, Abimelek tungah note lungdam unla, note tungah zong amah lungdam tahen.
Abimelek in Israelte tungah kum thum sung uk hi.
Tua ciangin Ebed' tapa Gaal in, “Abimelek, kua hi a, ama na i sepsak dingin ei Shekhem mite kua ihi hiam? Jerubbaal' tapa le ama ulian Zebul in Shekhem mite' pulepa Hamor' na sem uh hi lo ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin ama na semding ihi hiam?
Tua ahih ciangin tu in na ompih mite tawh zanin pai unla, gamlakah pangsim un.
Tua ciangin Zebul in ama kiangah, “Tu in na kamhanna koiah om ahi hiam? ‘Ama na i sep dingin Abimelek kua ahi hiam?' a cipa hi lo na hi hiam? Hih mite, na simmawhte hi lo ahi hiam? Tu in paikhia inla amaute tawh kido in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Shekhem mite' maiah Gaal kuankhia in Abimelek tawh kido hi.
A zing ciangin gamlakah Shekhem mite paikhia uh hi. Hih thu Abimelek kiangah kigen hi.
Shekhem Tausang mite khempeuh kikaikhawm uh hi, ci in Abimelek kiangah kigen hi.
Tua ciangin Thebezah Abimelek pai a, Thebez langpangin giahphual sat a, tua khua ala hi.
Tua ciangin Jair si in Kamonah kivui hi.
Topa'n Israel mite kiangah, “Egyptte le Amor mite, Ammon mite le Filistia mite kiang panin hong honkhia hi lo ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Israel mihonte le makaite khatlekhat in, “Ammon mite do dinga a kipan ngam kua om ihi hiam? A kipan ngam mipa, Gilead gam a teng mite khempeuh tungah lutang hiding hi,” a kici uh hi.
Tawlkhat khit ciangin Ammon mite in Israelte sim uh hi.
Ahih hangin Jefthah in Gilead upate kiangah, “Note'n kei hong mudahin ka pa' inn pan hong hawlkhia hi lo na hi uh hiam? Bang hangin thuhaksa na tuah uh ciangin kei kiangah hong pai na hi uh hiam?” na ci hi.
Tua ciangin Jefthah in Ammon mite' kumpipa kiangah kamtaite sawlin, “Ka gam a sim dingin kei kiangah nong pai nadingin kei' tungah bang thu om ahi hiam?” cisak hi.
Jefthah in Ammon mite' kumpipa kiangah kamtaite sawlkikin
Tua ahih ciangin Topa, Israelte' Pasian in ama mi Israelte' mai panin Amor mite paaikhia hi. Tu in nangmah in luahkikding sawm na hi hiam?
Tu in nang pen Moab kumpipa, Zippor' tapa Balak sangin ginazaw na hi hiam? Amah'n Israelte to ngei a, amaute do ngei ahi hiam?
Heshbon le a khuaneute, Aroer le a khuaneute, le Arnon gun panga om khuapite khempeuh sungah Israelte a ten kum zathum hun sung tengin bang hangin lakik lo na hi hiam?
Jefthah in Topa tungah thuciamna bawlin, “Ka khut sungah Ammon mite nong piak leh
Efraim mite galhiam tawi dingin kisam uh a, amaute Zafon gun kantanin galkah uh a, Jefthah kiangah, “Bang hangin Ammon mite a sim dingin galkahin, nang tawh a kuankhawm dingin kote hong zawn lo na hi hiam? Na inn tawh nang kong halnelhding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
Note'n kei nong hotkhiat lohding uh ka theih ciangin kei mahmah hanciam tawmin Ammon mite a sim dingin ka galkah a, Topa'n kei' khut sungah amaute hong pia hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin tuni in kei a hong sim dingin hong kuan na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Gilead mite in Efraim mite tung panin Jordan ngahmuntela uh hi. Efraim galtaite khat peuhpeuh in, “Hong galkah sak in,” a cih ciangin Gilead mite in ama kiangah, “Efraim mi na hi hiam?” ci uh hi. Amah'n, “Hi kei ing,” a cih ciangin
Ama nungah Bethlehem khuami Ibzan in Israelte thu khen hi.
Tua ciangin Ibzan si a, Bethlehemah kivui hi.

Tua ciangin Zebulun mi Elon si a, Zebulun gam Aijalonah kivui hi.
Ama nungah Pirathon mi Hillel' tapa Abdon in Israelte thu khen hi.
Tua ciangin Manoah dingin a zi zui a, mipa kiangah pai in, “Hihnu kiangah thugenpa nang na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Manoah in, “Na thugente a manin hong tun ciangin naupang' nuntakna ziading bang hi a, amah in bang hihding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa' vantungmi in Manoah' kiangah, “Numei' kiangah ka gente khempeuh na kidawm hen.
Manoah in Topa' vantungmi kiangah, “Na thugente a manin hong tun ciangin nang kong pahtawi theih nadingun, na min bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Topa' vantungmi in ama kiangah, “Hih thu a lamdang hi, ci in thei napi in bang hangin ka min hong dong na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa' kha in Zorah le Eshtaol kikal Mahanehdanah Samson hanthotding a kipan hi.
Khatvei Timnahah Samson va paisuk a, Timnahah Filistia nungak khat mu hi.
Ahih hangin a nu le apa in ama kiangah, “Nang pai in dawibia Filistia mite kiang panin zi na lak nadingin na tanaute' lak ahi a, i mipih khempeuh lakah ahi zongin numei khat beek om lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
A ni li ni in amaute in Samson' zi kiangah, “A thuhaksa bang hiam cih hong gen nadingin na pasal zol in. Tua hi kei le nang le na pa, na inn uh tawh kong halding uh hi. Kote a hong zawngsak dingin hih laiah hong sam na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Samson' zi ama maiah kapin, “Kei nong mudah hi, kei nong it kei hi. Ka gam mite tungah thuhaksa na gen a, bang hiam cih kei' tungah nong gen kei hi,” a ci hi. Amah'n numei kiangah, “En in, ka nu kiang hitaleh kapa kiang hitalehah ka gen kei hi. Nang kiangah hong gen tuanding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua khuapi mite in a ni sagih ni, ni a tum ma in ama kiangah gen uh a, “Khuaizu sangin bang khumzaw a, humpinelkai sangin bang hatzaw ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Ka bawngla tawh lo kho khawm lo hi le-uhcin, ka thuhaksa na thei keiding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih manin Samson' zi pen a moliah pa' zi dingin na kipia hi.
A sungpa in, “Amah mudah taktak hi ni teh, ci in ngaihsun ka hih manin na lawmpa' zi dingin ka pia hi. A naunu amah sangin hoihzaw hi lo ahi hiam? A u tangin amah na tenpih nadingin kong thum hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Filistia mite in, “Kua'n hih ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n, “Timnah mite' makpa Samson in hih hi; bang hang hiam cih leh a sungpa in a zi laksakin a lawmpa tungah piaksak hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin Filistia mite hong paito in tua nu le apa mei tawh a hallum uh hi.
Judah mite in, “Bang hangin kote simin hong paito na hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n, “Samson a hending le ko tungah amah in hong hih bangin ama tungah a hih dingin kong paito uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Judah mite mihing tulthum Etam suanghawmah paisukin Samson kiangah, “Filistia mite, eite a hong ukte ahihlam thei lo na hi hiam? Kote' tungah nang' hong bawl bang ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Samson in amaute kiangah, “Amaute'n kei tungah hong bawl bangin amaute tungah ka bawl hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah dangtak mahmah ahih manin Topa samin, “Na nasempa' tha tawh hih bang suahtakna lian nong piazo hi. Tu in dangtakin kei si in dawibia mite' khut sungah pukding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n Filistia mite' uk hun sung Israelte kum sawmnih sung thu a khen hi.
Tua khit ciangin Samson in Sorek kuamah Delilah a kici numei khat ngai hi.
Tua ciangin numei in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin na lungsim kei tawh a om lopi, ‘Nang kong it hi,' ci thei na hi hiam? Hih thumvei dong kei nong simmawh a, na thahatna a omna mun nong gen kei hi,” a ci hi.
Nisimin nakpitakin a kutkut ciangin, sihna dong dingin Samson lunggim hi.
Efraim mualtung gammi Mikah a kici min nei mi khat om hi.
Tua hun laitakin Judah gam Bethlehem khua sungah Levi mi tangval khat om hi.
Mikah in ama kiangah, “Koi panin hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Judah gam sung Bethlehem khua-a om Levi mi ka hi a, mun ka muhna peuhah a peemding ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Mikah in Levi mipa koihin, tangvalpa ama siampi suakin Mikah' innah a om hi.
Amaute Mikah' innah a om uh ciangin Levi mi tangval' aw khat khenthei uh hi. Amaute kihei in ama kiangah, “Kua'n hih laiah nang hong paipih ahi hiam? Hih lai munah bang hih na hi hiam? Hih laiah na nasep bang ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Amaute Zorah le Eshtaol-a a sanggamte uh kiangah hong tunkik uh ciangin, a sanggamte un amaute kiangah, “Bang thu gending nong nei uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Amaute'n, “Ding un, amaute a sim dingin paito ni. Bang hang hiam cih leh a leitang ka mu khin uh a, a lei hoih mahmah hi. Bangmah hih loin ommawkding na hi uh hiam? Paiding zekai kei un; lutin leitang va luah ni.
Amaute tua lai mun panin Efraim mualtung gamah paisuakin Mikah' innah a tung uh hi.
Tua ciangin Laish gam a ensim dingin a pai mi ngate in a sanggamte uh kiangah, “Hih innte khat sungah siampipuan khat, innsung pasiante, a kiseek milim khat, le a kisung milim khat a omlam thei lo na hi uh hiam? Tua ahih ciangin tu in na hihding uh ngaihsun un,” a ci uh hi.
Tua hun sungtengin galhiam a tawi Dan mi za gukte kulhkongpi lutna ahding uh hi.
Hih mite Mikah' inn sungah tumin a kiseek milim, a siampipuan, a innsung pasiante, le a kisung milim a lak uh ciangin siampipa in amaute kiangah, “Bang hih na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Amaute'n ama kiangah, “Pau kei in; na khutin na kam hum inla, kote tawh hong pai in kote a dinginpa le siampi hong hi in. Nang a dingin mi khat' inn sungah siampi hihding hoihzaw ahi hiam, tua ahih kei leh Israelte' sungah minam le beh siampi hihding hoihzaw ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Amaute'n Dan mite a otsan uh ciangin Dan mite hong kihei in Mikah kiangah, “Hih bang mihon tawh nong delh nading bang thu om ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Amah'n, “Note'n keima bawlsa ka pasiante le ka siampipala in na paikhia uh hi. Keimah in bang nei nawn ka hi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin, ‘Bang thu ahi hiam?' bang hangin hong ci thei na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah khuadak a, khualzin pa, khuapi kongzingah a mu hi. Tua ciangin puteekpa in, “Koiah paiding na hi hiam? Koi panin hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel minamte in Benjamin minam khempeuh kiangah mi sawl uh a, “Note' lakah a piang thu pen bangzah tatsiatna ahi hiam?
Israel mite dingin Bethelah paito uh a, “Benjamin mite a sim dingin kua pai masading ka hi uh hiam?” ci in Pasian a dong uh hi. Topa'n, “Judah minamte paito masading hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel mite paito in nitak dong Topa' maiah a kap uh hi. Amaute'n Topa' kiangah thu dongin, “Ka sanggam uh Benjamin mite a sim dingin gal phualah ka naihkikding uh hiam?” a ci uh hi. Topa'n, “Amaute a sim dingin kuanto un,” a ci hi.
Aaron' tapa Eleazar' tapa Finehas in tua laiah tua hunin na sem hi), “Ka sanggam uh Benjamin mite a sim dingin kuankik laiding ka hi uh hiam, tua ahih kei leh khawlding ka hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi. Topa'n, “Paito un; bang hang hiam cih leh zing ciangin amaute na khutsung uhah kong piading hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Israelte in Gibeah kiimah a pangsim dingin mi koih uh hi.
Benjamin mite sung pan galhang mihing tul sawm le tulgiat tuk uh hi.
Amaute'n, “Israelte' Pasian, Topa aw, tuni in Israelte sungah minam khat a pelem nading, hih thu bang hangin Israelte tungah hong tung ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Israel mite in, “ Topa ading kikhopnaah Israel minamte khempeuh sung panin kua teng hong pai lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in Topa kiangah a pai lo mite tawh kisai in Mizpahah kiciamna lianpi khat bawl uh a, “Kithatding hi,” a ci uh hi.
Eite in i tanute amaute tungah zi dingin pia loding hi hang, ci in Topa tawh kiciam khin ihih ciangin a nungta lai amaute' ziding bang cihding ihi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin amaute in, “ Topa kiang Mizpahah Israel minamte hong pai lo a om hiam?” a ci uh hi. En in, Jabeshgilead panin tua giahphual kikhopnaah kuamah pai lo hi.
Israel minamte sungah Topa'n kitapkhapna omsak ahih manin mite in Benjaminte khasiat uh hi.

Tua ahih ciangin Bethlehem a tun mateng uh a nihun paisuak uh hi. Bethlehem a tun uh ciangin amaute' hangin a khuazang un luum lialua in nupite in, “Hihnu Naomi mah ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.

Tua ciangin Boaz in anlate a uk a nasempa kiangah, “Hih ka muh ngei loh numei kuata ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah a mai in leiah puk a, leilakah kunin ama kiangah, “Kei gamdang mi khat hinapi, hih banga kei nong phawkna dingin bang hangin na maiah maipha ngah thei ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a teeknu in ama kiangah, “Tuni in koiah tawm na hi hiam? Koiah sem na hi hiam? Nang hong phawk mipa in thupha ngahta hen,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a teeknu kiangah a naseppihte gen a, “Tuni-a ka sepna mipa pen Boaz ahi hi,” a ci hi.

Tu in Perez' suanlekhakte hih bang ahi hi: Perez pen Hezron' pa,
Hezron pen Ram' pa, Ram pen Amminadab' pa,

Ahih hangin amaute in a pa' thu ngai lo uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua pen amaute a thah nadingin Topa' deihna ahi hi.
Tu in naupang Samuel a pumpi khangin Topa le mite' maipha a ngahtoto hi.

Eli in, “Amah'n nang kiangah hong gen bang ahi hiam? Kei kiangah hong im kei in. Amah'n nang tungah hong gente khempeuh kei kiangah ip nong neih leh, Pasian in nang hong dawm keita hen,” a ci hi.
Samuel khang a, Topa'n amah ompihin, Samuel' thugente khat zong leiah kiasak lo hi.
Mihonte giahphualah hong ciah ciangin Israel upate in, “Bang hangin Topa'n tuni in Filistia mite' maiah eite hong taisak ahi hiam? Eite' lakah amah hong pai in a thahat i galte' khutsung panin amah in eite hong hotkhiat theih nadingin Shiloh panin Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang paipih ni,” a ci uh hi.
Filistia mite in otna gamlumna a zak uh ciangin amaute in, “Hebru mite' giahphualah nakpi a hih bang otna bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang giahphual a tun khitna a theih uh ciangin
Gimna ngah hita hang! Kua'n hih a thahat pasiante' khutsung panin eite hong honkhiazoding ahi hiam? Hihte pen gimna a tuamtuamte tawh gamlakah Egyptte a vatgawp pasiante ahi hi.
Eli in kikona awging a zak ciangin amah in, “Hih gamlumna bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin mipa manlangin hong pai in Eli kiangah a gen hi.
Mipa in Eli kiangah, “Keimah, galphual panin hong ciah ka hi a, tuni in giahphual panin kong tai hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Ka tapa aw, bangci ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin amaute in mi sawlin Filistia uliante khempeuh khawm uh a, “Israelte' Pasian' Thuciamna Singkuang bang cihding ihi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n dawngin, “Israelte' Pasian' Thuciamna Singkuang Gathah koihsak ni,” a ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Israelte' Pasian' Thuciamna Singkuang tua laiah paipih uh hi.
Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang Filistia gam sungah kha sagih sung om hi.
Tua ciangin Filistiate in siampite le aisante sam uh a, “ Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang bang cihding ihi hiam? Ama omna munah bang tawh khading ihi hiam, hong gen un,” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin amaute in, “Amah i piakding mawhna hanga biakna bang ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n dawngin, “Filistia uliante a phazah tawh kizui in kham uilut nga le kham simbeng nga hiding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh note khempeuh le na uliante uh tungah a kibang gimna hong tung hi.
Egyptte le Faro in a lungsim uh a khauhsak bangin bang hangin na lungsim uh khauhsakding na hi uh hiam? Amah'n amaute a mawlpih khit ciangin amaute in Israel mite paisakin, tua ciangin Israel mite kihemkhia uh hi lo ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin Bethshemesh mite in, “Hih a siangtho Pasian, Topa' maiah kua omzoding ahi hiam? Eite' kiang panin kua kiangah amah paisakding ihi hiam?” a ci uh hi.

Tua ciangin Saul in a nasempa kiangah, “Ahih hangin pai lehang, tua mipa bang puakding ihi hiam? I van sunga i anlum beita a, Pasian' mipa kiangah i puakding letsong om lo hi. Bang nei nawn ihi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amaute khuapi omna mual tungah a paitoh laitakun khuapi panin tui tawi dingin hong paikhia nungaknote tawh kituak uh ahih manin amaute kiangah, “Thumupa hih laiah a om hiam?” a ci uh hi.

Tuma ni thum lai in a mang na late ahihleh, kimu khinta ahih manin tuate na lungsimah ngaihsun nawn kei in. Israelte' deihdeihte kua' tungah om ahi hiam? Nang le na pa' innkuante khempeuh tungah a om hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Saul in dawngin, “Kei pen Israel minamte sung panin a tawmpen Benjaminte hi lo ka hi hiam? Keima innkuan, Benjamin minam innkuan khempeuh sung panin a niampen hi lo ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin hih bangin kei tungah hong pau na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Samuel in sathau thawl khatla a, ama lu tungah buakin amah nam a, “ Topa'n ama mi Israelte tungah ulian dingin nang sathau hong nilh khin hi lo ahi hiam? Nangmah in Topa' mite ukin a kiima om amau' galte' khutsung panin amaute na honkhiading hi. Topa'n ama luahte tungah ulian dingin nang sathau hong nilh khitna lim hih bang hiding hi:
Tuni in kei kiang panin na paikhiat ciangin Benjaminte' gam Rachel' han kiang Zelzahah mihing nih na tuakding a, amaute in nang kiangah, ‘Pai a na zon late kimu khin a, tu in napa in late ngaihsun nawn loin nangmah hong lunghimawh a, “Ka tapa bang cihding ka hi hiam?” ci hi,' hong ciding uh hi.
Tua ciangin kamsangte tawh a gamtat khawmna, amah a theisa mi khempeuhte in a muh uh ciangin khatlekhat in, “Kish' tapa' tungah bang tung ahi hiam? Saul zong kamsang suak ahi hiam?” kici uh hi.
Tua ciangin tua lai-a mite khat in dongin, “Hih kamsang dangte kua' tate ahi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin, “Saul nangawn kamsang suak hi,” cihna paunak a kipatna hong suak hi.
Saul' pano in amah le a nasempa a muh ciangin, “Koiah pai na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Late a zong dingin ka pai uh hi. Late kimu zo loding ci in ka theih uh ciangin Samuel kiangah ka pai uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tu in Samuel in Mizpah-a Topa' kiangah mite khawm hi.
Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Topa kiangah dongkik uh a, “Tua mipa hih laiah hong pai hiam?” ci uh a, Topa'n, “En un, amahmah van kawm lakah bu hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Samuel in mi khempeuh tungah, “ Topa'n a teelsa mipa na mu uh hiam? Mi khempeuh lakah amah tawh a kibang khat zong om lo hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin mi khempeuh awngin, “Kumpipa khansau hen!” a ci uh hi.
Ahih hangin bangmah a man lo mi pawlkhat in, “Hih mipa in eite hong bangci hotkhiat zawhding ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amaute'n amah simmawhin ama kiangah letsong puak lo uh hi. Ahih hangin amah in tua mite bangmah cih lo hi.
Tu in Saul a bawngtalte' nung zui in lo panin hong ciah hi. Saul in, “Amaute a kah nadingin bang in mite nasak ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Jabesh mite' thute ama kiangah a gen uh hi.

Tuhun pen mangbuh lak laitak hi lo ahi hiam? Amah'n vanging le guah hong puaktheih nadingin Topa' tungah thu ka ngending hi. Note a dingin kumpi khat na ngetna uh hangin Topa' muhnaah na gamtatnasa na gitlohna uh a liatna thu thei in na muding uh hi,” a ci hi.

Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin Topa' thu mang lo na hi hiam? Bang hangin vankinusiate bawhin Topa' muhnaah a sia gamta na hi hiam?” a ci hi.

Tua ciangin Ramahah Samuel pai a, Gibeah-a a innah Saul zong a ciahto hi.
