Topa' thupiak bangin Samuel gamta in Bethlehemah a pai hi. Tua khuapi upate a lingsa in amah a dawn dingin hong pai uh a, “Thuhoih a hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Samuel in Jessi kiangah, “Na tapate khempeuh hih laiah a omkim mah ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Jessi in, “A nautum pen omlai a, ahih hangin amah tuu cingin om hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Samuel in Jessi kiangah, “Hih laiah amah hong tun mateng eite in bangmah dang i hih thei keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Amah'n a khete tungah sumngo ngaltuam bulh a, a liangkoah sumngo teipi khawh kikhai hi.
Amah dingin Israel uliante otsanin, “Galdo dingin bang hangin hong kuankhia ngam na hi uh hiam? Kei, Filistia mi hi in, note, Saul' nasemte hi lo na hi uh hiam? Note a dingin mi khat teel unla, tua mipa kei kiangah hong paisuksak un.
David, a nautum pen hi a, a upa pen thumte in Saul zui a,
Ni sawmli sung zing le nitakin Filistia-pa hong pai in hongding zelzel hi.
Israelte le Filistiate, galkap le galkap a kido dingin kinaih uh hi.
Israel mite khatlekhat kiho in, “Hih hong paikhia mipa na mu ngei uh hiam? Israelte a to dingin hong paito takpi hi. Amah a that mipa tungah kumpipa in sum tampi pia in, ama tanu zong piading a, a pa' innkuante, Israel sungah aana nasep le siah khempeuh kipengsakding hi,” a ci uh hi.
David in ama kiangading mite kiangah, “Hih Filistia-pa thatin Israelte' tung panin hih mindaina a beisakpa a dingin bang kihihding ahi hiam? A nungta Pasian' galkapte a to dingin hih dawibia Filistia-pa kua ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
David in mite kiangah thu a gen laitakin ama u a upen Eliab in a za hi. David tungah Eliab heh mahmah ahih manin, “Bang hangin hong paisuk na hi hiam? Tua tuu tawmkhatte gamlakah kua tawh nusia na hi hiam? Na kihaimuanna le na lungsim gitlohna ka thei hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh galkidona a en dingin nong paisuk hi,” a ci hi.
David in, “Bang hih ka hi hiam? Kam bek hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Filistia-pa in David kiangah, “Ui hong sa a, ciangkang tawh sat hong sawm na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Filistia-pa in a pasiante' min tawh David samsia hi.
Filistia-pa do in David a kuankhiatna Saul in a muh ciangin galkap mangpa Abner kiangah, “Abner aw, hih tangvalpa kua' tapa ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Abner in, “Kumpipa aw, ka thei kei hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in, “Tangvalpa kua' tapa ahi hiam, kan in,” a ci hi.
Saul in ama kiangah, “Tangvalpa aw, kua' tapa na hi hiam?” a ci hi. David in dawngin, “Bethlehem khuami na nasempa Jessi' tapa ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Saul heh mahmah a, hih thugenna in amah lungkim lo sak hi. Amah'n, “Amaute'n David tungah a tul sawmin pia in, kei tungah a tulin hong pia bek uh hi. Kumpi min puak cih simloh bang dang nei nawn ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ni a kipan Saul in David encik hi.
David in Saul kiangah, “Kei pen kumpipa' makpa ka hih nadingin kei, bang hi a, Israelte tungah ka tanaute, ka pa' innkuante bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Saul' nasemte in David kiangah hih thute gen uh hi. David in, “Kei pen mizawng hi in a zahtakhuai lo ka hihna mu napi in kumpipa' makpa suahding a thuneu sa na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
David a kihta semsem hi. Tua ahih ciangin Saul pen David' gal hi tawntung hi.
Amah'n a nuntakna pia ngamin Filistia-pa that a, Topa'n Israelte khempeuh a dingin gualzawhna lianpi piangsak hi. Nangmah in hih thu na mu a, na lung a dam hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin thu om lopi in David thahna tawh a mawhbaang lo mipa tungah khialding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Mikhal in tawletah David khiasuk hi. Amah taikhia in suakta hi.
Saul in Mikhal kiangah, “Bang hangin tua bangin kei hong khem a, amah a suahtak nadingin ka galpa khah na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Mikhal in Saul dawngin, “Amah'n kei kiangah, ‘Hong paisak in; bang hangin nang hong thatding ka hi hiam?' hong ci hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Saul kiangah, “En in, Ramah khuasung Naioth vengah David om hi,” kici hi.
Tua ciangin amahmah Ramahah pai a, Seku-a om tuikhuk lianpi tung hi. Amah'n, “Samuel le David koiah om ahi hiam?” ci in a dong hi. Mi khat in, “En in, Ramah khuasung Naioth vengah om uh hi,” a ci hi.
Amah'n zong a puante suahkhia in Samuel' maiah laamin awng a, tua sun tawntung le tua zan tawntung a guaktangin a om hi. Tua hun a kipanin, “Saul zong kamsang suak khin ahi hiam?” kici hi.
Tua ciangin Ramah khuasung Naioth veng panin David tai in, Jonathan kiangah hong tungin ama maiah, “Bang hih ka hi hiam? Ka mawhna bang ahi hiam? Amah'n kei thah dingin hong zon nadingin na pa' maiah ka khialhna bang om ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in David kiangah, “Tua bang hi het loding! Na si keiding hi. En in, kapa in kei kiangah gen loin a lian hitaleh a neu hitaleh bangmah hihlo hi; bang hangin kapa in kei tungah hih thu hong imding ahi hiam? Tua bang hi lo hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin thuman itna tawh na nasempa hong bawl in; bang hang hiam cih leh nang tawh a siangtho thuciamnaah na nasempa na tunpih hi. Ahih hangin kei sungah mawhna a om leh, nangmahmah in kei hong that in; bang hangin napa kiangah kei hong paipihding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Jonathan in, “Nang tungah tua bang hi het kei hen! Kapa in nang tungah siatna tungding a ngaihsutna thei leng nang kiangah hong gen loding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in Jonathan kiangah, “Napa in nang hong ngawh dawn leh kua in kei kiangah hong gending ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Jonathan in David kiangah, “Israelte' Pasian, Topa, teci hita hen! Zing ciang tubang hun ahi a, a ni thum ni in ahi zongin, ka pa' ngaihsutna tawng ka kankhiat khit ciangin, nangma tungah a lungsim a hoih leh, nang kiangah mi hong sawlin hong pulak loding ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin muitum bangin tua lampangah thaltang thum ka lawnding hi.
Ahih hangin a ni nih ni, Khadet ni khit a zing ciangin David' mun awng lai hi. Tua ciangin Saul in a tapa Jonathan kiangah, “Bang hangin Jessi' tapa zanni hitaleh tuni hitaleh an neknaah hong pai lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Jonathan in Saul dawngin, “Bethlehemah a pai dingin limtakin kei tungah David hong kingen hi.
Tua ciangin Jonathan tungah Saul heh mahmahin ama kiangah, “A kiheikhial, a lehdo numei' tapa aw, nangma maizum nading le na nu' mindai nadingin Jessi' tapa na pawlpihna thu a thei lo hong sa na hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Jonathan in apa Saul dawngin, “Bang hangin amah kithatding ahi hiam? Amah'n bang hih ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Jonathan' thaltang lot a tukna munah naupang a tun ciangin Jonathan in a naupang samin, “Nang' khen' hua lamah thaltang om hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Nob khua-a siampipa Ahimelek kiangah David pai hi. Ahimelek a lingsa in David a dawn dingin hong pai in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin nang guak hong hi a, kuamah hong tonpih lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin tu in nang bang nei na hi hiam? Anlum lum nga ahih kei leh hih lai-a a om peuhpeuh hong pia in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in siampipa dawngin, “A taktakin ci lehang, hih bangin ka paikhiat uh ciangin numeite kiang panin kote ka kikem tawntung uh hi. Khualzin mawkmawk ciang nangawnin zong tangvalte siangtho hi. Tuni in amaute bangzahin siangthozaw kanding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in Ahimelek kiangah, “Teipi ahi a, namsau ahi zongin hih laiah nei lo na hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh kumpipa' nasep pen nawhtatding kul ahih manin ka namsau ahi a, ka hiamte ahi zongin kala man kei hi,” a ci hi.
Akhish' nasemte in ama kiangah, “Hih David, a gam kumpipa hi lo ahi hiam? Amaute khatlekhat in ama thula in sa in laam uh a, ‘Saul in a tulin that, David in a tul sawmin that,' ci hi lo ahi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
David in hih thute a lungsimah ciamteh a, Gath kumpipa Akhish kihta mahmah hi.
Tua ciangin Akhish in a nasemte kiangah, “En un, hih mipa a hai ahihlam na mu uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin kei kiangah amah hong paipih na hi uh hiam?
Ka omnaah mihai-a gamta dingin hih mipa nong paipih nadingun mihai kisam thuah lai ka hi hiam? Hih mipa ka inn sungah hong paiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
note khempeuh in kei hong sawmsim na hi uh hiam? Tuni-a bangin hong pangsim dingin ka tapa in Jessi' tapa tawh thukimna a bawl ciangin kuamah in kei kiangah hong pulak loin, ka tapa in keimah a do dingin ka nasempa a hanthotnaah note kuamah dah loin, kei kiangah zong nong pulak kei uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Saul in ama kiangah, “Tuni-a bangin hong pangsimin kei a do dingin hong kipat theih nadingin bang hangin nang le Jessi' tapa in kei hong sawmsim a, ama tungah an le namsau pia in, ama a dingin Pasian kiangah thu dotsak na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Ahimelek in kumpipa dawngin, “Na nasemte khempeuh lak panin kumpipa' makpa ahi nangmah hong cingte a ukpa David bangin kua thumanin, na inn sungah kua kipahtawi ahi hiam?
Ama a dingin Pasian' kiangah thu ka dotsak a masa pen tuni ahi hiam? Hilo hi. Kumpipa in a nasempa ahi a, ka pa' innkuante khempeuh ahi zongin ngawh kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh na nasempa in a tam hitaleh a tawm hitaleh hih thu khempeuh bangmah thei lo hi,” a ci hi.
Saul in Topa' siampite a thah khitna thu Abiathar in David kiangah a gen hi.
Tua ahih ciangin David in Topa thu dongin, “Pai in Filistiate ka simding hiam?” a ci hi. Topa'n David kiangah, “Pai in Filistiate sim inla, Keilah khuamite honkhia in,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin David' mite in ama kiangah, “En in, Judah gam hih munah eite i lau hi. Filistia galkapte simin Keilahah pai lehang bangzahin lauzawding ihi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Keilah mite in ama tungah kei hong apding hiam? Na nasempa' zak bangin Saul hong paisukding hiam? Israelte' Pasian, Topa aw, kong thum hi, na nasempa tungah hong gen in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Topa'n, “Amah hong paisukding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in, “Keilah mite in kei le ka mite Saul' tungah hong apding uh hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Topa'n, “Amaute'n note hong apding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Saul' kiang Gibeahah Zif mite paito uh a, “Jeshimon leitaw lam, Hakhilah mualtung, Horesh a munmuanhuai sung kote' lakah David om hi lo ahi hiam?
Tua lai panin David paito in Engedi munmuanhuaiah a om hi.
Tua ciangin David in Saul kiangah, “Bang hangin, ‘En in, David in na siat nading zong hi,' a ci mite' thu um na hi hiam?
Israel kumpipa kua do-a hong kuankhia ahi hiam? Kua delh na hi hiam? Uisi maw! Uili maw!
David in hih thute Saul kiangah a gen a man khit ciangin Saul in, “Ka tapa David, tu-a ka zak nang' aw ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Saul a kap hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh mi khatpeuh in a galpa mu leh amah in a suakta in a galpa paikhiasakding ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin tuni in kei tungah nong bawlna hangin Topa'n a hoih tawh nang thaman hong pia tahen.
Nabal in a tuumul a metna thu David in gamlakah a za hi.
Tua ciangin Nabal in David' nasemte dawngin, “David kua ahi hiam? Jessi' tapa kua ahi hiam? Tulai in a tote kiang panin a taikhia nasem tampi om hi.
Ka anlum le ka tui le ka gan mul meette a dingin ka gawh ka satela in koilai panin hong pai cih ka theih loh mite tungah piading ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin David' tangvalte ciahkikin hih thu khempeuh ama kiangah a gen uh hi.
Tua khit ni sawm bang ciangin Topa'n Nabal vat a, amah a sita hi.
David in Jezreel khuami Ahinoam zongla a, amau tegel ama zi a suak uh hi.
Tua ciangin Saul kiang Gibeahah Zif mite hong pai uh a, “Jeshimon nisuahna lam Hakhilah mualtungah David bu hi lo ahi hiam?” va ci uh hi.
David in thukan simte sawl a, Saul hong pai taktak ahihna thu a thei hi.
Ahih hangin David in Abishai kiangah, “Ama tungah siatna bawl kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh Topa' sathau nilhpa a su peuhpeuh mawhna pan pengding sa na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
David in galkapte le Ner' tapa Abner samin, “Abner aw, hong dawng loding na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Abner in dawngin, “Kumpipa a sam kua na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
David in Abner kiangah, “Pasal hi lo na hi hiam? Israelte sungah nang tawh a kibang kua om ahi hiam? Tua ahihleh bang hangin na to kumpipa vil lo na hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh na to kumpipa a that dingin mi khat hong pai hi.
Saul in David' aw khenthei a, “Ka tapa David, tu-a a ging nangma' aw ahi hiam?” a ci hi. David in, “Ka topa, kumpipa aw, keima' aw ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “Bang hangin ka topa in a nasempa delh ahi hiam? Bang gamta khial ka hi hiam? Ka tungah bang mawhna om ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin David in Akhish kiangah, “Nong hehpih zawh leh, ka ten theih nadingin gam sung khuate khatah kei ading mun hong pia in; bang hangin na nasempa nang tawh kumpi khua sungah tengkhawmding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Akhish in, “Tuni in kua va sim na hi uh hiam?” ci in a dot ciangin David in, “Judah mite' Negeb gam,” ahih kei leh, “Jerahmeel mite' Negeb gam,” ahih kei leh, “Ken mite' Negeb gam,” a ci hi.
Saul in Filistia galkapte a muh ciangin lau a, a lungsim nakpi takin ling hi.
Numei in ama kiangah, “Saul' hihsa thu, gam sung panin vankahte le aisante a suksiatna na thei taktak hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin keima sih nading a piangsak dingin kei a dingin thangzak hong koih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin numei in, “Kua hong sapsakding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Samuel hong sapsak in,” a ci hi.
Numei in Samuel a muh ciangin a gingin kikokhia hi. Numei in Saul kiangah, “Bang hangin kei hong khem na hi hiam? Nang, Saul na hi hi,” a ci hi.
Kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Lau kei in; kua mu na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Numei in Saul kiangah, “Leisung panin pasian khat hong paikhiato ka mu hi,” a ci hi.
Amah'n tua nu kiangah, “Ama mel bangci ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua nu in, “Puteek khat hong paito a, amah in puantualpi silh hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Saul in tua pen Samuel hi, ci in thei a, leiah a maikunin zahtakna a bawl hi.
Tua ciangin Samuel in Saul kiangah, “Bang hangin keimah saptohna tawh hong nawngkaisak na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Saul in dawngin, “Nakpi takin ka lungkham hi; Filistiate in kei hong sim a, kei kiang panin Pasian kiheikhia in kamsangte tawh ahi a, mang tawh ahi zongin hong dawng nawn lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin ka gamtat nading zia a hong gen dingin nang kong sam hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Samuel in, “ Topa, nang kiang panin kiheikhia in na gal suak khin ahih ciangin bang hangin kei thu hong dong lai na hi hiam?
Filistia galkap a ukte in, “Hih Hebru mite in hih laiah bang hong hih uh ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Akhish in Filistia galkap a ukte kiangah, “Ni tampi, kum tampi kei tawh a omkhin, Israel kumpi Saul' nasempa David hi a, kei kiangah hong tai a kipanin tuni dongin ama tungah mawhna ka mu kei hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Filistia galkap a ukte ama tungah heh uh hi. Filistia galkap a ukte in ama kiangah, “Amah na koihna munah a ciahkik theih nadingin hih mipa sawlkik in. Gal kidona sungah eite' lang hong suak khading ahih manin galdona sungah eite tawh amah hong kuansuk loding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih mipa in a topa tawh kilemna bangci bawlding ahi hiam? Hih lai-a om mite' lutang tawh bawlding hi lo ahi hiam?
Amaute khatlekhat inla in sa in laam uh a, ‘Saul in a tulin that, David in a tul sawmin that,' a cihpa uh hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin David in Akhish kiangah, “Ahih hangin, keimah in bang hih ka hi hiam? Ka to kumpipa' galte do in ka pai theih loh nadingin nangma nasepnaah kong tum ni a kipan tuhun dong na nasempa' tungah bang mu na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in Topa thu dong a, “Hih mihonte ka delhding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Delh in; bang hang hiam cih leh na pha taktakding a, na mite na honkhiazo taktakding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in ama kiangah, “Nang kuate na hi hiam? Koi pan na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Kei pen Amalekte khat' nasem, Egypt mi tangval khat ka hi hi. Tuma ni thum lai in ka ci na ahih manin ka topa in hong nusia hi.
Tua ciangin David in ama kiangah, “Hih mite kiangah nong paipih suk nuamding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Nangmah in kei nong thahlohnading ahi a, ka topa' khut sungah nong apkik loh nading ahi zongin Pasian' min tawh kei tungah hong kiciam peuh lecin hih mihonte kiangah nang kong paipihsukding hi,” a ci hi.
David in Amalekte' laksa khempeuh ngahkik a, a zi nihte honkhia hi.
Hih thuah kua in no' thu hong ngaiding ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh gal sungah a kuan mipa' tanh zah mah, van a ngak mipa in tangding a, amaute in a kibangin ngahding uh hi,” a ci hi.

David in ama kiangah, “Koi panin hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in David kiangah, “Israel giahphual panin kong suakta hi,” a ci hi.
David in ama kiangah, “Bangci bang ahi hiam? Hong gen in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in dawngin, “Giahphual panin mite tai a, mi tampi zong pukin si uh hi. Saul le a tapa Jonathan zong a si hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin David in ama kiangah a gen tangvalpa kiangah, “Saul le a tapa Jonathan a sihna bangci theih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.

Amah'n Gilead, Ashur, Jezreel, Efraim, Benjamin, le Israel khempeuh tungah kumpi in amah bawl hi.

Tua ciangin Abner in a nung enin, “Asahel aw, nang na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Keimah ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Abner in Asahel kiangah, “Keimah zuihna panin pial in; bang hangin nang leiah hong vatgawpding ka hi hiam? Nang hong vatgawp leng na sanggampa Joab' maiah ka maitang bangci lakding ka hi hiam?” a ci kik hi.
Tua ciangin Abner in Joab samin, “Mi hih bangin kithat laiding ahi hiam? A tawpnaah a haksat zawk nading thei lo na hi hiam? A sanggamte uh a delhna panin na mite a kihei nadingin na thupiakding bangtan sawtlaiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tu in Saul in Aiah' tanu Rizpah min nei zineu khat nei hi. Ishbosheth in Abner' kiangah, “Bang hangin ka pa' zineu luppih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Ishbosheth' thugennate hangin Abner heh mahmah a, “Kei pen Judah mite a dingin ui bang lel ka hi hiam? Keimah in napa Saul' innkuante, a sanggam pasalte, le a lawmte tungah tuni dongin thumanna ka lak lai a, David' khut sungah note kong pia nai kei hi. Ahi zongin tuni in nang in numei khat lel tawh kisai in kei nong mawhsak hi.
Tua ciangin Abner in Hebron-a David kiangah kamtaite sawlin, “Hih gam kua in ukding ahi hiam? Kei tawh thuciamna hong bawl in. Israelte khempeuh nang kiangah a paipih dingin keimah kong pangding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa kiangah Joab pai in, “Bang hih na hi hiam? Na kiangah Abner hong pai hi. Nang in amah sawlkhia in amah a ciahkhiat khitna bang thu ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin Abner' hangin kumpipa in kahla in, “Mi haipa a sih bangin Abner siding ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin kumpipa in a nasemte kiangah, “Tuni in Israelte sungah ulian ahi milian khat a tukna thei lo na hi uh hiam?
Beeroth mite Gittaimah tai uh a, tuni dongin tua laiah peemta in om uh hi.)
Migilote in a thuman mi khat ama innsung a lupna tungah a thah ciangin note' tungah ama phu hongla in, leitung panin note hong susiazaw kanding hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahi zongin David in kumpipa' khua ahi Zion munmuanhuaila hi.
David lian semsem hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Vanglian Pasian, Topa'n amah ompih hi.
Jerusalemah a neih a tate' min: Shammua, Shobab, Nathan, Solomon,
Ibhar, Elishua, Nefeg, Jafia,
Elishama, Eliada, le Elifelet ahi hi.
Tu in Filistiate hong pai in Refaim kuamsung dim uh hi.
Tua ciangin David in Topa thu dongin, “Filistiate do in ka kuantoding hiam? Keima khut sungah amaute na hong piading hiam?” a ci hi. Topa'n David kiangah, “Kuanto in; bang hang hiam cih leh na khut sungah Filistiate kong pia taktakding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Filistiate hong kuantokik lai in Refaim kuamsung dim khin uh hi.
David in Israelte a kiteelkhia mi tul sawmthum khawmkik hi.
Tua ahih ciangin tua ni in David in Topa kihta hi. Amah'n, “ Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang bangci in ka kiangah hong tung theiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a innkuante thupha a pia dingin David a ciah hi. Ahih hangin David a dawn dingin Saul' tanu Mikhal hong paikhia a, “Tuni in Israel kumpipa, mi mawkmawkte khat maizum loin a guak om bangin, a nasemte' numeite' muhnaah tuni in a tangguakin omin, amahmah bangci kipahtawi ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin tua zan mahin Nathan kiangah Topa' thu hong tung a,
“Pai inla ka nasempa David kiangah gen in. ‘ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: Ten nading biakinn khat hong lamsakding na hi hiam?
Israel mite khempeuh tawh ka painasa mun khempeuhah, ka mi Israelte acing dingin ka piak thukhente khat peuhpeuh tungah, “Bang hangin taamtak biakinn hoih hong lamsak lo na hi hiam?” ci in kam khat beek gen ngei ka hi hiam?' ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpi David sungtumin Topa' maiah tu a, “Topa Pasian aw, tu ciang dong hih bangin kei nong kep nadingin kei kua hi a, ka innkuan bang ahi hiam?
David in nang tungah bang genthuah nawnding ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah in na nasempa na thei hi, O Topa Pasian !
“Ama mite' maiah minam khat le a pasiante hawlkhiatna tawh ama a dingin min bawlin, amaute a dingin a lian a lauhuai nate hih sakin, ama mi dingin a honkhia dingin Pasian a paina na mi Israelte, leitung minam dang kua tawh kibang ahi hiam?
Hadadezer' khuapite Betah le Berothai panin Kumpi David in sumngo tampi tak ala hi.
Hamath kumpipa Toi in David in Hadadezer' galkap buppi a zawhna thu a zak ciangin,
Zeruiah' tapa Joab in galkapte uk hi. Ahilud' tapa Jehoshafat thu ciamtehpa ahi hi.
Ahitub' tapa Zadok le Abiathar' tapa Ahimelek siampi ahi uh hi. Seraiah lai-atpa ahi hi.
Tua ciangin David in, “Jonathan' hangin ama tungah migitna ka lahtheih nadingin Saul' innkuan sungah mi khatpeuh a omlai hiam?” a ci hi.
Saul' innkuan sungah Ziba min nei nasempa khat om a, amaute in David kiangah amah sam uh hi. Kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Ziba na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Na nasempa kei pen Ziba ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in, “Pasian' tungah ka ciamsa bangin migitna ka lahtheih nading Saul' innkuanah mi khat beek omlai lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Ziba in kumpipa kiangah, “Jonathan' tapa khat omlai hi; amah a khe zaw hi,” a ci hi.
Kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Amah koiah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Ziba in kumpipa kiangah, “Lodebar-a Ammiel' tapa Makhir' innah amah om hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in zahtakna bawlin, “A sisa ui tawh a kibang kei bang lel, nong hici bawl nadingin na nasempa bang ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Ammon mite' uliante in a topa uh Hanun kiangah, “David in nangma kiangah hehnemte hong sawl manin napa a pahtawi hi, ci in ngaihsun na hi hiam? David in a nasemte khuapi sung a ending, le a lawnthal dingin hong sawl hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
David in mi sawlin tua numei' thu kansak hi. Mi khat in, “Hih nu pen Hit mi Uriah' zi, Eliam' tanu Bathsheba hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
“Uriah a innah ciahsuk lo hi,” ci in amaute in David kiangah a gen uh ciangin David in Uriah kiangah, “Khualzin a hong tung hi lo na hi hiam? Bang hangin na innah ciahsuk lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Uriah in David kiangah, “Thuciamna Singkuang, Israelte, le Judah mite gal sungah om uh a, ka topa Joab le ka topa' nasemte gamlakah giak uh hi. Tua ahih manin an ne tuidawnding le ka zi tawh a lum dingin ka innah ciahsukding ka hi hiam? Nangmah na hin mah bangin, hih bang ka gamta het keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Joab in mi sawlin galkidona thu khempeuh David kiangah a gen hi.
Amah'n kamtaipa thu hilhin, “Galkidona thu khempeuh kumpipa kiangah na gen khit ciangin,
kumpipa a heh suakin amah in nangma kiangah, ‘A sim dingin khuapiah tua zahin a nai in pai na hi uh hiam? Kulh tung panin hong kapding uh thei lo na hi uh hiam?
Jerubbesheth' tapa Ahimelek kua in that hiam? Numei khat in angawina suangpek tungnung kulh tung pan ama tungah khiatsukin Thebezah amah si hi lo ahi hiam? Bang hangin tua zahin kulh naiah pai na hi uh hiam?' hong cih leh nangmah in, ‘Hit mi na nasempa Uriah zong si hi,' na ciding hi,” a ci hi.
A haupa in tuuhon le bawnghon tampi nei hi.
Ama muhnaah a sia a gamta dingin bang hangin Topa' thu simmawh na hi hiam? Nangmah in Hit mi Uriah namsau tawh vatin, ama zi nangma zi dingin nala a, Ammon mite' namsau tawh amah na that khin hi.
A ni sagih ni in naungek si hi. Ama kiangah, naungek si hi, ci in a gending uh David' nasemte lau uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute in, “Naungek a hinlai nangawnin amah i hopih hangin i thu hong ngai lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin bangci in ama kiangah, naungek si, ci ngamding ihi hiam? Amahmah kisusia khading hi,” a ci uh hi.
Ahih hangin ama nasemte a kihuauna uh David in a muh ciangin naungek si hi, ci in a thei hi. Tua ciangin David in a nasemte kiangah, “Naungek si ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute'n, “Amah sita hi,” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin a nasemte in ama kiangah, “Hih banga na gamtatna a bangci hiam? Naungek a hin lai in an tangin na kap hi; ahih hangin naungek a sih ciangin tho in an na ne zawsop hi,” a ci uh hi.
Amah'n, “Naungek a hin lai in an tangin ka kap hi; bang hang hiam cih leh, ‘Naungek a hin nadingin Topa'n kei hong hehpihding hiam, hong hehpih loding hiam, cih kua in theikhol ahi hiam?' ka ci hi.
Ahih hangin tu in amah sita hi; bang hangin an tang nawnding ka hi hiam? Amah lakik theiding ka hi hiam? Ama kiangah kei ka paiding a, ahih hangin kei kiangah amah hong kik loding hi,” a ci hi.
Tu in Joab in Ammon khuapi Rabbah simin a khuapi tuikhukla hi.
Amah'n Ammon kiangah, “Kumpipa' tapa aw, bang hangin zingsang khat khit zingsang khat thakiam semsem na hi hiam? Kei kiangah a hang hong gen loding na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Ammon in ama kiangah, “Ka sanggampa Absalom' sanggamnu Tamar ka ngai hi,” a ci hi.
Keimah in ka maizumna koiah seelcipzoding ka hi hiam? Nang zong, Israelte sungah mihai luate khat bang na hiding hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu in kong thum hi, kumpipa kiangah gen in; bang hang hiam cih leh amah in nang a dingin kei hong khaktan loding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a sanggampa Absalom in ama kiangah, “Na sanggampa Ammon in nang hong bawlsia ahi hiam? Bangbang hitaleh kilungnuamsak in, ka sanggamnu aw; amah pen na sanggampa ahi hi; hih thu na lungsimah koih kei in,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin a sanggampa Absalom' innah Tamar lungzuang khawngai in a om hi.
Kumpi David in hih thute khempeuh a zak ciangin heh mahmah hi.
Tua ciangin Absalom in, “Tua bang hi loding ahihleh ka sanggampa Ammon kote tawh nong paisakding kong thum hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin nang tawh amah hong paiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Absalom in a nasemte thu pia a, “Ammon in zu a kham hun phawk unla, note kiangah, ‘Ammon sat un,' kong cih ciangin amah that un. Lau kei un; note thu hong pia khin hi lo ka hi hiam? Hang unla, thahat un,” a ci hi.
Absalom ahihleh Geshurah pai a, tua laiah kum thum sung a om hi.
Tu in kumpipa in Absalom a ngaihna thu Zeruiah' tapa Joab in a phawk hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Na lungkhamna bang om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Kalai, ka pasal sita a, meigong numei khat ka hi hi.
Tua ciangin a numei in, “Tua ahihleh bang hangin Pasian' mite' langah tua bang na hih sawm na hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh hih bang lungsim khentatna na piaknaah kumpipa in a hawlkhiatna a innah a paipih kik mateng kumpipa amahmah mawh a kipia ahi hi.
Kumpipa in, “Hih thu khempeuh Joab' vaihawmna tawh hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. A numei in dawngin, “Nang a nungta taktak na hih mah bangin ka to kumpipa aw, ka to kumpipa' gen bang teekteek mah ahi hi. Kei hong sawlpa pen na nasempa Joab hi a, na nasemnu' gen dingin hih thute a hong sawlpa amah ahi hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Joab dingin Geshurah pai a, Jerusalemah Absalom a ciahpih hi.
Tua hi a, kumpipa' omnaah pai loin Absalom kum nih bit Jerusalemah teng hi.
Tua ciangin Joab dingin Absalom' kiang ama innah pai in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin na nasemte in mei tawh ka lo hong halsak ahi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Absalom in Joab dawngin, “En in, nang kiangah thu kong puak a, ‘Kumpipa kiangah nang hong sawlin, “Bang hangin Geshur panin hong pai ka hi hiam? Tua laiah omlai leng kei a dingin hoihzawding hi,” ci in a va dong dingin hih laiah nong pai nading kong gen hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu in kumpipa omnaah kei hong paisak in; kei tungah mawhna a om leh amah hong thatsak in,' ka ci hi,” a ci hi.
Absalom tho baihin kulhkongpi lam geiah tu zel hi. Mi khatpeuh in thu khensak dingin kumpipa' maiah pai nading thu a neih ciangin Absalom in amah samin, “Koi khua pan na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Na nasempa, Israelte sungah tua minam tua khua ka hi hi,” a cih ciangin
Tua ciangin kumpipa in Gath mi Ittai kiangah, “Bang hangin nang zong kote hong zui na hi hiam? Ciahkik inla, kumpipa tawh om in; bang hang hiam cih leh nang pen gamdang mi na hi a, na inn panin gam dangah a om zong na hi hi.
Nang pen zan mah beka hong pai na hi hi. Koi lai munah kei paiding cih thei lopi in kote tawh a kawivak dingin nang hong bawlding ka hi hiam? Ciahkik in, na sanggamte ciahpih in. Topa'n itna kip le thumanna nang' tungah hong lakta hen,” a ci hi.
David in ama kiangah, “Nang hong zuisuak lecin kei a dingin vangik na hiding hi.
Siampi Zadok le Abiathar tua laiah nang tawh om hi lo ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin kumpipa' inn pan na zak peuhpeuh siampi Zadok le Abiathar' kiangah gen in.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in Ziba kiangah, “Bang hangin hihte hong paipih na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Ziba in dawngin, “Late pen kumpipa' innkuante a tuan nading, anlum le khuakhal singgahte pen tangvalte' nekding, le leenggahzu pen gamlakah a gimte' dawnding ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in, “Na topa Saul' tupa koiah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Ziba in kumpipa kiangah, “Amah Jerusalemah om hi; bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, ‘Tuni in Israel mite in ka pu Saul' kumpi gam kei hong piakikding hi,' ci hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a nu Zeruiah ahi Abishai in kumpipa kiangah, “Bang hangin hih uisi a banglel mi khat in ka to kumpipa samsiading ahi hiam? Hong kuansak inla a lu hong tankhiasak in,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin kumpipa in, “No Zeruiah tapate aw, note tawh bang kisai ahi hiam? Topa'n ama kiangah, ‘David samsia in,' a cihna hangin hong samsia ahihleh, ‘Bang hangin tuaci hih na hi hiam?' kua in ciding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Absalom in Hushai kiangah, “Hih bang pen na lawmpa tungah thumanna ahi hiam? Bang hangin na lawmpa tawh pai lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua banah, kua' na semding ka hi hiam? Ama' tapa hi loding ahi hiam? Na pa' na ka sep bangin nangma na ka semding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Absalom in Ahithofel kiangah, “Na ngaihsutna hong gen in; bang hihding ihi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua thugenna in Absalom le Israel upate khempeuh lungkimsak hi.
Absalom kiangah Hushai hong pai ciangin Absalom in ama kiangah, “Tua bangin Ahithofel in thu gen hi; ama genna bangin i hihding hiam? Tua ahih kei leh nang gen in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Hushai in Absalom kiangah, “Tutungin Ahithofel' thugen hoih lo hi,” a ci hi.
Absalom' nasemte tua nu' innah hong tun ciangin amaute in, “Ahimaaz le Jonathan koi laiah om ahi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi. A numei in amaute kiangah, “Amaute lui galkhatah pai khinzo uh hi,” a ci hi. Amaute'n zong a muh zawh loh uh ciangin Jerusalemah a ciahkik uh hi.
Tua ciangin Mahanaimah David tung hi. Absalom in Israel mite khempeuh tawh Jordan kantan hi.
Israelte le Absalom in Gilead gamah giahphual sat uh hi.
lupnate, kuangte, le leibeelte, mangbuh, mangbuhham, an, an kan, bepi le besan,
Joab in ama kiangah a gen mipa kiangah, “Bang! Nang amah mu maw! Bang hangin leilakah amah satkhiasuk lo na hi hiam? Nang tungah ngun peek sawm le kawnggak khat hong pia ngelding hi ve ing,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Zadok' tapa Ahimaaz in Joab kiangah, “Bangbang piang taleh kei zong Kush mipa' nungah hong taisak in,” a ci kik hi. Joab in, “Lungdamna thu puakna hangin thaman ngah loding cih thei napi in, ka tapa aw, bang hangin taiding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in, “Tangvalpa Absalom a hoihhoih hiam?” a ci hi. Ahimaaz in dawngin, “Joab in na nasempa hong sawl laitakin buaina lianpi khat ka mu a, ahih hangin bang hiam cih ka thei kei hi,” a ci hi.
Kumpipa in Kush mipa kiangah, “Tangvalpa Absalom a hoihhoih hiam?” a ci hi. Kush mipa in dawngin, “Ka to kumpipa' galte, le siat nadingin nangma langkhatah ading khempeuh, tua tangvalpa bangta hen,” a ci hi.
Joab kiangah, “En in, Absalom' hangin kumpipa kapin thum hi,” ci in kigen hi.
Ahih hangin eite' tungah sathau i nilh Absalom, gal sungah si khin hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu in bang hangin kumpipa lakkikding bangmah gen lo na hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Kumpi David in hih thu, siampi Zadok le Abiathar kiangah puakin, “Judah upate kiangah hih bangin gen un: ‘Israelte khempeuh' thu kumpipa kiangah tung khin hi. Bang hangin note in kumpipa a innah a ciahpih nunung pen hiding na hi uh hiam?
Note pen ka behnai na hi uh a, note pen keima si keima sa na hi uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin kumpipa a ciahpih nunung pen hiding na hi uh hiam?' ci un.
Tua ciangin Amasa kiangah, ‘Nang pen keima si keima sa hi lo na hi hiam? Tua kipan Joab' munah nang pen ka galkapte a ukpa na hih kei taak leh Pasian in kei hong dawm keita hen, ci hi,' ci in gen un,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a nu Zeruiah ahi Abishai hong paukhia a, “Amah'n Topa' sathau nilhpa samsia ahih manin hih thu hangin Shimei thahding hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin David in, “Note pen tuni in kei' lang bangin na om nadingun no Zeruiah' tapate tawh kei bang kisai ihi hiam? Tuni in Israel sungah mi khatpeuh kithatding ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh tuni in Israelte' tungah kumpi ka hihna thei hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Jerusalem panin kumpipa a dawn dingin hong pai ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Mefibosheth aw, bang hangin kei hong zui lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh ka to kumpipa' maiah ka pa' innkuante khempeuh a si zah dong dingin a sia ahi hi. Ahih hangin nangmah in na sabuaiah a ne mite lakah na nasempa na hong koih hi. Tua ahih ciangin kumpipa tungah ka kohding thudang bang neithuah nawnding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin nangma thu gen lailai na hi hiam? Ka lungsim ka khentatzo hi; nang le Ziba in leitang na hawmding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Barzillai in kumpipa kiangah, “Kei, kumpipa tawh Jerusalemah a paito dingin ka nuntakding kum bangzah hun nei nawn ka hi hiam?
Tuni in kei kum sawmgiat ka phata a, a nuam le a nuam lo khentel thei nawn ka hi hiam? Na nasempa in a nek ahi a, a dawn ahi zongin a limna phawk thei nawn ka hi hiam? Lasa numeite le lasa pasalte' aw za thei nawn ka hi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin ka to kumpipa tungah na nasempa vangik kibehlap hong hiding ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin Israel mite khempeuh hong pai in kumpipa kiangah, “Bang hangin ka sanggam uh Judah mite in nang hong gukhia in, kumpipa le a innkuante, le David' mite amah tawh, Jordan galah paipih ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Judah mite khempeuh in Israel mite dawngin, “Kumpipa pen kote tawh beh kinai ahihna hang ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin hih thuah heh na hi uh hiam? Kumpipa' sum bei in an ne peuhmah ka hi uh hiam? Tua ahih kei leh amah in letsong khat peuhpeuh kote hong pia ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ciangin Israel mite in Judah mite dawngin, “Kumpipa sungah tanh sawm ka nei uh a, David' sungah note khempeuh sangin tam ka neizaw uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin note in kote hong simmawh na hi uh hiam? Kote pen i kumpipa ciahpih kikding a gen masate hi lo ka hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi. Ahih hangin Israel mite' kammal sangin Judah mite' kammal kihtakhuai zaw hi.
Tua ciangin Joab in Amasa kiangah, “Ka sanggampa aw, bang cici na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Joab in amah a hopih kawmin a taklam khut tawh a khamul in Amasa man hi.
Tua ciangin tua nu' maiah Joab hong pai hi. Tua numei in, “Nang, Joab na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Ka hi hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin tua numei in ama kiangah, “Na nasemnu' thugente ngai in,” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Ka ngai hi,” a ci hi.
Kei pen Israel sungah tua bangin kilemna a deih a thuman mi khat ka hi hi. Nang in Israel sungah nu tawh a kibang khuapi khat suksiatding na hanciam hi. Bang hangin Topa' gamhluah valhtumding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Sheva pen lai-atpa ahi hi. Zadok le Abiathar siampite ahi uh hi.
Jair mi Ira zong David' siampi ahi hi.
Tua ciangin David in Gibeon mite kiangah, “Note a dingin bang hong hihsakding ka hi hiam? Note'n Topa' mite thupha na piaktheih nadingun bangci bangin kilemna hong bawlding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Gibeon mite in ama kiangah, “Kote le Saul ahi a, a innkuan tawh kikalah ahi zongin kitotna a om pen ngun le kham in maisak zo loding hi. Israelte sungah mi khatpeuh ka thah hangun zong lungkim zawh nading om lo hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Note ading kong hihsakding bang hi, ci na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Saul' zineu, Aiah' tanu Rizpah' gamtatna thu David kiangah a kigen ciangin,
Amah'n Israelte a phin ciangin, David' sanggampa Shimei' tapa Jonathan in amah that hi.
Amah'n, “ Topa, kei hong hupa, ka kulhpi, kei hong honkhia pa,
A phat taak Topa ka sam a, ka galte kiang panin kei hong kihon hi.
Leinuai khaute in kei hong kancip a, sihna thangte in kei hong dawntuah hi.
“Tua ciangin ama hehna hangin leitung kisingin, nakpitakin kilokgawp a, vantung bulpite kilinggawp hi.
Amah'n vantungte niamsakin hong paisuk a, ama khenuaiah khuamial sahpi om hi.
Kherub khat tungah amah tuangin hong leng a, huih khate tungah amah kimu hi.
Amah'n ama kimkotah khuamial bawl a, a tung kikhuh nadingin meii sahpi a zang hi.
Ama mai-a a taang sung panin mei-amte kuangkhia hi.
“Vantung panin Topa hong awngsuk a, Sang Penpa in a aw hong gingsak hi.
Amah'n thaltangte lawnin thehthang gawp a, khuaphialep phiasakin amaute a taisak hi.
Ama maiah kawk ka baang kei a, kisuanna dangte panin hoihtakin ka kikem hi.
Nangmah in mi niamte na honkhia a, ahih hangin a kiphasakte na niamkhiat hi.
Topa longal Pasian kua hiam? I Pasian simloh, hong hu kua hiam?
Hih Pasian, a muanhuai keima belh hi a, ka lampi khempeuh lungmuanhuaisak hi.
Amah'n sakhipite' khe bangin ka khe kipsak a, mun sangnaah keimah hong koih hi.
Amah'n galsimzia kei hong hilh a, sumngo thal khauhpente ka keekzo hi.
Ka kalsuan nading mun tanzau keima nuaiah nong pia a, ka khe taal lo hi.
Ka galte delhin ka susia a, amaute a beitum mateng kei ka kileh kei hi.
“Leivui bangin amaute ka satvui a, kongzing buante bangin amaute tuankhamin ka sikcipsuk hi.
Gamdang mite lungkia uh a, a phualkip panun lingin hong paikhia uh hi.
hong thuksakin, keima nuaiah mite a koihsuk Pasian,
Hi hi, ka innkuan zong Pasian tawh tua bangmah hi lo ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in tawntung thuciamna kei tawh hong bawl a, na khempeuh a hoih a kipin hih hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh keimah hong huhin, ka deihna khempeuh tangtungsakding hi lo ahi hiam?
Tua hunin munmuanhuai sungah David om a, Filistia khuacingte Bethlehemah om uh hi.
Joab' sanggampa Asahel zong sawmthumte' lakah khat ahi hi. Bethlehem mi Dodo' tapa Elhanan,
Harod khuami Shammah, Harod khuami Elika,
Palti mi Helez, Tekoa khuami Ikkesh' tapa Ira,
Anathoth khuami Abiezer, Hushah mi Mebunnai,
Ahoah mi Zalmon, Netofah khuami Maharai,
Netofah khuami Baanah' tapa Heleb, Benjamin mite' gam sunga om Gibeah khuami Ribai' tapa Ittai,
Pirathon khuami Benaiah, Gaash gei-a kuam pan Hiddai,
Betharabah khuami Abialbon, Bahurim khuami Azmaveth,
Shaalbon khuami Eliahba, Jashen' tapate, Jonathan,
Harar mi Shammah, Harar mi Sharar' tapa Ahiam,
Maakah khuami Ahasbai' tapa Elifelet, Gilo khuami Ahithofel' tapa Eliam,
Karmel khuami Hezro, Arbi mi Paarai,
Zobah khuami Nathan' tapa Igal, Gad mi Bani,
Ammon mi Zelek, Zeruiah' tapa galhiam a tawi Beeroth khuami Naharai,
Ithri mi Ira, Ithri mi Gareb,
Hit mi Uriah, a vekpi in sawmthum le sagih ahi uh hi.
Ahih hangin Joab in kumpipa kiangah, “Ka to kumpipa' muhin Topa na Pasian in mite tu-a a omzah za khatin a tamna behlap tahen. Ahih hangin bang hangin ka to kumpipa in hih thu deih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin David kiangah Gad hong pai in ama tungah gen a, “Na gam sungah kum thum sung kialpi hong tungding hiam? Ahih kei leh na galte in nang hong delh laitakin amaute' maiah kha thum sung taiding na hi hiam? Ahih kei leh na gam sungah ni thum sung pulnatna hong tungding ahi hiam? Tu in ngaihsun in; kei hong sawl pa' kiangah bang dawnna puakkikding ka hi hiam khentat in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin mite a vat vantungmi a muh ciangin David in Topa' tungah thu gen a, “En in, ka mawh hi; a khialpa pen kei ka hi hi. Hih mite in bang khialhna nei ahi uh hiam? Kong thum hi; kei le ka innkuante bek gim hong pia in,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Topa' thupiak bangin Gad' cihna zui in David paito hi.
Tua ciangin Araunah in, “Bang hangin ka to kumpipa a nasempa kiangah hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. “Mite' tung panin gimna a ven' theih nadingin Topa ading biakna tau lam nading na ancilna mun a leiding,” a ci hi.
Apa David in, “Bang hangin tua bang tua bangin gamta na hi hiam?” ci-a dotna tawh khatvei beek amah tai ngei lo hi. Amah pen a melhoih mahmah mi khat zong ahi hi. Amah pen Absalom zom a suak ahi hi.
Tua ciangin Nathan in Solomon' nu Bathsheba kiangah, “Haggith' tapa Adonijah kumpi suak khinin, David in tua thu a theih lohna thu za nai lo na hi hiam?
Thakhatin Kumpi David kiangah pai in ama tungah, ‘Ka to kumpipa in na nasemnu' tungah hong kiciamin, “Na tapa Solomon pen keima nungah maangin, keima kumpi tokhom tungah tuding hi,” ci hi lo na hi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin Adonijah kumpi suak ahi hiam?' ci in.
Bathsheba kunin kumpipa tungah zahtakna bawl a, kumpipa in, “Bang deih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Kumpipa tawh tua nu kiho in a om laitakin kamsangpa Nathan hong tum hi.
Tua ciangin Nathan in, “Ka to kumpipa aw, ‘Keima nungah Adonijah maangin ka kumpi tokhom tungah tuding hi,' ci na hi hiam?
Ka to kumpipa in hih thu thukimpihin, nangma khit ciangin ka to kumpipa' tokhom tungah kua tuding cih thu na nasem kote' kiangah hong im na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Kumpipa kiciamin, “Haksatna khempeuh panin kei a hong honkhia Topa a nungta ahih mah bangin,
Adonijah le amah tawh a om leenglate khempeuh in a pawi bawl a man khit uh ciangin hih thu za uh hi. Joab in peengkul aw a zak ciangin amah in, “Khuapi sungah hih gamlumna bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tu in Solomon in kumpi tokhom luah khinta hi.
Tua ciangin Adonijah in Solomon kihta hi. Amah pai in biakna tau kite pom hi.
David' sihding hun a nai ciangin amah in a tapa Solomon thuhilhin,
Tua ciangin David si a, David khuapi sungah kivui hi.
Tua ciangin Solomon' nu Bathsheba kiangah David in Haggith tawh a neih a tapa Adonijah hong pai hi. Tua nu in, “Thunuama hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Thunuam hi,” a ci hi.
Bathsheba in, “Hoih mahmah hi; kumpipa kiangah kong gensakding hi,” a ci hi.
Kumpi Solomon in a nu dawngin, “Bang hangin Adonijah a dingin Shunem mi Abishag hong ngen na hi hiam? Kumpi gam zong ama a dingin ngetsak lai vet in; bang hang hiam cih leh amah ka u hi a, ama lamah siampi Abiathar le Zeruiah' tapa Joab pang hi,” a ci hi.
Jerusalem panin Gathah Shimei pai in a ciahkikna thu Solomon kiangah a kigen ciangin
kumpipa in mi sawlin Shimei samsakin ama kiangah, “ Topa tawh hong kiciam sakin, thupi takin nang hong thuhilhin, ‘Nang, mun khat peuhpeuhah na paikhiat ni in na sihding teltakin thei in,' hong ci hi lo ka hi hiam? Tua ciangin nangmah in, ‘Na thugen hoih hi; ka mang hi,' na ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin Topa' tungah na kiciamna le nang hong thuhilhin kong thupiakna zui lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin keimah in a sia le a pha ka theihtheih nadingin na mite uk nading thu theihtelna lungsim na nasempa hong pia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih a lian a tam na mite kua in ukzoding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Solomon' thungetna in Topa lungkimsak hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa kiangah numei paktat nih hong pai in a mai ahding uh hi.
Amah'n delhphahkha ahih manin zanin hih numei' tapa a si hi.
Kumpi Solomon pen Israel mi khempeuh tungah kumpi hi a,
Tua a vaihawm uliante: Benhur: Efraim mualtung gam sungah;
Bendeker: Makaz khua, Shaalbim, Bethshemesh khua, le Elonbethhanan khua sungah;
Benhesed: Arubboth khua sungah (Soko le Hefer gam khempeuh ama a' hi);
Benabinadab: Nafathdor gam sung khempeuhah (amah in Solomon' tanu Tafath zi in nei hi);
Iddo' tapa Ahinadab: Mahanaim khua sungah;
Ahimaaz: Naftali gam sungah (amah in Solomon' tanu Basemath zi inla hi);
Hushai' tapa Baana: Asher gam le Bealoth khua sungah;
Paruah' tapa Jehoshafat: Issakhar gam sungah;
Ela' tapa Shimei: Benjamin gam sungah;
Solomon ading ni khatin annek tuidawn, annel lawh sawmthum, le an lawh sawmguk,
Solomon' pilna in nisuahna lam mi khempeuh le Egypt pilna khempeuh khumlet hi.
Amah'n paunak tulthum zong genkhia a, ama laphuah dawng tul le dawng nga ahi hi.
Tua ciangin Solomon in Hiram kiangah kam khak a,
Tua ahih ciangin Hiram in ama deih taamtak le taaksan singte Solomon pia a,
Tua ciangin amah in biakinn a dingin a pualam a kihui tawlette a bawl hi.
Tu in Topa' thu Solomon' tungah hong tung a,
Tua ahih ciangin Solomon in biakinn lamin a zo hi.
Biakinn sungnung mai-a innsung,pi sawmguk sau hi.
Amah'n Topa' Thuciamna Singkuang koih nadingin a sungtawng penah biakinn sungnung a bawl hi.
Amah'n kham tawh tua kherubte a zut hi.
A sungnung le a puanung inndei sung innsualte amah in kham tawh a zut hi.
Tua bangmahin amah in kiu li nei in biakinn sung lutna oliv sing kongkhak khuamte,
A kum lina, Ziv kha in Topa' biakinn a bulpi kipan hi.
Tua ciangin Kumpi Solomon in mi sawlin Taia khua-a om Huram samsak hi.
a kingakna sawmte, le a kingaknate tungah a om tuikuang sawmte;
tuikuangpi khat, le tuikuangpi nuaiah a om bawngtal sawm le nihte ahi hi.
Jordan zanglei, Sukkoth le Zarethan kikal beel leiah kumpipa in tua nate sungsak hi.
Siangtho mun panin siampite a paikhiat ciangin meii in Topa' biakinn tuam a,
Israel Pasian, Topa' min dingin biakinn khat lamding kapa David' lungsim sungah om ngei hi.
“Ahih hangin leitungah Pasian teng taktakding ahi hiam? Vantung le vantung a sangpen in nang hong huam zo lo hi. Tua ahih manin keima lamsa hih biakinn in bangzahin nang hong huam zo lo zaw kanding ahi hiam?
amau' hong thungetna le hong thumna vantung panin za in amau' vai huh in.
Tua ciangin amah dingin awging pha tawh Israel a kikhawmte khempeuh thupha pia in,
Gibeon-a ama tungah a kilahsa bangin Solomon tungah Topa a nihveina kilang hi.
Tua ciangin hih biakinn pen ninbulomtang suakding a, a nawkkha mi khempeuh in lamdangsa in, eh! ciding uh hi. Amaute'n, ‘Bang hangin Topa'n hih leitang le hih biakinn hih bangin hih ahi hiam?' ciding uh hi.
Solomon in inn nihte, Topa' biakinn le kumpi inn a lam kum sawmnih a beina,
Tua ahih ciangin amah in, “Ka sanggam aw, kei nong piak hih khuapite a bangci khuapi ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tuni dongin tuate Kabul gam kici hi.
Hiram in kumpipa kiangah a piak kham talen zakhat le talen sawmnih a pha hi.
Tua ahih manin Solomon in Gezer khua lamkik hi). Tua banah Bethhoron nuainung
le Baalath le Judah gam sung gamlakah Tamar,
Solomon' innlam nasep a uk ulianpite mi zanga le sawmnga ahi hi.
Sheba kumpinu in Solomon' pilna, ama lamsa a inn,
Tua bangin Kumpi Solomon in hauhna le pilna tawh leitung kumpi khempeuh khumkhelh hi.
Ahih hangin Faro in ama kiangah, “Nangma gamah ciahding na hanciam nadingin kei tawh na omnaah bang kitangsapna nei na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Ahi zongin amah in Faro' kiangah, “Hong paisak hoh in,” a ci hi.
Jerusalem panin Israelte khempeuh tungah Solomon in a uk hun kum sawmli sung ahi hi.
Tua ciangin Kumpi Rehoboam in apa Solomon a nuntak lai in ama maiah ading ngei khangham mite thu dongin, “Hih mite ka dawn nading ngaihsutna hong bangci piakding na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n amaute kiangah, “‘Napa in kote tungah hong suat vangik zangsak in,' kei tungah hong ci hih mite i dawn nading ngaihsutna hong bangci piakding na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Kumpipa in amau' thu a ngaih lohna Israelte khempeuh in a muh uh ciangin mite in kumpipa dawng uh a, “David sungah kote in bang ngah nei ka hi uh hiam? Jessi tapa sungah gamhluah ka nei kei uh hi. Israelte aw, na inn ciat uhah ciah un. Rehoboam in ama ading vaihawmtawmta hen,” a ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin Israelte a inn ciat uhah kihem uh hi.
Ahih hangin Rehoboam in Judah khuapite sungah a teng Israel mite a uk hi.
Tua ahih ciangin tuni dongin leilulam Israelte in David' suante' ukna lehdo uh hi.
Ahih hangin Pasian' mi Shemaiah' tungah Pasian' thu hong tung hi:
Amah'n Bethelah khat koihin, Danah adang khat a koih hi.
Tua ciangin apa un amaute kiangah, “Koi lamah amah pai ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin a tapate in Judah panin hong pai Pasian' mipa a paina lam a hilh uh hi.
Tua ciangin Pasian' mipa nungah amah pai a, tawsaw khat nuaiah tu in amah mu hi. Tua ciangin amah in Pasian' mipa kiangah, “Nang pen Judah panin a hong pai Pasian' mipa na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “Kei tawh innah hong ciahin an ne in,” a ci hi.
Tua hun laitakin Jeroboam' tapa Abijah a ci na hi.
Ahih hangin Ahijah in amah kongkhak hong tun a kheging a zak ciangin, “Hong tum in Jeroboam' zi aw, bang hangin midang khat kineih na hi hiam? Nang a dingin thugik khat kei tungah hong kipia hi.
Kumpi Rehoboam' kum ngana kumin Jerusalem a sim dingin Egypt kumpi Shishak hong kuanto hi.
Tua ciangin Rehoboam le Jeroboam' kikalah galkidona om tawntung hi.
Tu in Abijam' nuntak sung tawntung amah le Jeroboam' kikalah kidona om hi.
Israel kumpi Jeroboam' kum sawmnihna kumin Asa in Judah tungah ukding kipan a,
Ama pupi David a gamtat bangin Topa' muhnaah Asa a manin gamta hi.
Amau' hun sung tawntung Asa le Israel kumpi Baasha kikalah galkidona om hi.
Baasha in tua thu a zak ciangin Ramah a lam khawlin Tirzahah om hi.
Amau' hun sung khempeuh Asa le Israel kumpi Baasha kikalah galkidona a om hi.
Tua ciangin Baasha langpangin Hanani tapa Jehu tungtawnin Topa' thu hong tung a,
Omri' tapa Ahab, ama mai-a mite khempeuh sangin Topa' muhnaah a sia tamzaw gamta hi.
Amah'n Samaria-a a lam Baal inn sungah Baal a dingin biakna tau khat dingsak hi.
Tua ciangin ama kiangah Topa' thu hong tung a,
“Hih lai panin kihemin nisuahna lamah kihei inla, Jordan nisuahna lam Kherith luiah bu in.
Tua ciangin Elijah kiangah Topa' thu hong tung a,
Tua ciangin amah in Elijah kiangah, “Pasian' mipa aw, kei' langkhatah bang thu nei na hi hiam? Ka khialhna a pholakding ka tapa' sihna a piangsak dingin kei kiangah nong pai hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa' tungah kiko in, “ Topa ka Pasian aw, ama tapa thahna tawh ka peemna meigongnu' tung nangawnah gimna hong tungsak na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Elijah' aw ngai hi; naupang hong nak kikin a hingkik hi.
Obadiah lamkalah a om laitakin, Elijah in amah na dawntuah hi. Obadiah in amah thei in a mai lei ngatin puk a, “Ka to Elijah, nang na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n, “Hong thah dingin Ahab' khut sungah na nasempa nong piak nadingin bang thuah khial ka hi hiam?
Jezebel in Topa' kamsangte a thah lai in Topa' kamsangte mi zakhat, sawmngasawmnga in leihawm sungah seelin, amaute anletui tawh ka vakna thu ka topa tungah hong kigen nai lo ahi hiam?
Ahab in Elijah a muh ciangin, “Israel mite a lungkhamsak pa, nang na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin mi khempeuh' naiah Elijah hong pai in, “Ngaihsutna kibang lo thu nih kikalah bang tanvei khensat loin om nilohding na hi uh hiam? Topa pen Pasian ahihleh amah zui un; tua hi loin Baal pen Pasian ahihleh amah zui un,” a ci hi. Ahi zongin mite in kam khat beek dawng lo uh hi.
Tua ciangin biakna tau kimkotah tui luang a, a hawklam zong tui tawh kidim hi.
Tua ciangin leihawm khatah amah tungin tua laiah giak hi. Topa'n Elijah hopih a, “Elijah, hih laiah bang hih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Elijah in a zak ciangin a puan tawh a mai tuamin paikhia a, leihawm lutna ahding hi. Ama kiangah aw khat hong ging a, “Elijah, hih laiah bang hih na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in a bawngtalte nusia in Elijah' nungah tai a, “Ka nu le kapa kam vaikhakin hong namsak phot in; tua ciangin nang kong zuiding hi,” a ci hi. Amah'n Elisha kiangah, “Paikik in; nang hong khaktan ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel kumpi Ahab kiang naiah kamsang khat hong pai in, “ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: Hih mihon tampi khempeuh na mu hiam? En in, tuni in nangma khut sungah kong piading hi. Tua ciangin keimah, Topa ka hihna na theiding hi, ci hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Ahab in, “Kua tawh hiding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: Gamte a ukte' nasemte tawh, ci hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Kua'n galsim panding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Nangmah in na panding hi,” a ci hi.
Khuakhal ciangin Benhadad in Syriate khawmin Israel mite a sim dingin Afekah a kuanto hi.
Tua ahih ciangin amaute in a kawng uhah puanhampi tengin a lu uhah khauhual vialin Israel kumpipa kiangah pai uh a, “Na nasempa Benhadad in, ‘Kong thum hi, kei hong nungtasak in,' ci hi,” a ci uh hi. Amah'n, “Amah nungta lai ahi hiam? Amah ka sanggam bang ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin a zi Jezebel ama kiangah hong pai in, “An a ne lo zah dingin bang hangin na lungsim tua zahin heh ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a zi Jezebel in, “Tu laitakin Israel mite a ukpa hi lo na hi hiam? Tho in an ne inla, na lungsim nuamsak in. Keimah in Jezreel khuami Naboth' leenggui lo nangma tungah kong piading hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Tishbe khuami Elijah tungah Topa' thu hong tung a,
Nangmah in ama kiangah, ‘ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: “That khinin zong luahkhin na hi hiam?” ci hi,' na ciding hi. Tua ciangin ama kiangah, ‘ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: “Uite in Naboth' sisan a liahna munah uite in nangma sisan liakding uh hi,” ci hi,' ci in gen in,” a ci hi.
Ahab in Elijah a muh ciangin, “Ka galpa aw, kei hong mu na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “ Topa' muhnaah a sia a gamta dingin nangmah kipiatawm na hih manin nang kong mu hi.
Tu in Tishbe khuami Elijah tungah Topa' thu hong tung a,
“Keima maiah bangzahin Ahab a kiniamkhiatna na mu hiam? Keima maiah amah kiniamkhiat ahih manin ama hun sungin siatna ka tungsak keiding hi. Ahih hangin a tapa' hun sungin ama innkuan tungah siatna ka tungsakding hi,” a ci hi.
Kum thum sung Syria le Israel gal kido loin om uh hi.
Tua ciangin Israel kumpipa in a nasemte kiangah, “Ramothgilead eima a' hi a, eite pau loin omin Syria kumpipa' khutsung panin i lakkhiat lohna thu na thei uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in Jehoshafat kiangah, “Ramothgileadah galsim dingin kei nong zuiding hiam?” a ci hi. Jehoshafat in Israel kumpipa kiangah, “Kei a kipan ka mite le ka sakolte nangma a' ka hi uh hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Jehoshafat in, “Thu i dot theihding Topa' kamsang adang khat beek om nawn lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Kumpipa kiangah amah a tun ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Mikaiah aw, Ramothgileadah galsim dingin i kuanding hiam, ahih kei le i thuakding hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in dawngin, “Kuanto inla va gualzo ve. Topa'n kumpipa' khut sungah hong piading hi ven',” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “ Topa' min tawh thudang gen loin thuman bek kei tungah nong gen nading bangzah vei hong thuhilhding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel kumpipa in Jehoshafat kiangah, “Amah'n kei' thu a hoih gen loin a sia gending hi, nang kiangah hong ci khin hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n, ‘Amah kuanto in Ramothgileadah a va sih nadingin kua in Ahab va zolding hiam?' ci hi. Khat in thu khat genin adang khat in thudang khat gen hi.
Topa'n ama kiangah, ‘Bang lam tawh zolding na hi hiam?' a ci hi. Amah'n, ‘Keimah paikhia in, ama kamsangte khempeuh sungah a zuau kha ka va hiding hi,' ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Nangmah in amah a va zolding na hi a, nangmah in na zoding hi; paikhia inla tua bangin va hih in,' ci hi.
Tua ciangin Khenaanah' tapa Zedekiah a naiah hong pai in Mikaiah a paang bengin, “Nang' tungah thu a gen dingin Topa' kha in cikin kei hong nusia in nang kiang hong tung ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Israel kumpipa le Judah kumpipa Jehoshafat, Ramothgileadah kuanto uh hi.
Tua bangin Ahab si a, ama tangin a tapa Ahaziah in uk hi.
Israel kumpi Ahab' kum lina kumin Asa' tapa Jehoshafat in Judah gamah ukding kipan hi.
Jehoshafat in Israel kumpipa tawh zong kilemna a bawl hi.
Edomah kumpi om lo a, Judah kumpipa' khutnuai-a a huhpa khat in uk hi.
Ahab a sih khit ciangin Moab gam in Israel lehdo hi.
Ahih hangin Topa' vantungmi in Tishbe mi Elijah kiangah, “Ding in, Samaria kumpipa' kamtaite a dawn dingin paito in amaute kiangah, ‘Ekron pasian, Baalzebub kiangah thu a dong dingin na pai nadingun Israel sungah Pasian om nawn lo ahi hiam?' ci in.
Kamtaite zong kumpipa kiangah hong ciahkik uh a, amah in amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin hong ciahkik na hi uh hiam?” na ci hi.
Tua ciangin amaute in ama kiangah, “Kote a dawn dingin mi khat hong pai in kote kiangah, ‘Note hong sawl kumpipa kiangah paikik unla, Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: Ekron pasian, Baalzebub kiangah thu a dong dingin mi na sawl nadingin Israel sungah Pasian om nawn lo ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin tu-a na liamna panin na damkikzo nawn keiding a, na si taktakding hi,' hong ci hi,” a ci uh hi.
Amah'n amaute kiangah, “Note a dawn dingin hong pai in hih thute a genpa a bangci mi ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
tua ciangin ama kiangah, “ Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: ‘Nangmah in Ekron pasian, Baalzebub kiangah thu a dong dingin kamtaite na sawl khin hi. Thudot nading Israel sungah Pasian om nawn lo ahi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin tu-a na liamna panin nang na damkikzo nawn keiding a, na si taktakding hi,' ci hi,” a ci hi.
Ahaziah' gamtatna a sepsa a omlaite, Israel Kumpite' Khang Tangthu Laibu sungah kigelh hi.
Tua ciangin Bethelah a om kamsang honkhat Elisha kiangah hong pai in ama kiangah, “ Topa'n tuni in nangma kiang panin na topa a lakkhiatding na thei hiam?” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Hi hi, ka thei hi; bangmah gen nawn kei un,” a ci hi.
Jerikhoah a om kamsang honkhat in Elisha hong naihin ama kiangah, “ Topa'n tuni in nangma kiang panin na topa a lakkhiatding na thei hiam?” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in dawngin, “Hi hi, ka thei hi; bangmah gen nawn kei un,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in ama tung panin a kiakhia Elijah' puanla in tui sat a, “Elijah' Pasian, Topa koiah om na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n tui a sat khit ciangin a pang khat le a pang langkhatah a tui kikhen hi. Tua ciangin Elisha pai in a galkah hi.
Tua ciangin amah Jerikhoah a khawl sungin ama kiangah amaute hong paikik uh a, amah in amaute kiangah, “Note kiangah, ‘Pai kei un,' hong ci hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Elisha' kampauna tawh kizui in tuni dongin a tui hoih hi.
Tua lai panin amah Karmel Mualah paisuak a, tua ciangin Samariaah a ciahkik hi.
Ahih hangin Ahab a sih khit ciangin Moab kumpipa in Israel kumpipa lehdo hi.
Tua ciangin amah pai in Judah kumpi Jehoshafat kiangah thu zasak a, “Moab kumpipa in kei hong lehdo hi; Moab gam a sim dingin kei tawh nong kuanding hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Kong kuanding hi; keimah a kipan ka mite le ka sakolte nangma a' ka hi uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “Koi lam tawnin kuanding ihi hiam?” a ci hi. Joram in dawngin, “Edom gam lam tawnin i kuanding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Jehoshafat in, “Ama tungtawnin Topa' tungah thu i dot theih nadingin hih laiah Topa' kamsang om lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Israel kumpipa' nasemte khat in dawngin, “Elijah a huhpa om a, Shafat' tapa Elisha ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Elisha in Israel kumpipa kiangah, “Nang tawh bang kisai ka hi hiam? Na nu' kamsangte le na pa' kamsangte' kiangah pai in,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin Israel kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Hilo hi; Moab' khut sungah hong piak dingin ko kumpi thumte a hong sampa pen Topa ahi hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Elisha in tua numei kiangah, “Nang a dingin bang hong hihsak theiding ka hi hiam? Inn sungah bang nei na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Na nasemnu in sathau biing khat cih simloh inn sungah bangmah dang nei lo hi,” a ci hi.
Nikhat amah tua laiah hong pai in inndei sungah lutin
Tua ciangin Elisha in ama kiangah, “Tu in tua nu kiangah hih bangin gen in: Thei in, kote a dingin hih haksatna khempeuh na thuak hi. Nang a dingin bang hong kihihsakding deih na hi hiam? Kumpipa kiang ahih kei leh galkap a ukpa kiangah nang tangin thu khat peuhpeuh hong kigensakding na deih a om hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Kei pen ka mipihte lakah teng ka hih manin bangmah ka kisam kei hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “Tua bang ahihleh tuanu a dingin bang kihihsak theiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Gehazi in dawngin, “Thu khat bek om hi. Tua nu in tapa nei lo a, a pasal teekta hi,” a ci hi.
Naupang a gol ciangin ni khat apa kiang anlate lakah a pai hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “Bang hangin tuni in ama kiangah paiding na hi hiam? Khadet ni ahi a, Sabbath ni ahi zongin hi lo hi,” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Hong hoih nading hi,” a ci hi.
Amah a dawn dingin thakhatin va tai inla ama kiangah, ‘Na dam hiam? Na pasal a dam hiam? Naupang a dam hiam?' va ci in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin tua nu in, “Hoih hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin tua nu in, “Ka topa' tung pan tapa hong ngen ka hi hiam? Kei hong khem kei in, hong ci hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin a nasempa in, “Mihing za khatte' maiah keimah in hih bangci lui theihding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Ahi zongin amah in, “Amaute'n a nek theih nadingun mite tungah tuate pia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa'n, ‘Amaute'n ne in khamvalding uh hi,' ci hi,” a ci kik hi.
Israel kumpipa in a laikhak a sim ciangin amah in a puante balkekin, “Mi khat a phaknatna damsak dingin hih mipa in kei tungah hih thu hong puak nadingin a thatding le a nungtasak dingin kei, Pasian ka hi hiam? Ngaihsun dih un. Kei tawh kitotnading a zonna thei un,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Israel kumpipa in a puante a balkekna thu Pasian' mipa Elisha in a zak ciangin amah in kumpipa kiangah mi sawlin, “Bang hangin na puante balkek na hi hiam? Israel sungah kamsang khat a omna thu amah in a theih nadingin tu in kei kiangah amah hong paisak in,” cisak hi.
Israel tuite khempeuh sangin Damaskas gam a om Abana le Farpar gun tuite hoihzaw hi lo ahi hiam? Tuate' sungah kisilin siang thei loding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah kihei in paikhia hi.
Ahih hangin a nasemte a naiah hong pai in ama kiangah, “Ka topa aw, kamsangpa in na lian khat a sem dingin hong sawl hileh semding hi lo na hi hiam? Tua ahih ciangin amah in nang kiangah, ‘Kisil inla siang in,' hong cih ciangin na hihding bangzahta in kilawmzaw hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Gehazi in Naaman nungdelh hi. Tua ciangin ama nungah mi khat hong taina Naaman in a muh ciangin amah a dawn dingin a leeng panin kum a, “Thu a hoihkim hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah sungtumin a topa' mai ahding a, tua ciangin Elisha in ama kiangah, “Gehazi aw, koiah pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n, “Na nasempa koimah pai lo hi,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin Elisha in ama kiangah, “Nangmah a dawn dingin a leeng tung panin mipa a kihei laitakin nang tawh ka kha omkhawm hi lo ahi hiam? Sum le puante, oliv huante le leenggui lote, tuute le bawngtalte, nasem numeite le nasem pasalte sanding hun ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin Pasian' mipa in, “Koi laiah kia ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n a kiatna mun ama kiangah a lah ciangin amah in ciangkang khat khiakin tua munah lawn a, a heitang laamtosak hi.
Tua ciangin hih thu hangin Syria kumpipa nakpitakin patau hi. Amah'n a nasemte samin amaute kiangah, “Eite sung panin Israel kumpipa lamah a pangsim mipa hong gen loding na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Pasian' mipa' nasempa zingsangin tho baihin a paikhiat ciangin, en in, khuapi kimkotah sakolte le leengte tawh galkap honpi na om hi. Tua ciangin nasempa in, “Ala, ka topa! Bangcihding ihi hiam?” a ci hi.
Israel kumpipa in amaute a muh ciangin amah in Elisha kiangah, “Kapa aw, amaute ka thatding hiam? Amaute ka thatding hiam?” a ci hi.
Amah'n dawngin, “Amaute na that keiding hi. Na namsau le na thal tawh loin galmatin na laksate thatding na hi hiam? Amaute'n an ne in tui a dawn khit ciangin a topa uh kiangah a ciahkik theih nadingun amaute' maiah anletui lui in,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in, “ Topa'n nang hong huhding ahih kei leh koi lai panin nang hong huhding ka hi hiam? An ahi a, leenggahzu ahi zongin nei ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in tua nu dongin, “Na lungkhamna bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Hih numei in kei kiangah, ‘Tuni in amah i nek theih nadingin na tapa hong pia in; zing ciangin keima tapa i neding hi,' hong ci hi.
Elisha a inn sungah tu a, upate amah tawh tukhawm uh hi. Tu in kumpipa in ama omna panin mi khat sawlkhia hi. Ahih hangin kamtaipa a tun ma in Elisha in upate kiangah, “Hih mi thatpa in ka lutang a tankhia dingin hong sawlna na mu uh hiam? En un, kamtaipa hong tun ciangin kong khak unla, ama langkhatah khauhtakin kongkhak lencip un. Ama nungah a topa' kheging hong kiza hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Amaute tawh amah a kiho laitakin ama kiangah kumpipa hong paisukin, “Hih lungkhamna Topa' piansak hi lo ahi hiam! Bang hangin Topa'n bang khat peuhpeuh a sepding ngaklaiding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin a ban tungah kumpipa a kingapna galkap ukpa in Pasian' mipa kiangah, “ Topa mahmah in vantung tawlette honghong taleh zong, hih bang thu hi theiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Ahih hangin amah in, “Nangma mit mahmah tawh hih thu na muding a, ahih hangin nang in na nekha keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua laitakin kulhkongpi lutnaah a phak mi li om hi. Amaute khatlekhat in, “I sih dongin bang hangin hih laiah tuding ihi hiam?
galkap ukpa in Pasian' mipa dawngin, “ Topa mahmah in vantung tawlette honghong hitaleh zong, hih bang thu hi theiding ahi hiam?” ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Nangma mit mahmah tawh hih thu na muding a, ahih hangin nang in na nekha keiding hi,” ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin amah a dawn dingin Hazael pai a, Damaskas a na hoih namkim kalaoh puak sawmli, letsong a keng hi. Amah hong tungin ama maiah a din ciangin amah in, “Syria kumpipa na tapa Benhadad in nang kiangah kei hong sawlin, ‘Hih natna panin ka damkikzoding hiam?' ci hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Hazael in, “Bang hangin ka topa kap na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Bang hang hiam cih leh Israel mite tungah nangmah in na bawlding siatna ka thei hi. Nangmah in amau' munmuanhuaite mei tawh na halding a, namsau tawh amau' tangvalte thatin, amau' naupang neute lei na denkhapnading a, naupaii amau' numeite na phelkhamding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Hazael in, “Ui bang ahi lel na nasempa in hih na lian a hih dingin bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Elisha in dawngin, “Syria tungah nang kumpi na hihding thu Topa'n kei tungah hong lak khinzo hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Elisha kiang panin amah kihemkhia a, ama kiangah, “Elisha in nang kiangah bang hong ci ahi hiam?” a na ci Benhadad kiangah va tung hi. Tua ciangin amah in dawngin, “Amah'n kei kiangah nang na damkik taktaknading thu hong gen hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin kamsang tangvalpa Ramothgileadah pai hi.
Amah a tun ciangin, galkap a ukte in thu kikupna na nei uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “A ukpa aw, nang tungah thugending khat ka nei hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Jehu in, “Kote lakah kua' tungah nei na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Nangma tung hi, a ukpa aw,” a ci hi.
A topa' nasemte kiangah Jehu hong pusuah ciangin amaute in ama kiangah, “Thu khempeuh a hoih hiam? Bang hangin hih mihaipa nang kiangah hong pai ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “A mipa le a thugen na thei uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua laitakin Jezreel tausang tungah galvil pading a, amah hong pai laitakin Jehu' pawlte amah in mukhia a, “Mi honkhat ka mu hi,” ci hi. Tua ciangin Joram in, “Sakol tung tuang mi khatla in amaute a dawn dingin sawl inla, ‘Thuhoih ahi hiam?' cisak in,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin sakol tung tuangin amah a dawn dingin mi khat pai a, “Kumpipa in hih bangin ci hi: ‘Thuhoih ahi hiam?' ci hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Jehu in, “Thuhoih tawh bang hihding na hi hiam? Kihem inla ka nungah hong pai in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin galvilpa in thu zasakin, “Kamtaipa in amaute kiang ban a, ahih hangin amah hong kilehkik lo hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin amah in sakol tung tuang a nihna sawlin amaute kiangah tuapa paisak a, “Kumpipa in hih bangin hong ci khin hi: ‘Thuhoih ahi hiam?' ci hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Jehu in dawngin, “Thuhoih tawh bang hihding na hi hiam? Kihem inla ka nungah hong pai in,” a ci hi.
Joram in Jehu a muh ciangin, “Jehu aw, thuhoih ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Na nu Jezebel' paktatnate le aisannate tua zahin a tam laiteng bang thuhoih om theiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Kulhkongpiah Jehu hong lut laitakin Jezebel in, “Nang Zimri! A topa a thatpa aw, bang hih a hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin tawlet lamah Jehu khuadak to in, “Kei' lamah kua om na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Innsung maangte nih khawng thum khawng in amah hong ensuk hi.
Ahih hangin amaute nakpitakin lau uh a, “En un, kumpi nihte in amah nang zo lo uh ahih ciangin eite in bangci nanzawhding ihi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Zingsangin amah a paikhiat ciangin tua mite khempeuh kiangah, “Note na paubaang kei uh hi. Kumpi Joram sawmsimin a thatpa keimah ka hi hi. Ahih hangin hihte khempeuh a sattuk kua ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin amah dingkhia in Samariaah a pai hi. Lamkal, Tuucingte' Buk a tun laitakin,
Jehu in Judah kumpi Ahaziah' behte tuak a, amah in, “Kuate na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amaute in dawngin, “Ahaziah' behte ka hi uh a, Jezreel khua-a om kumpinu' tapate le kumpita dangte kiangah a hawh dingin hong paisuk ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
Tua lai panin amah a kihepkhiat ciangin amah a dawn dingin a hong pai Rekhab' tapa Jehonadab tawh kituak hi. Jehu in tuapa hopihin ama kiangah, “Keima lungsim nang tungah a thuman bangin nang' lungsim kei' tungah a thuman hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Jehonadab in dawngin, “Man hi,” a ci hi. Jehu in, “A man le na khut hong khak in,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a khut a khak hi. Tua ciangin Jehu in leeng sungah amah kaito hi.
Baal biakinn sunga om biakna song paikhiatpihin a hal uh hi.
Tua bangin Jehu in Israel sung panin Baal siakkhia hi.
Jehu in Samaria panin Israel tungah kum sawmnih le giat sung a uk hi.
Tua ciangin Sabbath ni in na semin Topa' biakinn acing no a khennihte in
Joash in ukding a kipat ciangin ama khan kum sagih pha pan hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Kumpi Joash in siampi Jehoiada le siampi dangte samin amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin biakinn puah lo na hi uh hiam? Tua ahih ciangin tu in na nasepna uh mite kiang panin na sumlakte uh kem nawn kei unla, a sumte biakinn puah nadingin ap un,” a ci hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa' biakinn a puah nasemte tungah tua sumte kipia hi.
Tu in Syria kumpipa Hazael in Jehoahaz' hun sung khempeuh Israel mite nengniam hi.
Syria kumpipa Hazael a sih ciangin ama tangin a tapa Benhadad kumpi a suak hi.
Nangmah in Edom na vatgawp khin a, na lungsim in nang hong liansak hi. Na minthanna tawh lungkim inla, innah om in; bang hangin nang tukin, Judah tawh nang na tuk nadingin buaina piangsak seding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tu in Amaziah' nasepna a omlaite, Judah Kumpite' Khang Tangthu Laibu sungah kigelh hi.
Apa Amaziah' sepna khempeuh tawh kizui in Topa' mitah a man gamta hi.
Tu in Zekhariah' sepna a omlaite, Israel Kumpite' Khang Tangthu Laibu sungah kigelh hi.
Tua ciangin Menahem si a, ama tangin a tapa Pekahiah in a uk hi.
Apa Uzziah' gamtatnasa khempeuh bangin Topa' mitah amah a manin gamta hi.
Kumpi Ahaz' thupiak bangin siampi Urijah in hih thu khempeuh a hih hi.
Note a dingin a gelh thukhamte, ngeina kipte, zuihding ngeinate, le thupiaknate zuihding na kingaihsun tawntungding uh hi. Note'n pasian dangte na kihta keiding uh a,
note tawh ka bawlsa thuciamna na mangngilh keiding uh hi. Note'n pasian dangte na kihta keiding uh a,
A pu David' hihna khempeuh tawh kizui in Topa' mitah a man gamta hi.
Tua ciangin a ulianpa in amaute kiangah, “Hezekiah kiangah hih bangin gen un. ‘Assiria kumpipa, kumpi lianpa in hih bangin ci hi: Hih banga na kimuanna uh bang suang na hi uh hiam?
Note'n kampau lel pen galsim nadingin thu lamlahna le thahatna in na ngaihsun uh hi. Note'n kei nong lehdo nadingun bang suang na hi uh hiam?
“‘Ahih hangin note in kei kiangah, “Kote'n Topa ka Pasian uh ka suang uh hi,” na cih uhleh, Hezekiah in mualtung a biaknate le biakna taute hepkhiatsakin Jerusalem tungah, “Jerusalem khuasung hih biakna tau maiah na biading uh hi,” a cihpa hi lo ahi hiam?
Tua ahih ciangin note in leengte le sakol tung tuangte tawh kisai in Egypt a suang kimlai in bangci in ka topa' nasemte lakah a neupen galkap ukpa khat lehnawhzoding na hi uh hiam?
Tua tham loin, Topa tawh a kikop lopi in hih mun simin a susia dingin a hong paito ka hi hiam? Topa'n kei kiangah, “Hih gam a sim dingin paito inla susia in,” hong ci hi,' ci in,” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin a ulianpa in amaute kiangah, “Ka topa in hih thute na topa uh le note tung bekah a gen dingin hong sawlin, amau' ek mah ne in, amau' zun mah dawnin note tawh a siakhawmding kulh tunga tu mite kiangah a gen lo dingin hong sawl ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Assiria kumpipa' khutsung panin minam dangte' pasian khatpeuh in a gam honkhiazo ngei ahi hiam?
Hamath le Arpad' pasiante koiah om ahi uh hiam? Sefarvaim, Hena, le Ivvah pasiante koiah om ahi uh hiam? Keima khutsung panin amaute in Samaria a honkhiazo uh hiam?
Topa'n ka khutsung panin Jerusalem a hotkhiat nadingin, gam sungah pasiante khempeuh lakah kua in keima khutsung panin a gam uh honkhiazo ngei ahi hiam?' ci hi,” a ci hi.
Kumpi Hezekiah' nasemte Isaiah kiang hong tun uh ciangin
En in, Assiria kumpite in gam khempeuh a hihnasa, a suksiat mangna thu na za khin hi. Tua ahih ciangin nang hong honkhiazoding ahi hiam?
Ka pu ka pate in a suksiat minam Gozan, Haran, Rezef, le Telassar gam sunga Eden mite, tua minamte' pasiante in amaute honkhiazo ahi hiam?
Kua zahko in, a simmawh na hi hiam? Kua langpangin na aw sang sakin kihihsakna tawh gamta na hi hiam? Israelte' a Siangtho pa, a simmawh na hi hi.
Sawt pek lai in ka ngaihsutsa ahihlam za nai lo na hi hiam? Tanglai pek panin ka geelkholhsa hi a, tu-a ka tunsakding thute kulh a nei khuapite ninbulomtangin na heinading,
Tua ciangin Assiria kumpipa Sennakherib kihemkhia a, innah ciahin Ninevehah a teng hi.

Tua ciangin Hezekiah in Isaiah kiangah, “ Topa'n kei hong damsaknading, le a ni thum ni in Topa' biakinnah ka paitohnading a lim bang hiding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Isaiah in, “ Topa'n a ciamsa thu hong hih nadingin Topa' tung panin nangma tungah a lim hih bang hiding hi: A liim kal sawm maipaiding hiam, ahih kei leh kal sawm nungkikding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Kumpi Hezekiah kiangah kamsang Isaiah hong pai in ama kiangah, “Hih mite in bang gen ahi hiam? Koi lai panin nang kiangah hong pai ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Hezekiah in, “Amaute, Babylon gam, a gamlapi panin hong pai uh hi,” a ci hi.
Amah'n, “Amaute'n na inn sungah bang mu ahi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Hezekiah in dawngin, “Amaute'n ka innsunga om khempeuh mu uh hi; ka vankoihna inn sungte panin amaute ka lah loh bangmah om lo hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Isaiah in Hezekiah kiangah, “ Topa' thu za in:
Tua ciangin Hezekiah in Isaiah kiangah, “Na gensa ahi Topa' thugen a hoih hi,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Keima hun sungin kilemna le lungmuanna a om nakleh bang phamawhding ahi hiam?” ci in ngaihsun hi.

Ama min siangtho hangin nuamin diang unla, Topa a zong mite khempeuh lungdamta uh hen!
Topa le ama hatna zong unla, ama ompihna zong den un!
A lamdang a nasepte phawk unla, a lamdang ama genkhiat a thukhennate phawk un,
no ama nasem Abraham' suante, Jakob' suante, ama teeltuamte aw!
Amah, eite' Topa Pasian hi a, ama thupiaknate leitung khempeuh ading ahi hi.
Amah'n a thuciamna phawk tawntung hi. Khang tul khat-a dingin a thupiakna kammal,
Abraham tawh a thuciamna, Isaac tungah a khapna,
Jakob tungah thu ciamin, amah in a kipsak, Israel tungah tawntung thuciamna in a kipsak,
Amaute a mi in tawmin, gentaak loin peemta hi uh a,
amaute kuamah nengniamsak lo hi. Amaute' hangin amah in kumpite taigawp a,
“Ka sathau nilhte lawng kei unla, ka kamsangte tungah siatna hih kei un!” ci hi.
Leitung mi khempeuh aw, Topala sak un! A nini in ama hotkhiatna thu gengen un.
Pahtawina le minliatna in amah umcih a, thahatna le lungdamna in amah kimkot hi.
Leitung mi khempeuh aw, Topa theitel unla, Topa' minthanna le a thahatna theitel un!
Israel mi khempeuh tawh ka painasa mun khempeuhah, keima mite tuu bangin acing dingin ka sawl thukhente khat peuhpeuh tungah, “Bang hangin taamtak biakinn khat kei a dingin hong lamsak lo na hi hiam?” ci in kam khat beek ka gen hiam?' ci hi.
Tua ciangin Kumpi David tumin Topa' maiah tu a, “ Topa Pasian aw, nangmah in hih ciang dong kei nong tunpihna kei kua hi a, ka innkuanpihte bang ahi hiam?
Na nasempa nong pahtawinaah David in nang tungah bang gending nei nawn ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh nangmah in na nasempa na thei hi.
Egypt panin na hotkhiat na mite' maiah minam dangte hawlkhiatna tawh nang a dingin a lian a lauhuai min khat na bawlna, Pasian pai in ama mi dingin a hotkhiat Israelte tawh a kibang mi leitungah minam dang kua om ahi hiam?
Ahih hangin Ammon mite' uliante in Hanun' kiangah, “David in nang kiangah hehnemte hong sawlna hangin napa a pahtawi hi, ci in ngaihsun na hi hiam? Gam sung a pheklekding le a lumletding le gam sung a ensim dingin ama nasemte na kiangah hong pai hi lo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Syria mite in Ammon mite huh nuam nawn lo uh hi.
Amah'n Israel a to ciangin David' sanggampa Shimea' tapa Jonathan in amah that hi.
Ahih hangin Joab in, “ Topa'n a mite a zah za khatin behlapta hen! Ka to kumpipa aw, amaute khempeuh ka topa' nasemte hi lo ahi uh hiam? Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin ka topa in hih kisam sa na hi hiam? Bang hangin Israel tungah mawhna tunding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin hih thuah Pasian lungkim lo a, amah in Israelte vatgawp hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n David' thumupa Gad tungah thu gen a,
Tua ciangin David in Pasian kiangah, “Mi phazah a sim dingin thu a piapa keimah hi lo ka hi hiam? Khialin a gitloh gamtat mahmahpa keimah ka hi hi. Ahih hangin hih mite in bang gamtat khialhna nei ahi uh hiam? Topa ka Pasian aw, kong thum hi, keimah le ka innkuan gim hong pia in. Ahih hangin na mite tungah gimna tungsak kei in,” a ci hi.
Tua ahih ciangin Topa' min tawh a gen Gad' kammal bangin David paito hi.
Tua ciangin Topa' thupiakna tawh vantungmi in a namsau a pai sungah a siatkik hi.
Israel makaite khempeuh in zong a tapa Solomon a huhnading David in thu pia a,
“ Topa na Pasian uh note tawh hong om hi lo ahi hiam? Amah'n na kiim khempeuh uhah lungnopna hong pia hi lo ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in gam sunga teng mite keima khut sungah hong pia khin a, Topa le ama mite' maiah gam sung khempeuh kinuaisiah hi.
