le siamneelte in a hihding nasepna khempeuh a dingin kham zatnading nateah kham, le ngun zatnading nateah ngun ahi hi. Kua teng utna lungsim tawh Topa' tungah tuni in amahmah kipia in ki-apding na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
“Ahih hangin kote in hih bangin utna tawh kong piak nadingun kei kua hi a, ka mite bang ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh na khempeuh nang kiang pan hong pai hi a, nangma a' mah nang tungah a hong pia ka hi uh hi.
Tua hi a, Jessi' tapa David in Israel khempeuh tungah a uk hi.
Hih mite ka uk theih nadingin tu in pilna le theihna hong pia in; bang hang hiam cih leh hih zahin a tam hih na mite kua in ukzoding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin vantung, a sang pen vantung nangawn in amah huam zo lo ahih manin ama a dingin kua in biakinn lamzoding ahi hiam? Ama maiah paknamtui halnading cih simloh ama a dingin biakinn a lamsak dingin kei kua ka hi hiam?
Amah'n ama uk a kum lina a kha nihna sungin lamding kipan hi.
Amah'n suangmanpha phutin a inn zem hi. A kham zatte Parvaim kham ahi hi.
Amah'n siangtho pen mun sungah sing kherub nih bawlin kham tawh tuate zut hi.
Tua ciangin amah in inn khang nisuahna lam kiuah tuikuangpi koih hi.
tuikuang a kingaknate le tuate tungah a kikoih tuikuangte,
tuikuangpi khat, le tua nuai-a a om bawngtal sawm le nihte,
Jordan zanglei sung Sukkoth le Zeredah kikal beel leiah kumpipa in hihte sungsak hi.
Solomon in hih nate tampi tak bawlsak a, sumngo a gikzah kithei zo lo hi.
a kigelhsa bangin biakinn sungnung maiah vak dingin kham citak meivakkhuamte le a meivakte;
kham hoih pen tawh a kibawl a paakte, a meivakte, le a tehte;
Tua ciangin Solomon in, “Khuamial sahpi sungah tending a teel Topa aw,
“Ahih hangin Pasian pen mite tawh leitungah hong teng takpiding ahi hiam? En in, vantung le a sangpen vantung in nang hong huam zo lo hi; hih keima lamsa biakinn in hong huam zo lo zaw kanding!
amau' hong thungetna le hong thumnate vantung panin za in amau' vai huh in.
“Amaute nang tungah hong khialin (a khial lo kua om ahi hiam?) amaute tungah nang heh a, galte tungah amaute pia in, amaute a gamla gam ahi a, a naiah ahi zongin galmatin kipuakhia a,
Tua ciangin kumpipa le mi khempeuh in Topa' maiah biakna pia uh hi.
note' tungah kong piaksa leitang panin note kong botkhiading hi. Tua ciangin ka min dingin ka apsa hih biakinn ka muhna panin ka lawnkhiading a, mi khempeuh lakah paunak le gentehna ka suaksakding hi.
“Tua ciangin a minthangsa hih biakinn a nawkkha khempeuh in lamdangsa in, ‘Bang hangin hih bangin Topa'n hih gam le hih biakinn bawl ahi hiam?' ciding uh hi.
Solomon in Topa' biakinn le ama inn a lam khit kum sawmnih a cin ciangin,
Tua ciangin Hamathzobahah Solomon pai in tua gam ala hi.
Amah'n khuapi kulh, kongpite, le zawlte a nei Bethhoron Tungnung leh Bethhoron Nuainung,
Sheba kumpinu in Solomon' pilna, a lamsa inn,
Solomon a dingin Egypt le gam khempeuh panin sakolte kila hi.
Solomon in Jerusalem panin Israel khempeuh tungah kum sawmli sung uk hi.
Amah kumpi a suaksak dingin Israel khempeuh Shekhemah pai ahih manin Shekhemah Rehoboam pai hi.
Amah'n amaute kiangah, “Kei kiangah, ‘Napa in kote tungah hong suat vangik zangsak in,' a hong ci hih mite i dawnnading bang ngaihsutna hong pia na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in amaute ngawh dawnin, khangham mite' ngaihsutna nusia a,
Kumpipa in amaute' thu a ngaih lohna Israel mi khempeuh in a muh uh ciangin mite in kumpipa dawngin, “David' sungah kote in bang ngah nei ka hi uh hiam? Jessi' tapa' sungah gamhluah ka nei kei uh hi. Israelte aw, na inn ciat uhah ciah un. Rehoboam in ama ading vaihawm tawmta hen,” a ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin Israel mi khempeuh a inn ciat uhah kihem uh hi.
Ahih hangin Judah khuapiteah a teng Israel mite tungah Rehoboam in a uk hi.
Tua ahih ciangin tuni dongin leilu lama om Israelte in David innkuan lehdo uh hi.
Ahih hangin Pasian' mi Shemaiah' tungah Topa' thu hong tung hi:
Jerusalemah Rehoboam teng a, kihut nadingin Judah gam sungah khuapite a lam hi.
Amah'n Bethlehem, Etam, Tekoa,
Bethzur, Soko, Adullam,
Gath, Mareshah, Zif,
Adoram, Lakhish, Azekah,
Tua nu in amah tawh tapate Jeush, Shemariah, le Zaham nei hi.
Amah'n kulhnei khuapitela in Jerusalem ciang dong hong tung hi.
Tua ciangin Judah uliante le kumpipa kiniamkhiatin, “ Topa thuman hi,” a ci uh hi.
Amah'n Topa zonding a lungsimah koih lo ahih manin a sia a gamta hi.
Israel Topa Pasian in David le a suante tungah Israel kumpi hihding thuciamna kip tawh a piakna na theihding uh kilawm hi lo ahi hiam?
Ahi zongin David' tapa Solomon' nasempa, Nebat' tapa Jeroboam kipanin a topa lehdo hi.
Note mi tampi na hihna uh le note' pasian dingin Jeroboam in hong bawlsak kham bawngnote note tawh a om manin, David' suante' khut sungah a om Topa' kumpi gam doding tu in na ngaihsun uh hi.
Note'n Aaron' suan, Topa' siampite, le Levi mite hawlkhia in, gamdang mite bangin note a dingin siampite bawl khin hi lo na hi uh hiam? Bawngtalno khat tawh ahi a, tuutal sagih tawh ahi zongin a ki-ap dingin a hong pai peuhpeuh, pasian a hilote' siampi suak pahpah hi.
Abijah' gamtatna a omlaite, ama ziate le a thugente, Kamsang Iddo' Tangthu sungah kigelh hi.
Oded' tapa Azariah' tungah Pasian' kha hong tung hi.
Asa' uk kum sawm le ngana a kha thumna sungin Jerusalemah amaute kikhawm uh hi.
Amaute'n awging pha, otna, peengkulte, le sakite tawh Topa' tungah kiciamna a bawl uh hi.
Asa' uk kum sawmthum le nga ciang dong galkidona om nawn lo hi.
Ethiopia mite le Libya mite pen leeng tampi tak le sakol tung tuang tampi tak tawh a om galkap tampi hi lo ahi hiam? Ahi zongin Topa suang na hih manin amah in na khut sungah amaute hong pia hi.
Tua ciangin a tapa Jehoshafat in ama tangin uk a, Israel langpangin amahmah kithakhauhsak hi.
Israelte' gamtat bang hi loin ama pa' Pasian zongin ama thupiakna a zui hi.
Jehoshafat hau in hong minthan' ciangin Ahab tawh numei-a kizopna a bawl hi.
Israel kumpipa Ahab in Judah kumpipa Jehoshafat kiangah, “Ramothgileadah kei tawh nong kuanding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah'n dawngin, “Kei pen nangmah bang ka hi a, ka mite zong nangma mite mah bang ahi hi. Kote pen galsimnaah nang tawh kong kuanding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel kumpipa in kamsangte mihing zali khawmin amaute kiangah, “Ramothgilead a sim dingin kuantoding ka hi hiam, tua ahih kei leh thuakding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amaute in, “Kuanto in; bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian in kumpipa' khut sungah hong piading hi,” a ci uh hi.
Ahih hangin Jehoshafat in, “Eite in i dot theihding Topa' kamsang adang hih laiah om nawn lo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Kumpipa kiangah amah hong tun ciangin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Mikaiah aw, Ramothgileadah galsim dingin kuanding ka hi hiam, tua ahih kei leh thuakding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in dawngin, “Kuanto inla va gualzo ve! Na khut sungah amaute hong kipiading hi ve'n,” a ci hi.
Tua laitakin Topa'n, ‘Israel kumpipa Ahab kuanto in Ramothgileadah a pukna dingin kua in amah zolding ahi hiam?' a ci hi. Tua ciangin khat in thu khat gen a, adang khat in thudang khat a gen hi.
Tua ciangin kha khat hong madawkin Topa' mai ahding a, ‘Keimah in amah ka va zolding hi,' a ci hi. Tua ciangin Topa'n ama kiangah, ‘Bang lam tawh zolding na hi hiam?' a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Israel kumpipa le Judah kumpipa Jehoshafat, Ramothgileadah a kuanto uh hi.
Judah kumpipa Jehoshafat lungmuang takin Jerusalem-a ama innah ciahkik hi.
Ahih hangin amah a dawn dingin Hanani' tapa, thumupa Jehu hong paikhia a, Kumpi Jehoshafat kiangah, “Mi gilote huhin Topa a mudahte itding na hi hiam? Hih thu hangin Topa' hehna nang tungah hong tungzo hi.
Amah'n gam sunga Judah khuapi kulhnei khempeuh a khuapi a khuapiah thukhen dingte seh a,
Tua ciangin Topa' biakinn huangsung, inntual thak mai, Judah le Jerusalemte' kikhopna sungah Jehoshafatding a,
“ Topa , ka pu ka pate uh Pasian aw, nang, vantungah Pasian hi lo na hi hiam? Minamte' kumpi gam khempeuh tungah nang a uk hi lo na hi hiam? Na khut sungah vangliatna le thahatna om a, kuamah in nang hong nang zo lo hi.
Kote' Pasian aw, hih gamah a teng mite na mi Israelte' maiah hawlkhia in, na lawmpa Abraham' suanlekhakte tungah a tawntung dingin pia hi lo na hi hiam?
Hih gamah amaute tengin, nangma min dingin hih laiah biakinn khat lam uh a,
Kote' Pasian aw, amaute tungah thu khen loding na hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh kote a sim dingin a hong pai hih mihon tampite a do dingin thahatna ka nei kei uh hi. Ka cih nading uh ka thei kei uh a, nangmah bek kong mitsuan uh hi,” a ci hi.
Note'n hih kidonaah na doding uh kisam lo hi. Judah gam mite le Jerusalem khuamite aw, na panmun uhla in taang loinding unla, note' tangin Topa' gualzawhna mu un,' ci hi. Kihta kei unla, lungkia kei un. Zing ciangin amaute a do in pai un. Topa'n note hong ompihding hi,” a ci hi.
Amaute, harp lasaknate le laiza lasaknate tawh Jerusalem-a Topa' biakinnah tung uh hi.
Amah'n apa Asa' gamtat bangmahin Topa' muhnaah a man na sem hi.

Siampi Jehoiada' hunsung khempeuh Topa' mitah Joash a manin gamta hi.
Hih hun khit ciangin Joash in Topa' biakinn a ngei batsakkikding ngaihsun hi.
Tua ahih ciangin kumpipa in amau' ukpi Jehoiada samin ama kiangah, “ Topa' nasem Moses in Topa' ompihna puanbuk-a dingin Israel mihonte tung panin a khon mangmu bang hangin Judah le Jerusalem panin Levi mite khawmsak lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin siampi Jehoiada' tapa Zekhariah' sungah Pasian' kha hong lut hi. Tua ciangin amah dingin mite en sukin mite kiangah, “Pasian in hih bangin ci hi: ‘Bang hangin na mavan' theih loh nadingun Topa' thupiaknate palsat na hi uh hiam? Note'n Topa nusia na hih manun amah in note hong nusia hi,' ci hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Amaziah in Pasian' mipa kiangah, “Ahita zongin Israel galkapte tungah ka piaksa talen zakhat thu bang cihding ihi hiam?” a ci hi. Pasian' mipa in dawngin, “ Topa'n hih sangin nakpitakin a tamzaw hong pia thei hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Amaziah tungah Topa hehin ama kiangah kamsang khat sawl a, tuapa in, “Bang hangin nangma khut panin ama mite a honkhia lo, mi pawlkhatte' pasiante beel na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
Ahih hangin amah in thu a gen laitakin kumpipa in ama kiangah, “Kumpipa tungah ngaihsutna a pia dingin nang hong koih ka hi uh hiam? Khawl in! Bang hangin nang hong kithatding ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin kamsangpa khawl a, ahih hangin ama kiangah, “Hih bang gamta in ka thugenna ngai lo na hih manin Pasian in nang hong suksiatding a lungsim a khentatna ka thei hi,” a ci hi.
Apa Amaziah' hihsa khempeuh bangin amah in Topa' mitah a man sem hi.
A thahat galkapmang a vekpi in tulnih le zaguk ahi hi.
Ahih hangin Topa' siampi Azariah, a thahat mihing sawmgiat tawh ama nungah pai hi.
Tu in note in Judah mi le Jerusalem mi, numei le pasalte, na sal dingun nuaisiah na sawm uh hi. Topa na Pasian uh tungah nomau mahmah in khialhna nei hi lo na hi uh hiam?
Hih Kumpi Ahaz mah pen, a lungkham hunin Topa' tungah citak lozaw lai hi.
A pu David' hihnasa khempeuh bangin Topa' mitah a man gamta hi.

A ki-ap biaknate bawngtal zaguk le tuu tulthum ahi hi.

Note'n na theih uh bangin, amau' pute pate' Topa Pasian' tungah a cihtak lohna uh hangin nakpitakin gim a piak na pute na pate uh le na sanggamte uh bang kei un.
Asher mi, Manasseh, le Zebulun mi tawmkhat bek kiniamkhiatin Jerusalemah hong pai uh hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Hezekiah' thungetna pia in mite' mawhna maisak a, gimna ngahsak lo hi.

Sennakherib hong pai in Jerusalem simding a sawmna thu Hezekiah in a theih ciangin,
Mi tampi tak kikhawm uh a, gam sungah a luang tuinak le lui khempeuh khakcipin, “Bang hangin Assiria kumpite hong pai in tui tampi muding ahi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
“Assiria kumpipa Sennakherib in hih bangin ci hi: ‘Note'n Jerusalem umcihna na nannading uh bang suang na hi uh hiam?
Hezekiah in note kiangah, “Assiria kumpipa' khut panin Topa i Pasian in eite hong honkhiading hi,” hong cih ciangin, note gilkial dangtakin a hong sisak dingin amah in note hong makai khial hi lo ahi hiam?
Hih Hezekiah mah in mual dawna a biakpiaknate le ama biakna taute lakhia in Judah le Jerusalem thu pia a, “Biakna tau khat maiah note in bia in tua tungah na biakpiaknate uh na halding uh hi,” ci hi lo ahi hiam?
Keimah le ka pu ka pate in gamdang mi khempeuh tungah ka hihnasate uh thei lo na hi uh hiam? Tua gam minamte' pasian in keima khutsung panin a gam uh honkhiazo ahi uh hiam?
Na Pasian un keima khutsung panin note hong hotkhiat theih nadingin ka pu ka pate in a suksiatmang tua minamte' pasian khempeuh lakah kua in a mite honkhiazo ngei ahi hiam?
Tua ciangin ama nasemte in amah sawmsimin ama inn sungah amah that uh hi.
Kumpipa in thukham kammalte a zak ciangin a puante balkek hi.
Tua ciangin kumpipa in mi sawlin Judah le Jerusalem upa khempeuh kaikhawm hi.
Amah'n siampite amau' panmunteah seh a, Topa' biakinn sunga nasepnaah amaute hanthawn hi.
Note a khenkhenin na beh uh tawh kizui in kithawi unla, Israel kumpipa David' lamlahna le a tapa Solomon' lamlahna zui un.
Josiah' uk a kum sawm le giatna kumin hih Paisan Pawi kibawl hi.
Ahih hangin Neko in ama kiangah kamtaite sawlin, “Judah kumpipa aw, ei tegel khatlekhat i kihihnading bang om ahi hiam? Tu in nang a sim dingin hong kuan ka hi kei a, ka galte a sim dingin a hong kuan ka hi hi. Ka kinawhnading Pasian in kei tungah thu hong pia khin hi. Kei tawh a omkhawm Pasian na nialna khawl in. Tua hikeileh nang hong susiading hi,” cisak hi.
Note lakah ama mi peuhmah a Pasian in ompih henla, Judah gam sung Jerusalem khuaah paito henla, Israel Pasian, Topa' biakinn lamkik hen. Amah pen Jerusalemah a om Pasian ahi hi.

Tua laitakin Eufratis Gungal gam sung teng a uk sawn Tattenai, Shetharbozenai, le amau' lawmte hong paipahin amaute kiangah, “Note'n hih biakinn lamkikin a nate na bawlnading uh kua in thu hong pia ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.

“Kote' Pasian aw, hih bang hi khin ahih ciangin kote in bang gen thei nawnding ka hi uh hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh na nasem kamsangte tungtawnin kote thu hong pia in, ‘Note va lutin na luahding uh gam pen, tua gam aa na teng gamdang mite in ninsakin a kihhuai a gamtatnate uh tawh mong khat pan mong khat dongin a ninsa gam nin ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin na tanute uh amau' tapate tawh kitengsak kei unla, na tapate uh zi dingin amau' tanute zongla kei un. Amaute' phattuamnading le a maavannading uh hanciam kei un. Tua bang hileh note thahatin tua gam a piangte nuamtakin na neding uh a, na tate un a luah tawntung dingun tua gam na piasawn theiding uh hi,' ci in nong thupiaknate ka zui kei uh hi.
Hih banga ka thuak khit uh ciangin kote in na thupiaknate mang lo kikin, a kihhuai in a gamta mite tawh kitengin kizomkikding ka hi uh hiam? Tua bang hi kik le-ung, a suakta, a nungta ka om nawn loh dongun kote' tungah na hehna hong tungsakding hi lo na hi hiam?

Na nasem Moses tungah, ‘Na cihtak kei uhleh minam dangte lakah kong thehthangding hi.
Amah'n, “Cina lopi in bang hangin na mai khing ahi hiam? Na dahna khat om hiding hi,” hong ci hi. Tua ciangin lau mahmahna tawh
kumpipa ka dawng a, “Kumpipa nungta tawntung in. Ka pute ka pate a kivuina khuapi siagawp a, a kongpite kangtum ahih ciangin maikhing loin bangci om theihding ka hi hiam?” ka ci hi.

Jerusalem khua ka tun ciangin ni thum sung ka tawlnga hi.

Tua ahih ciangin uliante tungah ka lungkim kei a, “Bang hangin Pasian' biakinn kinusiacip ahi hiam?” ka ci hi. Tua hi a, amaute kaikhawm kikin amau' sepna ngei mun ciatah ka pangsakkik hi.
Tua ciangin Judah uliante tungah lungkim loin amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin hih bangin hoih lohna gamta in Sabbath ni ninsak ngam na hi uh hiam?
Na pu na pate uh tu-a bang teekin a gamtat manin eite tung le hih khuapi tungah hih bang siatna khempeuh hong tung hi lo ahi hiam? Tua hinapi in note in Sabbath ni nitsakna tawh Israel tungah hehna tamzaw na tungsak uh hi,” ka ci hi.
Ahi zongin amaute hilhkholin amaute kiangah, “Bang hangin kulh geiah giak na hi uh hiam? Nong giah kik uhleh note tungah thu kong bawlding hi,” ka ci hi. Tua hun a kipanin Sabbath ni in amaute hong pai nawn lo uh hi.
Israel kumpipa Solomon zong tua bang numeite' hangin khial hi lo ahi hiam? Minam tampite lakah amah tawh a kibang kumpi khat zong om lo a, ama Pasian in amah itin, Israel khempeuh tungah kumpi in amah koih hi; ahita zongin gamdang numeite in amah nangawn khialsakzo hi.

Tua hi a, Jew mite in suahtakna, lungdamna, le pahtawina ngah uh hi.

Tua ciangin Topa'n Satan kiangah, “Ka nasem Job na phawkkha hiam? A paubaang lo, a thutang, Pasian zahtakin gamtat hoih lo a peel amah tawh a kibang midang leitungah na mu keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Satan in Topa dawngin, “Job in Pasian hong mawk zahtak ahi hiam?

Hih thu khempeuhah Job khial lo a, Pasian zong mawhsak lo hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Satan kiangah, “Koi lai panin hong pai na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Satan in Topa dawngin, “Leitung khempeuh a lu pan a taw dong vak kawikawi in ka va phehlehna mun panin kong pai hi,” a ci hi.

Tua ciangin Job in,
“Ka suah ni, le ‘Pasal naungek khat kipaii hi,' a kicih zan beimang hen!
Tua zaninta piang kei henla, lungdam otna awging tua zanin ging nawnkei hen.
“Bang hangin a sisa in suak hoh lo a, bang hangin ka suah phetin si pah hoh lo ka hi hiam?
Bang hangin ka nu' khuk tungah hong kitawi se a, ka nu' nawi hong kiteepsak se ahi hiam?
inn hoihnono a lam kumpite le uliante,
Bang hangin a huncing lo-a suakte bang, khuavak a mu man loin a si naungekte bangin hong kiseelcip hoh lo ahi hiam?
Tua laiah migilote in hong sukha nawn loding a, a gim mite tawlnga hithiatding hi.
Tua lai munah milian mineu omkhawm a, silate nangawn a topa' kiang pan suakta hi.
“Bang hangin lungkhamna a thuak mipa, a nuntakna haksa a sa mahmah mipa,
han sung a tun ciangin a nuam mahmah, hankhuk a tun ciangin nuam lua in a dianggawp mite, khuavak a mu dingin mi in piang laizang ahi hiam?
Bang hangin mailam thuding a thei lopi in a mot omding, a kimkotah Pasian in daai a khaknelh mipa, mi in piang zenzen ahi hiam?
Ka kihtaktak thu ka tungah hong tungta a, ka laulau thu, ka tuakta hi.
Tua ciangin Teman khuami Elifaz in thu hong gen a,
“Mi khatpeuh in thu hong genpih leh na hehding hiam? Kua'n a kam ipzo nawnding ahi hiam?
Lunghiang mite na hanthotna, khut kha ban kha mite na thakhauhsakna,
a puk mite na thugenna tawh na kipsakna, khukzaw mite na hatsak ngeite ngaihsun in.
Na biakna in hong hehnem zo lo ahi hiam? A paubaang lo, na nuntakna in lametna hong pia zo lo ahi hiam?
Tu in ngaihsun in: Midik kimlai kua sia ngei ahi hiam? A thutang mi a kisuksiatna koiah mu ngei na hi hiam?
Mi a ihsip hun zankim laitak, zan mangmat hun laitakin
Huih in ka mai hong mut a, ka khuasikmul hong suaksak hi.
‘Pasian' maiah mi khatpeuh paubaang loin omzo ngeiding ahi hiam? Amah a Bawlpa' maiah sitbaang loin omzo ngeiding ahi hiam?
Pasian in ama nasemte mahmah muangzo loin, ama sawltakte' mawhna mu ahihleh,
amau' liatna in taisan pakding a, pilna ngah ngei loin si pakzawding hi lo ahi hiam?' hong ci hi.
“Tu in na thu ko in: Nang hong huhding om ahi hiam? A siangthote kua pen' lam zuanding na hi hiam?
Mihaipa in a hehna sihlawh a, muhdahna in sihna piangsak hi.
Leilak panin gimna hong piangtawm lo a, lei sung panin lungkhamna hong pokhiatawm lo hi.
Mei-ek a to leen mah bangin mihingte in amau' lungkhamnading mah a piangsak uh hi.
Amah'n guah zusak a, lo khempeuh tui a buak hi.
Amah'n mi niamte sangkoih a, a dahte lungnuamsak hi.
Amah'n migilote amau' gitlohna mahah awksak a, ngian a zangte' geelna zong a lumletsak hi.
Sunthapai in khuamial sung kidenna a, suntangpi mahin zan bangin mial a zawt uh hi.
Tua ahih manin mizawngte in lametna neikik uh a, thuman lo mite ahihleh kihencip hi.
“Pasian in a taii mite mi nuamsa hizaw ahih manin, Vanglianpa' taiina thupi san in.
Gensiatna panin nang hong kihuding a, siatna hong tun ciangin na lau keiding hi.
Suksiatding le puksih dingte na nuihsan lelding a, leitung gamsate na kihta keiding hi.
Tua ciangin Job in dawng a,
“Ka lunggimna kitawikhai henla, ka haksatna khempeuh kitawiteh leh!

An lim lote, ci sawh loin kine thei a, aktui da kang in limna nei ahi hiam?
“Ka ngetna ngah thei hi leng a, Pasian in ka deihna hong piading hileh
Pasian in kei hong sucip henla, a khut zanin kei hong that vet leh!
Ka thuak lai nadingin bang hatna nei nawn a, lungduai a ka om nadingin lametding bang om nawn ahi hiam?
Ka thahatna suang bang hi a, ka pumpi in sumngo tha paii ahi hiam?
Kei le kei' sung panin huhna bangci ngahtawm theihding ka hi hiam? Kei hong kihuhnading ka ngetnading kuamah om lo hi.
No ka lawmte pen, lui tuikhang bang, a mangthang pak tui let bang,
nin a khalhnelh vuk le tuikhal bangin na zuautat uh hi.
Khua a lum ciangin tuate tui mangthang a, ni a sat ciangin a kang hi.

ka galte' kiang panin hong honkhia un, kei a hong nengniamte' khutsung panin hong tankhia un,' hong ci ngei zenzen ka hi hiam?
“Hong hilh thei le-uhcin, pau loin ka ompahding hi. Ka khialhna hong theitelsak dih un.
Lungsim takpi tawh thugennate heh loin kisang thei a, ahi zongin no hong taiina in bang phatuamsak ahi hiam?
Kamging mawkmawk lelte heh taak sa a, huih' letmang cihmawh kamte thupi ngaihsut na hi uh hiam?
Mi cimawh khat suksiatgawp sawm a, na lawm khat uh hihgawp sawm na hi uh hiam?
Tu in kong thum hi; kihei unla kei hong en un. Na maitang uhah zuau a gen dingin kilawm ka hi hiam?
“Leitungah mihing in nasep haksa nei a, ama hun pen nasempa-a' bang hi lo ahi hiam?
Sila nasemte in niliim lunggulhin nasempa in a thaman a ngak tawh kibang hi lo ahi hiam?
Meiilum kaite bei in a manthan bangin Leinuai a paisukpa mangthangding hi.
“Kei a hongcingding na koih nadingin kei, tuipi ganhing hong sa na hi hiam?
Lum leng nuamding a, ihmu leng phatuamding hi, ci leng lah,
a lauhuai mang nong mansak a, a lauhuai maangmuhna tawh nong lausak hi.
“Nang in hih zahin na thupi ngaihsut dingin na lungsimah na ngaihsut dingin
zingsang simin gim a pia dingin ama kiangah pai in amah na ze-et themthum nadingin mihing bang hi lel ahi hiam?
Tomkha sung beek hong pelh loding a, ka hu beek hong sangsak man loding na hi hiam?
Mihingte a encikpa aw, a khial ka hih leh zong nangma tungah bang gamta khial ka hi hiam? Bang hangin kei hong ngim a, bang hangin nangma muitum suak zenzen ka hi hiam?
Bang hangin ka khialhna hong maisak lo a, ka mawhna hong maisak lo na hi hiam? Tu in han sungah ka lumding a, nong zonzon hangin ka na om nawn keiding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Shuah gammi Bildad in dawng a,
“Tua bang thu bang tanvei gengending a, bang tanvei paupauding na hi hiam?

Na tate ama tungah khial a, amau' mawhnate amaute a tuaksak ahi hi.
A hun lai in Pasian zong inla, Vanglianpa' hehpihnading thuum lecin,
Tua hileh, na zawn' mahmah khit hangin a tawpnaah na hau kikding hi.
“Khangluite' thu kantel inla, pute pate' tuahsa thute ngaihsun pha in.
Amaute'n nang hong hilhin, a thu hong genin, amau' phawksa thute hong gending hi lo ahi hiam?
“Ciknawng om lohnaah laiphai kung po thei ahi hiam? Tui om lohnaah pumpeeng pung thei ahi hiam?
Ahi zongin suangtum lakah a zung a kivialgawp, suangtawphah a phukha zung a suak hi.
Hih bang danin ama nuntakna bei a, lei sung panin kung dangte hong pokhia hi.
Nang hong mudahte in maizumna ngahding uh a, migilote' puanbuk maimangding hi,” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Job in Pasian dawng a,
“Kuamah in Pasian a zawhzawh lohna a teltakin ka theita hi.
Amah pil mahmah a, vanglian mahmah hi. Kua'n khauhtakin nial a, nial paisuakzo ahi hiam?
Pasian in mualte lingsak a, tawlngasak lo hi. Ama hehna tawh mualte a lumlet hi.
Amah'n leitung lokgawp a, a khuampite kiling hi.
Amah'n ni a suak lo dingin thu pia a, aksite sincip hi.
Amah bek in vanpi zal a, tuipi tuihualte tuancil hi.
Amah pen vana a om Khawlei-uikai, Zawlzawng, Seguk, le Khanglam aksite a bawlpa ahi hi.
Amah'n lakhia nuam leh a khaktanzoding kua om ahi hiam? Bang hih na hi hiam, kua'n ci theiding ahi hiam?
Tua ahih ciangin keimah in bangci dawn theihding a, amah ka nialnading kammal bangci muhding ka hi hiam?
Ka hu nangawn hong sangsak man lo a, lungkhamna tawh kei hong kidimsak hi.
Thatanghat thuding hileh, amah hat mahmah a, thutang kituh hi leng, kua in thukhen zumah amah samzoding ahi hiam?
Migilote' khut sungah leitung kipia a, amah in thukhen mangte' mit a tuncipsak hi - amah hikeileh kua hiding ahi hiam?
“Laitaite sangin ka hun nawhtai zaw a, beipak ahih manin nopna ngah kha lo hi.
Pumpeeng gunkuang bangin ka hun nawhpai a, muvanlai sa bawh bangin a nawhlen' hi.
Ka dahnate kimangngilh bawlin kimaitaisakding ci taleng zong,
Kei a mawhin hong kiseh veveding ahihleh bang hangin a mawkna in na semding ka hi hiam?
Satpiang tawh kei kisilin, vuttui tawh ka khut sawp taleng,
Na khut tawh na sepsate simmawh bawlin, migilote' vai panpihin, hih bangin nong netniamnaah bang phattuamna ngah na hi hiam?
Mihing bang lelin gamta na hi hiam?
Na nuntak hun tan kote' nuntak tan bang lelin ngaihsun na hi hiam?
Bang hangin ka mawhna hong sulzuihin, ka khialhna khempeuh hong kantel na hi hiam?
Leivui pana kei nong bawlna hong phawkkik in. Leivui mahin hong dengvui kik takpiding na hi hiam?
“Pasian aw, bang hangin ka nu' sung panin kei hong piangsak peuhmah na hi hiam? Kuama hong muh ma in a si hizaw hoh leng!
Keima nuntakna bei dektakta hi lo ahi hiam? Hong hici omsak hoh in! Ka hun neih laisun teng nuam takin hong zangsak in.
Tua ciangin Naamah gammi Zofar in dawng a,
“Kampau hih zahta hong kidawng loding sa a, kam tam pauna hangin thumanin hong kiseh dingin ngaihsun na hi hiam?
Job aw, na thugente hong dawng thei lo dingin hong ngaihsun na hi hiam? Na simmawh kampaute hong kidawng mawh dingin ngaihsun na hi hiam?
Pasian in na thugente hong dawngkik le ut mahmah ing!
“Pasian' thuthuk thei khinzoding na hi hiam? Vanglianpa' hih theihna thei khinzoding na hi hiam?
Pasian' liatna pen leitung sangin golzaw a, tuipi sangin zaizaw hi.
Pasian in nang hong manin thu hong sit leh amah a khaktanding kua om ahi hiam?
Pasian in mi hoih lote thei takpi hi. Mawhna a muh ciangin thudon loding ahi hiam?
Gamlak a om late mihing suak ngeiding a, mihaite pil ngeiding ahi hiam?
“Job aw, na lungsim a hoihin bawl inla, Pasian' lamah kihei in.
Khialhna na bawl khak leh paaikhia inla, na inn sungah gitlohna omsak kei in.
Na lungkhamnate vengding a, tuikhang pak bangin na phawk nawn keiding hi.
Ahi zongin note zah mahin kei zong thu ka thei a, midangte sangin na theihzawk uh bang om tuan ahi hiam?
Note'n lungkhamna bangmah na nei kei uh a, kei na hong ciamnuih bawl gawpgawp uh hi. A puk dektak mipa na satgawp uh hi.
Guta mite nuamtakin om hithiat uh a, Pasian a simmawhte nuamtakin nungta uh hi.
Pasian' khut in amaute a bawlna thu a vekpi-un thei kim uh hi lo ahi hiam?
Leii in an a ciap mah bangin, bil in ngai thei hi lo ahi hiam?
“Khanghamte in pilna nei a, nuntak saute in thu theitel uh hi.
Pasian in pilna le vang nei a, amah thukipin thu a theitel hi.
Amah'n mipilte' pilna susia in, makaite pen mihai bangin gamtasak hi.
Amah'n kumpite zakiasak a, thongah a khia hi.
Siampite mihai suaksak a, mi vangliante lawnthal hi.
Amah'n mi' muante a pau thei loin bawl a, khanghamte' pilna a paihkhiatsak hi.
Amah'n mi vangliante mindaisak a, mi thupite' kihihsakna a beisak hi.
Amah'n khuamial sung panin thuthukte kalkhia a, a kithei zo lo thute kitelsak hi.
Amah'n minamte thahatsakin liansak a, ahi zongin amah in tuate zogawpin susia hi.
Amah'n minam makaite a pilna uh paihkhiatsak a, lampi om lohna gamlakah vakvaisak hi.
Khuamial lakah amaute in mialzawt uh a, zukham bangin amaute hoihoi uh hi.
Note' theih khempeuh, kei zong ka thei hi. Note khempeuh sangin ka neuzaw tuan het kei hi.
Note'n na haina uh zuauthu tawh na melh uh a, kuamah a damsak zo lo zato siam-a kinei mite tawh na kibang uh hi.
Pau hetloin om hi le-uhcin, mipil mah hong kisazawding hi.
“Tu in ka thugen hong ngai unla, ka gen laitakin limtak ngai un.
Pasian' min dingin thuman lo genin, ama a dingin zuauthu gensakding na hi uh hiam?
Pasian angvanding a, ama ading gensakding na hi uh hiam?
Pasian in limtakin note hong entel leh note' sungah hoihna muding ahi hiam? Mihingte na khem bangun Pasian a khem thei dingin kingaihsun na hi uh hiam?
A simthamin angvanna na zat uhleh amah in note hong taii taktakding hi.
Ama vangliatna in note hong lausakding a, note tungah amah kihtakna hong tungding hi lo ahi hiam?
“Ka nuntakna pia ngamin, ka nuntakna ka ap ngam hi.
Ka thugente limtak ngai unla, ka lahtelnate na za un.
“Pasian aw, keimah hong mawhsakding na hi hiam? Nong mawhsak leh pau hetloin a si dingin ka kiging hi.
Ka mawhna ka khialhna bangzah pha ahi hiam? Ka mawh ka khialhna teng hong theisak in.
“Bang hangin kei hong peel a, gal bangin hong ngaihsun na hi hiam?
Bang hangin keimah lausakding hanciam na hi hiam? Kei, singteh bang lel hi lo ka hi hiam? Anvai themkhat galin doding na hi hiam?
“Mihingte a nuntak hun tom mahmah a, lungkhamna tawh kidim hi.
Amaute paak bangin khangin keu pak uh a, niliim bangin pai hanhanin, mangthang uh hi.
Pasian aw, tua bang lel mi kei hong en a, thukhenna a thuak dingin na maiah hong sam na hi hiam?
Mihing banga a ninte sung panin a siang hong piang loding hi.
Amah en loin tuaci omsak mai inla, a nuntak haksapi mah zomzomsak hoh in.
Lei sungah a zungte teek a, a bulsum a si zongin,
guahtui ngahin, singkungno in hong selkik hi.
Ahi zongin mi si a, amah maimang pah hi. Amah a beina tungta a, koiah om nawn ahi hiam?
“Gun tuite le tuipi tuite a kan' hun om theiding hi.
Tua ciangin Teman khuami Elifaz in Job dawng a,
“Job aw, mawk paupau kei in! Nang' pau bangin mipilte pau ngei lo a,
Ahi zongin nangmah in Pasian zahtakna na beisak a, ama maiah thugennading na khaktan hi.
“Mihing aa piang lakah a masa pen kisa na hi hiam? Pasian in mualte a bawl lai in a piang khin kisa na hi hiam?
Pasian' vaihawmnate a za simin kingaihsun na hiam? Nang bek in pilna khempeuh a nei in kingaihsun na hi hiam?
Ko' theih loh thu bang thei tuan na hi hiam? Ko' muh loh thu bang mu tuan na hi hiam?
“Pasian in nang hong hehnem hi; bang hangin nialnial na hi hiam? Kam khum kam nem tawh Pasian' tangin nang tungah thu kong gen uh hi.
Ahih hangin na lung khauhin kote nong heh et hi.
Pasian' tungah a heh na hi a, amah a simmawh na hi hi.
“Mihing aa piang peuhmah paubaang hetloin siangtho taktak zoding ahi hiam? Pasian' tungah a thumanzo kua omding ahi hiam?
Pasian in a siangtho vantung mite nangawn muang lo ahihleh, ei mawhnei mite bang hangin hong muang mahding ahi hiam?
“Job aw, ka thutheihte na ngai in.
“Mi a nengniam migilopa in a khan tawntungin lungkhamna thuakding hi.
Launading awging a bilah za ngitngetding a, lungmuangin a om laitakin gutate in buluhding hi.
“A thatang muanhuai in a pumpi a liat hangin
ama tenna khuapi sia in, ama inn kinusiading a, a sawt loin ninbulomtang suakding hi.
Amah sauvei hau loding a, a neihsate kip loding hi. Ama liim nangawn maimangding a,
Amah'n gitlohna suanin nei ahih manin, gitlohna bek mah ngahkikding hi.
“Tua bang thute ka zaza khin a, no' hehnepna pen gimnading bek ahi hi.
Khawl hun nei loin gengen laiding na hi uh hiam? Na gending uh omom lai ahi hiam?
Note le keimah a kikhek thei hi lehang, note' gen khempeuh kei zong ka gen theiding hi. Note ka lu hong peisanin thu tampi tak mah ka hong gen theiding hi.
Pasian aw, kei nong paatsak ngingei a, ka innkuan khempeuh na sisakmang khin hi.
Mite'n kei hong zahko uh a, ka paang a beeng dingin hong kikhawmtuah uh hi.
Pasian in migilote' khut sungah kei hong pia hi.
“Kei thumin puanhampi ka silh a, guallelin leivui lakah ka om hi.
Kei a dingin adingding, a hong panpihding mi khat vantungah om hi.
Pasian aw, kei hong hu in. Ka thugente hong panpihding kuamah dang om lo hi.
Ka dahna hangin ka mit mial a, ka khut ka khete ciangkang bangta hi.
Mihoihin a kineite in lamdang hong sa uh a, migiloin kei hong seh uh hi.
Mite' zahtaka a kinei mite in amau' ngaihsutna uh man mahmah sa semsem uh hi.
“Ka hun beita hi. Ka geelna teng maimang a, ka lametna teng beita hi.
Kei' lametding misite' gam bek omlai a, tua khuamial sungah lumin ka ihmuding hi.
Kei' lametding tua laiah bang om ahi hiam? Tua laiah ka lametding bang nong muhsak uh hiam?
“Job aw, khawl hun nei thei loding na hi hiam? Hong khawl phot lecin, thu kong gen theiding uh hi.
Bang hangin bawng bang lelin kote hong ngaihsun a, mihaipi in kote hong seh na hi hiam?
Na hehna tawh nangmah a kigimsak bek na hi hi. Nangma hangin leitung kinusiading a, mualte a kinkhia dingin ngaihsun na hi hiam?
“Migilo pa' meivak kisumitding a, cikmah hunin kuangkik nawn loding hi.
Ama buk sungah a meivak mitding a, ama inn sungah khua a mialding hi.
Thangsiahna ngen sungah amah bungbu tuk a, gum sungah amah kia hi.
Thangah a khetulin awk a, thangkhau in amah gakcip hi.
Amah siahna in leilakah khauzak kitung a, a pai nading lampiah thang kisiah hi.
Lauhuaina in amah pang a, a kalsuanna khempeuh a sulzuih hi.
Lei sunga ama zungte keu in, a tunga a hiangte a sita hi.
Inn le gamah ama minthanna beita a, kuamah in amah phawkkha nawn lo hi.
A nungtate' gam panin amah kihawlkhiading a, khuavakna mun panin khuamialnaah kihawlkhiading hi.
Amah'n suanlekhak nei lo a, ama tennasa munah ama gui a zomding om lo hi.
Nisuahna pan nitumna dong ama thuakna a za peuhmah kigaihin a ling uh hi.
Migilote, Pasian a ngaihsun lote a thutawpna uh tu-a bang ahi hi,” a ci hi.
“Bang tanvei thu genin hong gimsakding na hi hiam?
A khial takpi hi taleng zong nang' lainatnading bang om ahi hiam?
Hih thu hong piangsakpa Pasian ahihlam mu thei lo na hi hiam? Kei hong mat nadingin amah in thang hong siah hi.
Amah'n ka hauhna khempeuh hong lakkhiatsak a, ka min hoih kimlai hong siasak hi.
“Pasian in ka sanggamte hong taisansak a, kei hong theisate kiangah khualmi ka suak hi.
Ka behte le ka lawmte beimang khinta uh hi.
Hong hehpih un! Hong hehpih un! Keima lawmte hi lo na hi uh hiam? Pasian in kei hong satpaita hi.
Pasian' hong bawlsiat bangin bang hangin no zong kei hong bawlsiading na hi uh hiam? Nong gimsakna uh kicingta hoh hi lo ahi hiam?
Bang hang hiam cih leh, ‘Amah bangci gimsak theiding ihi hiam?' na ci uh hi. Kei nong suktheih nadingun paulap khatpeuh na zong uh hi.
“Job aw, ka heh nong suaksak a, ka ki-ipzo nawn kei hi.
Tanglai pek a kipan, leitung mi a om cil a kipanin,
migilote' nopsak hun a tom mahmahna thu, Pasian a don lote' lungdam hun a tom mahmahna thu thei lo na hi hiam?
leivui them bangin maimang veve lelding hi. Amah a thei ngei mite in, ‘Amah koiah omta ahi hiam?' ci in lamdangsading uh hi.
Ama tenna ngei mun panin amah maimangding a,
mizawngte' na a suhsakte, a tate in lohsakding uh hi.
Amah'n bawngnawi le khuaizu gun tui bangin a luang mukha loding hi.
Amah'n a nasep thamante nusiading a, a hauhna khempeuh zangkha man loding hi.
“A huaihamna bei ngei lo a, a duh khempeuh siit nei lo hi.
A cihtheih pen hun laitakin lungkhamna lianpen a tuak hi.
Amah'n a duhduh ne mai hen! Pasian in hehna tawh amah gim pia ngawnding hi.
Amah'n namsau pelhin a tainaah sumngo thal in kaptukding hi.
Pasian' hehna hangin ama hauhna khempeuh a kisusiamangding ahi hi.
“Kei' kitotpih pen mihing hi lo hi. Bang hangin lungtom loding ka hi hiam?
Kei hong en dih un. Lamdangsak taak hi lo ka hi hiam?
Keima tunga thupiang ka ngaihsut ciangin lamdangsa mahmahin lau in ka ling hi.
“Bang hangin Pasian in migilote khantosak a, hausakin liansak ahi hiam?
A bawngte uh pung a, tatolh cih om ngei lo hi.
Tuuno bangin a naupangte uh taikhia in kimawl uh a,
tamngai le harp lasakna aw tawh a kituakin a lam uh hi.
“Migilo pa' meivak kisukmitsak ngei ahi hiam? Amaute khat beek in lungkhamna tuak ngei ahi uh hiam? Pasian in hehna tawh migilote gim pia ngei ahi hiam?
Huih in a letkhiat buhkungte, le huihpi in a mutkhiat buhsi bangin amaute bawl ngei ahi hiam?
Mawhneite amau' mawhna hangin gimna thuaksak henla, Vanglianpa' hehna theisak tahen.
Mi khat a nuntakna a bei khit ciangin, a naupangte' nopsakna phawk thei nawn ahi hiam?
Mi khat in Pasian' tungah thu hilh theiding ahi hiam? Vanglianpa tungah thu khen theiding ahi hiam?
“Mi pawlkhatte a cithei mahmahin si a, lungmuang tak le lungnuam takin om uh a,
annek tuidawn a kicingin a nei uh hi.
Mi pawlkhatte ahihleh nopsak cih theikha ngei loin lunggimin a si uh hi.
Siatna a gamta, mi lianpa' inn, koiah omta ahi hiam, na ci uh hi.
“Khualzinzin mite tawh kiho ngei lo na hi uh hiam? Amaute' thugente, thei lo na hi uh hiam?
Pasian hehin, mite gim a piak ciangin migilote peng tawntung zawsop hi.
Migilopa a gamtatna bangin a thukkikding, migilopa mawhsakin a langpangding kuamah om lo hi.
Migilopa a kivui ciangin a hankhuk kicing a,
mi tul tampi in amah kha in hoihtakin lei tawh kivuk hi.
Tua ciangin Teman khuami Elifaz in dawng a,
Na mawhna a tamna hang, na gitlohna a liatna hang hizaw hi.
Na sanggampa' leiba tangin a silhding sitsak loin a puan teng na laksak hi.
Na vangliatna le na za liatna zangin, gam khempeuh nala khin hi.
Ahi zongin nangmah in, ‘Pasian in bang theiding ahi hiam? Meii in Pasian tuamcip hi. Eite' thu bangci in khentheiding ahi hiam?' na ci hi.
“Migilote' gamtat ngeite mah gamtatding ngaihsun na hi hiam?
Amau' hun tung lopi in tuikhang in amaute taai hi.
Ama hong hilhnate zui inla, ama thute ciamteh in.
Lungsim tak tawh Vanglianpa lamah kihei inla, na innsung pan gamtatsia beisak inla,
na kham neihte leivui bang lelin ngaihsunin, na Ofir khamte suang bang lelin ngaihsunin,
Vanglian Pasian pen na kham le na ngun hisak lecin,
Pasian muanin na nei tawntungding a, na lungdamna bulpi amah ahihlam na theiding hi.
Thu na nget ciangin na ngetna hong piading a, nangma thuciamnate na tungsakding hi.
Na hih khempeuh na tangtunding a, na maa hong vangding hi.
Pasian in mi kiphasakte niamkhiat a, mi niamte a hon hi.
Amah ka zon danding thei in, ama kiang ka tunnading zia a thei hi leng,
Ama hong gending thute le kei a hong dawnnading thute ka thei nuam hi.
Pasian in a thaneih khempeuh tawh keima langkhatah hong pangding ahi hiam? Hong langpan loding a, ka thugen hong ngaiding hi.
Ama hong lamlahna citakin ka zui cinten a, lam ka pial ngei kei hi.
Vanglian Pasian in ka lungsim hanna hong mangsak hi.
“Pasian in bang hangin a thukhen niding seh lo a, ama nasemte thutang ahihna a lah niding seh lo ahi hiam?
Zanin puan silhloin lum uh a, khuadampi lakah silhding nei loin om uh hi.
Pasian in a lungnuamin amah nungtasak a, ahi zongin Pasian in amah encik tawntung hi.
Hih thu kua in nialzoding na hi uh hiam? Ka thugennate man lo hi, ci in kei langah hong pangin ka thugente hong selzoding kua om na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
Ama na a sem vantung mite bangzah pha cih kua in simzoding ahi hiam? Pasian' khuavak in a bat lohna koi lai mun om ahi hiam?
Pasian' muhnaah kua dikzoding a, siangthozoding ahi hiam?
Tua ahihleh, lungno, ganhing no ahi lel mihing pen bangciding ahi hiam? Mihing in Pasian' muhnaah bang man lel ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
“A hehpihhuai kei nong huhna, a thazawngkhal kei nong hotna, hih bang ahi hiam?
Kei bang mihai tungah thu manpha nong gen a, pilna thu tampi nong pulak hi.
Tua bang thu a gen dingin kua in hong sawl a, kua' lungsim hong pulakkhia na hi hiam?
“Misite' gam kiling a, a sunga a teng mite launa tawh a ling hi.
Amah'n meiilom lakah tuite khol a, tua a gik mahmah tui meii a puazosak hi.
Amah'n kha a liahding bawl a, meii tawh kha a khuh hi.
Amah'n muh tawpnaah git dinden a, khuavak le khuamial a khen hi.
Ama thahatna tawh tuipi zo a, ama siamna tawh tui ganhing golpi Rahab thatlum hi.
Hihte pen ama vangliatna themkhat bek hi pan a, i zak thute pen a hemlam bek hi pan hi. Pasian a liatna taktak kua'n theizoding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
Tua ciangin Job in thu genkik a,
ka sungah nuntakna a omlaiteng, Pasian' hu, ka nakah ka diik laiteng,
Note a thuman hi, kong ci ngei keiding a, ka nuntak laiteng, kei a thuman hi'ng, ka cihna thu ka khia ngei keiding hi.
Pasian in amaute' nuntakna a laksak hun ciangin, migilote a dingin lametna om nawn ahi hiam?
Lungkhamna a thuak uh ciangin Pasian in amau' kikona awging ngaiding ahi hiam?
Ahi zongin tuate khempeuh na theih khitsa uh ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin bang hangin mawk pau na hi uh hiam?
“Vanglian Pasian in migilote, mi ngongtatte, gim a piakzia hih bang ahi hi.
Lauhuaina in tuikhang pak bangin nawkgawpding a, zan ciangin huihpi in amaute mutkhiamangding hi.
Nisuahna huihpi in amaute leenkhia in a inn panun gamlapiah leenkhiading hi.
Amaute a suahtak theih nading a hanciam tantan kimlai mah, hehpih ngaihsut hetloin leenkhiamangding hi.
Amaute a tai laitakun huih in nawk gawpin, a susiagawp dingin mutkhiagawpding hi.
Suangte a tawhvang uh ciangin suangmanphate a mu uh hi.
Ahi zongin koi laiah pilna kimuding ahi hiam? Koi laiah thutheihna nak om ahi hiam?
“Tua ahihleh koi lai panin pilna hong piang ahi hiam? Thutheihna koi laiah om ahi hiam?
Sihna le siatna nangawn in a thu hemzak bek ung, ci lai uh hi.
Pasian in huih a gikding zah bawlin, tuipi a liatnading zah a seh laitak,
Tua ciangin Job in a thu genkik a,
Khuasung upate a kikhop uh ciangin a kikhawm dingin kei ka pai ciangin
Migilote' gitlohna khempeuh ka susia gawpmang a, amau' sukgawp mi khempeuh ka honkhia hi.
Mi khempeuh in kei hong phat tawntung uh a, ka tha a hat tawntung hi.
Amaute zawng mahmahin gilkial uh ahih manin gamlak singzung keu peuh teep lelding uh hi.
Gutate otkhai in a kidelh khiat bangin mite lak panin amaute kihawlkhia hi.
Ganhing bangin gamlakah amaute ham uh a, sawlkawm nuaiah kilomin a omkhawm uh hi.
Kei ka bukna leihawmah amaute hong tuaksuk uh a, kei hong sucipsuk uh hi.
Launa tawh ka kidim a, ka cihtheihna khempeuh meii bangin a thengta hi.
Pasian in ka puan ngawng pan kei hong manin ka puan tawh hong heekcip hi.
Buannawng ciim sungah kei hong lawnkhia a, ninbulom bang lel ka hita hi.
Kei tungah nong gilo mahmah a, nong hih theih zahin kei na hong bawlsia hi.
Na hehpihding a hong thumding cih lohbuang, bangmah dang a hih thei nawn lo misia pa, bang hangin sugawp na hi hiam?
A lungkham mite tawh kei kap khawmin, a cimawh mite dahpih hi lo ka hi hiam?
Lungdamna le khuavakna ka lamet laitakin, lungkhamna le khuamialna hong tung zawsop hi.
Lungkham sinkhamin ka om a, mihon lakah dingin huhna ka ngen hi.
Ka vun vomin dulhkhia a, ka pumtangin ka ci sa gawp hi.
“Lunggulhna tawh nungak khatpeuh ka et ngei loh nading, kiciamna ka bawlkhin hi.
Vanglian Pasian in eite bang hong cih a, mihingte' gamtatna bangci thuhkik ahi hiam?
A man loin a gamtate tungah siatna le gimna a tungsak hi.
Pasian in ka gamtatna khempeuh thei a, ka kalsuanna khempeuh a hong mu hi.
Pasian in tawikhaina manah hong tawikhai hen; ka paubaan hetlohna hong muding hi.
ka khawhsa ante midangte' nek suak henla, ka an neih khempeuh maimang tahen.
“Ka vengte' zi zawlmitin, a kong geiah ngakin ka buk taak leh
ka it ka zi in midangte' an suksak henla, midangte' angah lum tahen.
(Tua bang mawhna pen a siahuai hi a, sihna a thuakding ahi hi.
Ka neih khempeuh a kangtum thei mei husia tawh a kibang ahi hi.)
Tuaci kei leng, Pasian' mai mu ngamding ka hi hiam? Keima thu a khen dingin Pasian hong pai ciangin bang gen mawkding ka hi hiam?
Kei a hong piangsak Pasian mah in keima nasemte zong a piangsak ahi hi.
“Mizawngte ka huhding ka mangngilh ngei kei a, meigong numeite ka guaksuaksak ngei kei hi.
Keimah in an ne napi in, tagahte a gilkialin ka koihkhong ngei kei hi.
Ka khang tawntungin tua bangte ka en tawntung hi.
“Mi a cimawh, puan silhding a lei zo lo, a zawng lua ka muh ciangin,
“Zum thukhennaah zo-na ning cih ngaihsutna tawh tagah khatpeuh ka khem taak leh,
ka khutte buisum henla, ka liang bul panin kilongkhia tahen.
Pasian' gimpiakding kihta ka hih manin, tua bang peuhmah ka gamta ngei keiding hi.
“Leitung hauhna muan le suanin ka nei ngei kei a,
ka hauhna zong ka kisaktheihpih ngei kei hi.
A sihding uh deihna tawh ka samsia ngei kei hi.
“Ka thugente kuamah in na ngai loding ahi hiam? Ka gen thu khempeuh man hi, ci in ka kiciam hi. Vanglian Pasian in kei hong dawng tahen. “Ka langte in kei hong mawhsakna thute ka tawi theih dingin lai sungah a kigelh hileh
No a khangham zawte in thu a gending kilawm hi, ci in ka ngaihsun hi.
Khanghamna in mi pilsak lo a, thuman zong theisak tuan lo hi.
Bang hangin pilna a nei in kigen theiding na hi uh hiam? Note'n lel na hih manun Pasian in Job dawngding hi.
Amaute pau loin a om ciangun kei zong pau loin ngak lailaiding ka hi hiam? Amaute'n a gending uh thei nawn loin ommawk uh hi.
Tu petpetin kei zong nang kong dawngding a, keima ngaihsutnate ka hong pulakding hi.
Ka thuakzo nawnkei a, ka genkhia tading hi.
Hih ka thugennaah kuamah ka pawlpih keiding a, kuamah phattuam ka nei keiding hi.
“Job aw, tu in ka thugen khempeuh limtakin hong ngai in.
Ka lungsim sunga om thute a hong gending ka hi hi.
“Na hong dawn theih leh limtakin hong dawng in. Na hong seelnading limtakin kiging in.
“Keima zakin thu na gen khin a, na thugente ka za khin hi.
Pasian in kei hong suknading thu zongzong a, gal bangin kei hong bawl hi.
“Ahih hangin, Job aw, nangmah na khialzaw hi. Pasian pen mihing sangin lianzaw hi.
Pasian in mihingte' phunna thudon ngei lo hi, ci in thugenna tawh bang hangin Pasian mawhsak na hi hiam?
Zanin mite a ihmut ciangin, mang le maangmuhna sungah Pasian in thu a gen hi.
Pasian in thu hong gen a, ama hilhkholhna hangin mite lau mahmah uh hi.
Pasian in mihingte siatna thuaksak lo a, sih nading panin amaute a honkhia hi.
Pasian in cinatsakna tawh mihingte thuhilh a, a pumpi khempeuh natna tawh a kidimsak hi.
A ci a sa khempeuh kiam a, a guh guak bekin a om hi.
A beinading a nai hita a, misi gam a zuanding hita hi.
Tua ciangin ama pumpi khangnosuak kikin, a thahat pen hun laitak a bangkikding hi.
Pasian in hih thute khempeuh mihingte tungah hong hihkik zelzel a,
sih nading panin honkhia kik zelin nuntak nuam a pia kik hi.
Tua ciangin Elihu in,
Thuman bang hiam cih tengkhia ni. Thuhoih bang hiam cih mukhia ni.
“Hih Job tawh a kibang mi na mu ngei uh hiam? Amah'n Pasian zahtakna lim bangmah nei het lo hi.
Amah'n migilote tawh kikholh nuam sa mahmah a, mawhnei mite tawh a vak kawikawi hi.
“Ahi zongin thu ngaihsun thei a kinei note khempeuh in ka thugenna hong ngai un. Pasian a giloin gamta ngeiding a, Vanglianpa in a man loin sem ngeiding ahi hiam?
Pasian in ama vangliatna mi khatpeuh tung panin a ngah ahi hiam? Leitung khempeuh a uk dingin mi khatpeuh in amah a koih ahi hiam?
Pasian in ama ngaihsutna kheel henla, nuntakna hu a dokkik hileh
nuntakna a nei khempeuh si pahding uh a, mihing khempeuh leivui suakkikding uh hi.
“Job aw, mipil-a kinei na hih leh ka thugente hong ngai in.
Vanglianpa in thutang a deih lo dingin ngaihsun na hi hiam? Nang in a thuman Pasian mawhsak na hi hiam?
Gamtatsia mite a buk theih nadingun a seelcipzoding, khuamial khuazing koimahah om lo hi.
Pasian' maiah mihingte in thukhenna a thuak niding, a kiseh hun omtuam lo hi.
Pasian in mi khempeuh' muhin mawhneite gim a pia hi.
Amaute'n mizawngte kapsak gawp uh a, mizawngte' huh ngetna awging Pasian in a za hi.
Migilote hong uksak taleh zong, tua panin suahtaknading kuamah in vaihawm zo loding hi.
“Job aw, Pasian' tungah na khialhnate pulakin na khialh nawn loh nading thu ciam nai lo na hi hiam?
Pasian in na khialhnate a hong lahnading ngenin, na gamtatsiat nawn loh nading ut nai na hi hiam?
Pasian nial na hih manin amah in nangma utna a bang hangin hong hihsakding ahi hiam? Hih thu pen kei' ngaihsutding hi loin, nangma khensatding ahi hi. Tu in nangma ngaihsutna a kician takin hong gen in.
Job' thugente khempeuh ngaihsun le-uhcin, migilo bangin a kampauna na theiding uh hi.
Tua ciangin Elihu mah in,
“Job aw, Pasian' muhnaah ka paubaang kei hi, na cihding kilawm lo hi.
Pasian kiangah, ka khialh hangin bang phamawh sa na hi hiam? Khialhna ka gamtat loh manin bangmah phattuamna ka ngah kei hi, na cihding kilawm lo hi.
Nang le na lawmte tungah thu ka hong gending hi.
“Vantung ento dih un. Meiite bangzah takin sang omto ahi hiam?
Mawhna na gamtat manin, Pasian bangmah sukha lo hi. Tampi tak khial talecin zong amah sukha tuan ahi hiam?
Na thumanna hangin Pasian in phattuamna ngah ahi hiam? Pasian in nang kiang panin bangmah deih lo hi.
Lungzin' hun laitakin thahatna a pia, amaute a Piangsak Pasian' lam nga lo uh hi.
Amaute migilo mi kihisakte ahih manun, huhding a nget hangun Pasian in pia lo hi.
Elihu in a thugen zomlai a,
“Lungduai takin tawmkhat hong ngailai in. Pasian' tangin ka gending thu pawlkhat omlai hi.
Ahi zongin mite sikkol kibulh a, a gamtatnasate hangin gimna a thuak uhleh,
Pasian in amau' mawhna le a kiphatsaknate uh a lakkhia ahi hi.
A gamtatsiatna panun a khawl nadingun amau' bil sungah thu a gengen hi.
Amaute khansih uh a, a zumhuaipi in a bei uh hi.
Ahi zongin tu in na ngah dinga kilawm gimna a thuakta na hi hi.
Sumgolh' khemsa in gamta kei inla, leitung nate' bawlin lam kipialsak kei in.
Mihingte a beimang hunding, zan khuamial hong tun hunding lunggulh kei in.
“Amah'n tuipi panin tuite lato a, tua a lak tuite guahtui in a bawl hi.
Amah'n meii sung panin guah piangsak a, mihing khempeuh a dingin guah a zusak hi.
Amah'n vantungah khua phiasak a, ahi zongin tuipi thuk sung a mialsak hi.
Amah'n tu-a bangin mihingte hong vak a, annekding tampi tak a hong pia ahi hi.
Amah'n keek thu pia a, a kap nop penpen a kha dingin a sawl hi.
“Hih huihpi in ka dip hong kuasak a, ka dip vana khai hong bangsak hi.
Ama kam panin a hong gingkhia hih vanging Pasian' pauna awging, limtakin ngai in.
Amah'n vanah khua phiasak a, leimong khat pan mong khat dong a taan hi.
Amah'n leitungah vuk a kia dingin sawl a, guah tampi tak a zusak hi.
Amah'n mihingte a nasep uh khawlsak a, amah a gamtang ahihna a kilangsak hi.
Gamsate in a lupna ngei delh uh a, a kua sungah bucip uh hi.
Leitaw lam panin guahpi hong zu a, leilu lam panin huihpi hong nung hi.
Pasian' husanna in tuite khalsak a, tui lianpite khalin sik bangin a sak hi.
Amah'n meiipi nomsak a, meiipi in khua a phiasak hi.
“Job aw, tawlkhat khawlin ngai inla, Pasian' bawlsa na lamdangte ngaihsun dih in.
Pasian in thu pia a, meii lak panin khua a phiatsak theihna na thei hiam?
Bangmah in a len lopi in vantungah meii a omsak theihna, a lamdang hih ama siamna na thei hiam?
Limlang bangin a sak mahmah van peekpi ama hih bangin zalzo na hi hiam?
Pasian tawh kiho theih nading ka ngen keiding hi. Kei hong suksiat nadingin kei kipiading ka hi hiam?
Tua ciangin huihpi lak panin Topa'n Job tungah thu hong gen a,
“Kei' pilna a nial dingin nang kua na hi hiam? Thu na theih lohlam a kilangsak na hi bek hi.
Kipasalsakin dingto inla, kong thudot dingte hong dawng in.
Leitung ka bawl laitakin nang om na hi hiam? Thei kisa na hih leh tua thu hong gen in.
Bangcia in golsakding cih kua in seh ahi hiam? Kua'n a golnading zah khau khai ahi hiam? Hihte khempeuh thei kisa na hi hiam?
Leitung a pua khuampite bang tungah kiphut ahi hiam? Kua'n leitung a bulpi phut ahi hiam?
“Lei sung panin tuipi hong suahkhiat laitakin, tua tuipi a khaktanding kongpi kua in na khak ahi hiam?
Meii tawh tuipi a tuamcip pa, khuamial tawh a vialcippa keimah ka hi hi.
Tuipi gamgiding ciamteh sakin, ama huangsungding bekah ka omsak hi.
Job aw, nangmah in, ‘Tuni in khua vak in,' ci in na nuntak sung tawntung thu pia ngei na hi hiam?
Zing khuavak in leitung a mongin manin, a kawma bu migilote a sinkhiatding, thu pia thei ngei na hi hiam?
Migilote a dingin sun khuavak taanglua a, siatna a gamtatnading uh a khamcip hi.
“Tuipi sungtawng tuinakah pai ngei na hi hiam? Tuipi nuai lei tam tungah lam pai ngei na hi hiam?
Misite' gam khuamial kongkhakpi, mi khatpeuh in nang hong lak ngei ahi hiam?
Leitung bangcia lianding cih na thei hiam? Hih thute thei na hih leh hong dawng in.
“Leitung khuavak hong kipatkhiatna mun ahi a, leitung khuamial hong kipatna mun ahi zongin, thei na hi hiam?
Nangmah in amau' omna mun ciang dong va thei a, tua ciang dongah va kha kik ngei na hi hiam?
“Vuk a kikoihna munah nang va lut ngei a, gial a kikhopna mun va mu ngei na hi hiam?
Tuate, lungkham hunading, gal om hun cianga dingin ka koihcing ahi hi.
Leitung nitaang a hong suahkhiatna mun ahi a, nisuahna huihpi hong kipatna mun ahi zongin, va tung ngei na hi hiam?
“Kua'n guahzuknading tui lampi bawlsak a, keek' lampiding sialsak ahi hiam?
Mihing om lohna mun leilakah, kua in guah zusak ahi hiam?
Lopate a po theih nadingin lei keu in a sak bekbakte kua in tui buak ahi hiam?
Guah inpa nei ahi hiam? Daitui inpa nei ahi hiam?
Kua' sung panin tuikhal hong piangkhia a, kua' sung panin vana vukte hong suak ahi hiam?
Tua tuite suang bangin sak a, tuipi tui teng khalcip hi.
“Vana om Seguk henkop thei a, Zawlzawng a kikhihna phel thei na hi hiam?
Ama hun hunin aksite lam lak thei a, Khawlei-uikai a pai nading lampi lak thei na hi hiam?
Vana om nate' zuihding ngeina bawlsak thei a, lei-a om nate' zuihding ngeina bawl thei na hi hiam?
“Vana om meiite in guah hong zuksaknading nangmah in sawl na hi hiam?
‘Khua phia in,' ci in thu pia lecin, ‘Nong sawl bangin phia ning,' hong ciding ahi hiam?
Nail gun a khanding a thei gun vapite kua in hilh a, guahzukding a thei akluite, kua in hilh ahi hiam?
Leivuite khalcipin, leitang a sak ciangin, meiite thu pia in vana tuibemte a hong dingin kua in pilna nei ahi hiam?
“Humpinelkai le a note leihawm sungah bu in, a kua sung uhah lumin ngakin a om laitakun, a anding uh zonsak thei a, a note' gilkialna vahsak thei na hi hiam?
Va-akte a gilkialin leng kawikawi in, a note in an duhin kei tungah hong nget ciangun, tua va-akte an a piapa kua ahi hiam?
“Sathakte a suah hunding thei ngei na hi hiam? Sakhite a suah laitakin nau va dom ngei na hi hiam?
Tuate a ni ciamtehin, a suah hunding uh thei na hi hiam?
A no suak dingin leiah a bawhsuk hun laitak thei na hi hiam?
A note gamlakah khangin, a nute kiang pan paikhia in ciahkik nawn lo uh hi.
“Kua'n gam-late tungah suahtakna pia ahi hiam? Kua'n khahin a ut utin vaksak ahi hiam?
“Gambawngtal in nangma na hong semding ahi hiam? Na ganbukah gambawngtal hong giak nuamding ahi hiam?
Nangmah in khauhual tawh khihzoding a, na loah na lokhawhna leeng kaisakzoding na hi hiam?
Nasem dingin a hat mahmah hangin, nangma na hong sepsak dingin lamen ngam na hi hiam?
Lo a na anpiangte hong kaihkhop sakin, na ancilnaah an hong khawm dingin um na hi hiam?
Ahi zongin a tai ciangin sakol sangin hatzaw hi.
“Job aw, sakolte a hatsakpa nang na hi hiam? Sakol zaangmul a posakpa nang na hi hiam?
Sakolte kauphe bangin diangsak thei in, mite' kihtak dingin phitsak thei na hi hiam?
Amaute' tungah a tuang mite' galhiam, lum le teite a tee zalzal hi.
“Simbung in a kha zalin leitaw lamah a leentheihnading nangma kiang panin hong sin ahi hiam?
Muvanlai in sang leenin mualtungah bu a tomnading nang' thupiakna hong ngak ahi hiam?
Suangpi dawnah bu bawl a, suangheeng kawmte phualpi in nei hi.
Tua lai mun panin khuadak kawikawi a, manin a nekding an a gal et hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n Job kiangah,
“Job aw, nangmah in Vanglian Pasian nong dem hi. Tu in khawlding na hiam, ahih kei leh keima thugen nong dawngding hiam?” a ci hi.
“ Topa aw, ka haipau kha hi. Hong bangci dawn theihding ka hi hiam? Tu a kipanin ka pau nawn keiding hi.
Tua ciangin huihpi sung panin Topa'n Job tungah thu genkik a,
“Kipasalsakin dingto inla, ka thudotnate hong dawng in.
Kei a thutang loin hong seh a, nang thutang kisa in kei hong mawhsak na hi hiam?
Kei zahin nang hat na hi hiam? Kei' awging zahin nang a' gingzoding ahi hiam?
A kiphasak mite en inla, na hehna tawh amaute niamkhiat gawp in.
Amaute khempeuh lei sungah phumcip inla, misite' gam sungah amaute khihcip in.
ahi zongin ama pum sungah bangzah hatna om a, bangzahta in a sazang khauh ahi hiam?
Ama guhte sumngo bangin khauh a, ama khete sikzawl bangin a khauh hi.
Gamsate omna mualtung panin ama anding lopa kipuak hi.
Amah lingkung nuaiah lum a, nawng sunga pumpeeng lakah a bu hi.
Lingkungte le lui gei-a gialhek kungte in ama ading niliim piangsak hi.
Kua'n ama mit tawsakin manzoding ahi hiam? Kua'n a nakphehah khau vawhzoding ahi hiam?
“Ngasa siahna sikkawi tawh Awle manzoding a, khauhual khat tawh a leii henzoding na hi hiam?
A nakphehah khau vawhzoding a, a khaguhah sikkawi bulhzoding na hiam?
Amah'n na khahnading hong thumding a, na hehpihnading hong ngending ahi hiam?
Na sila ahi tawntung dingin nangma tungah thu hong ciamding ahi hiam?
Na nasem numeite na mawlpih bangin mawlpihzoding a, vasa khawi bangin bawlzoding na hi hiam?
Ngasa bengte in lei dingin hong deekding a, sa zuakte in zuak dingin a sa semding ahi hiam?
Ngasa khawhna teipi tawh a vun khawhletzoding a, teipi lingnei tawh a lutang khawhletzoding na hi hiam?
“Awle a mu mi peuhmah lau in leiah a puk uh hi.
Awle a heh ciangin kihtakhuai mahmah a, ama omna maiah kuamah om ngam lo hi.
Leitung a om mihingte lakah Awle a suk manin a sihlawh lo kua om ahi hiam?
Kua'n ama puan tungnung hawkkhiatsak zo a, a sik puanpi sunletzo ahi hiam?
A kihtakhuai a hate a kam sungah om ahih manin, kua in ama kam phensak ngam ahi hiam?
Tua lipte khatlekhat kithuapcip bikbek ahih manin, khatlekhat kikalah huih nangawn thawl zo lo hi.
Tuate kinak mat lua ahih manin, bangmah in phelkhia zo lo hi.
A kam panin mei kuangkhia a, mei-ek leengkhia zaizai hi.
A nak panin meikhu suak a, selkeu khu tawh kibang hi.
Ama husanna in mei tawhkuang a, ama kam panin meikuang a suakkhia hi.
Ama a dingin sikte, buhkung bangin nip a, sumngote nangawn sing muatsa bang lel hi.
A khecinte, beelpei kitamte tawh kibang a, lam a pai ciangin leilak kuikek gawp hi.
A painasa khempeuhah tuihual om dandan a, tuipi phuansak pheuphau hi.
Tua ciangin Job in Topa dawng a,
Kei bangmah a thei lo kimlai, ‘Bang hangin ka pilna hong dem ngam na hi hiam?' na hong ci hi. Keimah in ka tel zawh loh thute, kei a dingin a lamdanglua thu a gengen ka hi hi.
Thu na gen laitakin ka na ngaihnading, na thugente kong dawnding, na hong gen hi.
Amah'n tapa sagih le tanu thum neikik a,
Tua khit ciangin a khankhinin a teeksihta hi.
Bang thu hangin minam dangte siatna dingah kithukhat sim uh a, mite in a mawkna dingpi in sawmsim uh ahi hiam?
Leitung kumpite le gam ukte in Topa le ama sathau nilhpa langpangin vaihawm uh a,
Vantunga a tupa in amaute na nuihsan a, tua Topa'n amaute a zahko hi.
Tua ciangin hehna tawh amau kiangah thu gending a, hehluat mahmahna tawh amaute linglawng sakin,
“Ka mual siangtho Zion tungah ka kumpi ka tusak khin hi,” ci hi.
Pasian in amah huh loding, mi tampi in hong ci uh hi.
Lumin ka ihmu a, Topa'n hong kem ahih manin ka thokik hi.
Gualzawhna pen Topa nangma hang ahi hi. Na mite tungah na thupha hong tungta hen!
Mite aw, ka minphatna in bang tanvei daina thuakding ahi hiam? Bang tanvei thumawkna deihin zuauthu zongding na hi uh hiam?
A man biakpiaknate lui unla, Topa muang un.
Topa aw, kong paunate hong ngai inla, ka hong thumnate hong thudon in.
Ka hingim mahmah hi. Topa aw, bang tanvei nang hong zekai laiding na hi hiam?
Bang hang hiam cih leh misite omna gam sungah nangmah phawk theih nading bangmah om lo ahih manin, Leinuai panin kua in nang hong phat theiding ahi hiam?
Topa'n keima thumna hong za khinzo a, Topa'n ka thungetna hong sangta hi.
Ka galte khempeuh zahhuai mahmahin gentheiding uh hi. Amaute nungkikin maizumna thuak pahding uh hi.
Topa ka Pasian aw, ka gamtat a siat a, ka khut a khialh leh,
bangmah thu om lopi in ka lawmte khemin, ka galte ka huh taak leh,
Nangma omna kiimah mite kikhawmsak inla, amaute' omna tung a sangna munah tu in.
Pasian, kei hong hupa hi a, lungsim man mite a hon hi.
Pasian, thu a tangin a khenpa hi a, migilote tungah a heh denpa ahi hi.
Amah'n mei thaltang bawl a, sih theihna ama galhiamte a baihsa in a koihzo hi.
Migilo in thusia paii a, suak nuamin na a, zuauthu a hingkhia hi.
Amah'n gum to a, ama tawhsa gum sung mahah amah a kia hi.
Na nasepna, na bawlsa, kha le aksite, le na vantungte ka et ciangin,
na ngaihsut tham dingin mihing bang hi lel a, na phawk tham dingin mihingta bang hi lel ahi hiam?
Tuu le bawng khempeuh, gamsa khempeuh zong,
Topa, kote' Topa aw, leitung khempeuhah na min lian mahmah hi.
Nangma hangin nuamin ka diangding a, na min phatna ka sading hi, Sangpenpa aw.
Ka galte a nungkik ciangin, nangma maiah amaute pukin kisia uh hi.
Topa ahihleh kumpi zaah tu ngitnget a, thukhen nadingin a tokhom a bawl hi.
Leitung mite' thu a mantakin khen a, a kilawm bangin mite' thu a khen hi.
Zionah a om Topa phatnala sa un! Ama nasepnate mite' lakah gen un!
Topa'n thu hong khenin migilote amau' nasepna mahah awksakna tawh amah hong kilang hi.
Pasian a mangngilh minam khempeuh sung panin migilote, Leinuaiah paiding uh hi.
Amaute lausak in, Topa ! Mi ahih lelna uh minamte theisak in!
