Topa pen keima tanh ahi hi. Na thute zuihding ka kiciam hi.
Ka gamtatnate ka ngaihsun a, na ngeinate zuihding ka kiciam hi.
Kei kinawhin, na thupiakte zuihding ka zekai kei hi.
Migilote' khau in kei hong vialh hangin nangma thu ka mangngilh tuan kei hi.
A thuman na ngeina kipte hangin nangmah a phat dingin zankim laitakin ka tho hi.
Topa aw, na thuciamna bangin na nasempa na limbawl hi.
Na thupiakte um ka hih manin thu khentel theihna le theihsiamna hong hilh in.
Na teci pannate a theih nadingun nang hong zahtakte kei' lamah hong kiheisak in.
Na thuciamnate ka etetna in ka mitte thazawta hi. “Cik ciangin hong hehnemding na hiam?” kong ci hi.
Na nasempa in bang tanvei ngaklaiding ka hi hiam? Kei hong bawlsiate cik ciangin thu khending na hi hiam?
Topa aw, vantungah nangma thu kip tawntung hi.
Nangma thumanna khang tawntungin kip hi. Nangmah in leitung na kipsak a, om tawntung hi.
Nangma thu, nuam a sa lo hileng, ka gimthuaknaah ka kisia khinzo tading hi.
Na thu deih mahmah ing. Sun tawntungin ka lungngaihngaih ahi hi.
Na thu ka zuih theih nadingin gamtatsia khempeuh ka pelh hi.
Nangma thute khum mahmah a, khuaizu sangin khumzaw hi.
Nangma thu pen lam hong lakding meivak hi a, ka paina lampiah khuavak ahi hi.
Nakpi takin gimna ka thuak hi. Topa aw, nong ciamsa bangin kei hong nungtasak in.
Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte tawntung keima luah ahi hi. Tuate pen keima lungdamna ahi hi.
Nangma ngeina kipte ka sih mateng a zui tawntung dingin ka lungsim ka khensat hi.
Nang kong zahtakna hangin ka khuasikmul suak a, na thukhennate ka zahtak hi.
Thutang thumanin ka gamta hi. Hong nengniamte' khut sungah kei hong nusia kei in.
Na nasempa a dingin nangmah hong kikham inla, mi kiphasakte hong nengniamsak kei in.
Topa aw, nangma thu kipalsat khin ahih ciangin thu na khending hun hita hi.
Tua ahih ciangin khamte, le kham hoihpente sangin nangma thupiakna ka deihzaw hi.
Na thuhilhnate lamdang pha mahmah a, ka lungsim khempeuh tawh tuate ka zui hi.
Na thupiakte ka lunggulhna in ka kam ka in ka leii ka kha hi.
Nangma thuhilhte ka zuih theih nadingin hong nengniamte' kiang pan kei hong honkhia in.
Na nasempa tungah na mai hong taangsak inla, na ngeina kipte hong hilh in.
Mite'n nangma thu zui lo uh ahih manin ka khitui hawk luanin a luang hi.
Topa aw, nang na thuman a, na thukhennate zong thuman mahmah hi.
Nangma koihsa ngeina kipte thumanin thutak hi.
Na thuciamnate kician mahmah a, na nasempa in tuate deih mahmah hi.
Nangma thumanna kip tawntung a, na thukham zong man tawntung hi.
Nang tungah kong kiko hi. Na thuhilhnate ka zuih theih nadingin kei hong hon in.
Nangma thuciamna a lungngaingai dingin zan khuavakin ka zanhak hi.
Vankinusia tampi tak a ngahpa bangin na thuciamnaah ka lung a dam mahmah hi.
Zuaunate zadahin ka kih a, ahih hangin nangma thu ka deih mahmah hi.
Nangmah biakna ngeina kipte hangin nisimin sagihvei nang kong phat hi.
Topa aw, nong hotkhiatding ka ngak a, na thupiakte ka sem hi.
Na thuhilhnate ka zui a, tuate ka nak deih mahmah hi.
Na ngeina kipte kei hong hilh na hih manin kong phat tawntungding hi.
Na thupiak khempeuh man mahmah ahih manin nangma thu phatnala ka sading hi.
Topa aw, nong hotkhiatding ka lamen a, nangma khut sungah nuam ka sa mahmah hi.
Ka cihmawh ciangin Topa' tungah ka kiko a, amah in hong dawng hi.
Topa aw, mizuaute le mikhemte' kiang panin kei hong honkhia in.
Mikhem theite aw, note' tungah bang hong kipiading a, note' tungah bang hong kihihding ahi hiam?
Galhang pa' thal hiamte le sesing hol-am hiding hi.
Note lakah ka omkhak pen Meshek gam sungah tenkhak sangin haksazaw a, Kedar mite lakah tenkhak sangin siahuaizaw hi.
Gal kilemna a deih lo mite lakah sauvei ka teng luakha hi.
Keimah in mualtung lam ka ento hi. Keimah huhna koi lai pan hong paiding ahi hiam?
Van le lei a bawl Topa' kiang panin keimah huhna hong pai hi.
Amah'n ka khe taalsak loding a, kei hong kempa lusu loding hi.
En un, Israel a kempa lusu lo a, zong ihmu lo hi.
Topa'n nang hongcingding a, nangmah a hong hu dingin na kiangah hong om hi.
Topa'n tua kipan a tawntungin na vaksuk na vaktohnaah nang hong kemding hi.
Jerusalem aw, na kulhkongpi sungah kote hong tungin kading khinta uh hi.
David' innkuante' kumpi tokhom, thukhennading kumpi tokhomte, tua laiah kikoih hi.
Jerusalem khuapi, a nopsaknading thu ngen unla, “Nang hong itte a dau pai tahen.
Sanggamte le kikholhpihte ka khualna in, “Jerusalem in nopna omta hen,” ka ciding hi.
Topa eite' Pasian' inn ka khualna in nangma hoihnading thu ka ngending hi.
Vantungah a ompa aw, nangmah kong ento hi.
Israel mite aw, Topa'n hong panpih lo hileh i tuahding thu thei un.
Eite langpangin mite hong kipat ciangin eite' lamah Topa hong pang lo hileh,
Tuikhang in eite hong tai in, tuihual in hong tum khinding a,
tuipi husiate in hong tuummang khinding hi.
Amaute' suksiat dingin eite a hong piakhia lo Topa'n thupha ngah tahen.
Van le lei a bawl Topa' tung panin eite huhna hong pai hi.
Topa a muang mite pen ling hetloin a om tawntung Zion Mual tawh kibang hi.
Topa'n Zionah eite hong ciahpih kik ciangin i mang tawh kibang liang hi.
Topa'n eite a dingin na lianpite bawl khinta a, eite i kipak hi.
Khitui tawh khai a tuhte lungdamin kikona tawh anla sakta in.
Topa zahtakin ama thu a zui mi khempeuh thupha ngah mi ahi hi.
Na khut tawh na sep thaman na neding a, na lungdamin na maavangding hi.
En un, Topa a zahtak mi tua bangin thupha kipiading hi.
Na tute a mu dingin hong siam tahen. Israel tungah nopna omta hen!
Zion a mudahte khempeuh maizumin kinungkiksak tahen.
Topa aw, ka lungkham mahmahna panin nang tungah kong kiko hi.
Topa aw, ka aw hong za in. Ka thumna awgingte hong ngai in.
Topa aw, nangmah in mawhneite ciamteh lecin, Topa aw, kua in thuakzoding ahi hiam?
Ahih hangin nangmah hong kizahtak theih nadingin nangmah in mawhna na maisak hi.
Topa' hong huhding lawpna tawh ka ngak a, ama thugen ka muang hi.
Mawhna a om khempeuh panin amah in Israelte a honkhiading hi.
Israel aw, tu a kipanin a tawntungin Topa muang in.
Jaar gam sungah Thuciamna Singkuang ka mu uh hi, cihna thuthak Bethlehemah kiza hi.
“Ama omna munah va pai ni; ama khengaknaah va bia ni,” ka ci uh hi.
Topa aw, tho inla na vangliatna lim Thuciamna Singkuang tawh na omna munah pai in.
Na nasempa David tungah thu na ciamzo hi; na sathau nilhpa nial kei in.
Ama beemlepang thupha tampi ka piading a, a mizawngte an ka vak khamding hi.
En un, sanggamte pumkhat suakin a tut khawm uh ciangin bangzahin hoihin nuam ahi hiam?
Siangtho mun lamah na khutte uh laamto in Topa phat un.
Van le lei a bawl Topa'n Zion panin note tungah thupha hong pia tahen.
Amah'n Egypt gam sungah mihing ganhing tacil khempeuh a vatmai hi.
Minam tampite vatmai in kumpi vangliante that a,
Amor kumpipa Sihon, Bashan kumpipa Og le Kanaan kumpite a that hi.
Amau' leitang khempeuh, ama mi Israelte' luah dingin a piakhia hi.
Minam dangte' pasiante pen mihingte' khut tawh a kibawl, ngun le kham ahi hi.
Israel mite aw, Topa phat un. Aaron' innkuante aw, Topa phat un.
Levi mite aw, Topa phat un. Topa a zahtakte aw, Topa phat un.
Jerusalem inn-a a nei, Zion-a om Topa'n thupha ngah tahen. Topa phat un.
Khuavak lianpite a bawlpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
San Tuipi a phelkhampa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
Kumpi liante a vatmaipa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
Kumpi minthangte a thatpa tungah, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
Bashan kumpipa Og' hangin, bang hang hiam cih leh ama itna kip tawntung hi.
Zion khuapi i ngaihsut khak ciangin Babylon luite geiah eite tusukin i kapkap hi.
Tua lai-a gialhek kungte tungah i laiza lasaknate i khai hi;
Topa'la, gam dangah bangci sak theihding ihi hiam?
Jerusalem khuapi aw, nang kong mangngilh taak leh ka taklam khut buisumta hen!
Na taneute hong laksakin suangtumpi denna in a hong neihsakpa in lungdamna ngahta hen!
Nang kong sap ciangin kei nong dawng a, na thahatna tawh kei nong thakhauhsak hi.
Topa' minthanna lian mahmah ahih manin amaute in Topa' nasepna ziatela in sading uh hi.
Topa aw, nangmah in kei na hong entel a, nong thei khin hi.
Nangmah a pelh dingin koiah paiding a, nangma omna panin koi laiah taikhiading ka hi hiam?
Leimong pekah leengin, tuipi mong pekah omta leng zong,
Pasian aw, migilote that inla, kei kiang panin mi that theite paikhia sak in.
Topa aw, nang hong mudah mite ke'n mudah hi lo ka hi hiam? Nang' langah hong pangte ke'n kih hi lo ka hi hiam?
Amaute ka mudah mahmah a, amaute ka galin ka seh hi.
Kei sungah siattheihna a omkha hiam hong en inla, tawntung lampiah kei hong kha in.
Amaute'n a lung sung uhah thusia geelgeel uh a, gal phuang ngitnget uh hi.
A leii uh gulpi leii bang a, a thugente uh gulgu bang hi.
Topa, keima Topa, a thahat hong honkhiapa aw, galkidona sungah keimah nong hu hi.
Mi gensiapa leitungah mavangsak kei inla, mi ngongtatpa pen thusia in sulzuihta hen!
Amaute'n kei hong siahna uh tehlop le siatna bawlte' thangzak panin kei hong kem in.
Kei ka suahtak khit ciangin amau' ngenthang sung mahah migilote awksak in.
Topa' hong huhding ngenin ka kiko a, Topa' tungah ka thum hi.
Topa aw, nangmah in na hong phawk tham dingin mi pen bang hi a, nangmah in na hong ngaihsut tham dingin mihing' tapa bang ahi hiam?
Topa aw, na vanpite niamsak inla, hong paisuk in. Mualte lawng inla, meikhu suaksak in.
Khuaphialep phiasak inla, amaute kithehthang sak in. Na thaltangte lawn inla, amaute susia in.
Pasian aw,la thak khat kong sakding a, harp zangsawm khausai lasakna nang kong tumding hi.
Kumpite tungah gualzawhna a piapa, na nasem David a honkhiapa na hi hi.
Ka kongzingte uhah cimawhin kikona om kei tahen.
Nisimin hong pahtawi in a tawntungin nangma min kong phatphatding hi.
Topa lian hi; nakpitakin phatding hi a, ama liatna ngaihsutzawhding hi lo hi.
A khang a khangin nangma nasepnate kiphatphatding a, a vanglian na bawlnate kigengending hi.
Na liatna le na minthanna a lamdang nangma sepnate ka lungngaingaiding hi.
Amaute'n nangma liatna, na minthanna genkhia in nangma thumanna nakpitakin sading uh hi.
Topa dikin hehpihna nei a, heh hak mahmahin itna kip lianpi a nei hi.
Topa pen mi khempeuh tungah hoih a, a bawlsa khempeuh tungah hehpihna a nei hi.
Amaute'n na kumpi gam a minthanna thu gengenin na vangliatna thu sutsutding uh a,
Topa'n a puk mite khempeuh huh a, niamsakna a thuakte khempeuh a sangtosak hi.
Topa pen a sepna khempeuhah thutang a, a gamtatna khempeuhah hehpihna a nei hi.
Topa'n amah a itte khempeuh kem a, ahih hangin migilo khempeuh amah in susiading hi.
Topa phat un. Ke'n, Topa ka phatding hi.
Zion aw, nangma Pasian Topa'n khang tawntungin ukding hi. Topa phat un.
Topa'n Jerusalem khuapi lam a, amah in a kinilkhia Israelte a kaikhawm hi.
Amah'n lungsim kitamte damsak a, amau' meimate a tuamsak hi.
Amah'n aksite a phazahding seh a, tua aksite amau min ciatin a sam hi.
Topa'n a kisikcip mite laamto in, migilote leilak a denna hi.
Topa tungah lungdamkohnala sa unla, laiza lasakna tawh eite' Pasian' tungahla ngaih sa un.
Amah'n ganhingte le a ham va-aknote an a vak hi.
Amah a zahtak mite le ama itna kip a muangte tungah Topa a lungkim hi.
Jerusalem khuapi aw, Topa phat in. Zion aw, nangma Pasian phat in.
Amah'n na gam sungah kilemna bawl a, mangbuh hoihpente tawh nang hong gilvahsak hi.
Amah'n thu hong pia a, ama thu manlangin leitung hong tungsuk hi.
Amah'n tuumul bangin vukkhal hong pia a, vut bangin vukpak hong thehthang hi.
Amah'n suangtum bangin tuikhalte hong lawnkhia hi. Tua a votna kua in thuakzoding ahi hiam?
Topa phat un. Vantung panin Topa phat unla, a sangna panin amah phat un.
Ama vantungmi khempeuh aw, amah phat un. Ama mihonte khempeuh aw, amah phat un.
Ni le kha aw, amah phat un. A taang aksi khempeuh aw, amah phat un.
Van sangpente le vantung a om tuite aw, amah phat un.
Leitung panin Topa phat un, no gulpi liante le tuipi thuk khempeuh,
mei le gial, tuikhal le vuk, ama thupiakna a mang huihpi!
Gamsate le innsate khempeuh, a bokvak ganhingte le a leeng vasate khempeuh!
No leitung kumpite le mihing khempeuh, leitung uliante le thukhente khempeuh!
Nungakte le tangvalte, teeksiate le naupangte aw, amah phat un.
Amah a Bawlpa tungah Israel lungdam henla, amau' Kumpipa' tungah Zion mite kipak tahen.
Lamna tawh amah phat unla, khuang le laiza lasakna tawh ama tungahla ngaih sa un.
Peengkul aw tawh amah phat unla, githa lasakna le harp lasakna tawh amah phat un.
Khuang le lamna tawh amah phat unla, khausai lasaknate le tamngai tawh amah phat un.
Daltuahte tawh amah phat unla, nakpitakin a ging daltuahte tawh amah phat un.
Husang thei khempeuh in Topa phat un. Topa phat un.
David' tapa, Israel kumpi Solomon' paunakte:
A hoihin a pil gamtat theih nading, thuman, thutang, a kilawmin a gamtat theih nading.
Mi ciimsate ciimsak semsemin, mi pilsate pilsak semsemin,
Kata aw, na pa' hong thuhilhna hoihtakin zui inla, na nu' hong thugente ngai in.
Kata aw, mi hoih lote in nang hong zol ciangin, amau' zolna zui kei in.
Amaute'n, “Hong pai in, mi khatpeuh va that ni! Mi ommuang khat va muansuam ni!
Kata aw, tua bang mite tawh kikhawl kei inla, amaute kiang panin kihemkhia in.
I matnop vasate' muhtangpi in, i siahna ngenthang zaak leeng a mawkna ahi hi.
Ngai in! Kongzing lampi le van kizuakna phualpiah pilna hong kiko hi.
Khuapi kulhkongpi tual le mi a kikhopna mun khempeuhah nakpitakin hong awngkhia a,
“Mihaite aw, bang tanvei hai omom nuam na hi uh hiam? Bang tanvei pilna thudon loin omding na hi uh hiam? Pilna ngaihsutin nei ngei loding na hi uh hiam?
Kong thuhilhna hong ngai un; ka ngaihsutna kong gending a, ka theihna kong zasakding hi.
Note'n pilna na deih kei uh a, Topa na zahtak nuam kei uh hi.
Ka thugente na deih kei uh a, kong thuhilhna ngai nuam lo na hih manun,
na gamtatna bangun na thuakding uh a, nomau' gamtatna mah in note hong gimsakding hi.
Kata aw, kong hilhte thei inla, kong gente mangngilh kei in.
Pilna thute limtakin ngai inla, na theihtel zawh nadingin hanciam in.
Thu theih nading hanciam takpi inla, thu muhnading hahkat takpi in.
Ngun, ahih kei leh a kiseel sum manpha zon bangin, hahkatin pilna zong in.
Tua hileh, Topa zahtakna thu na theiding a, Pasian na theitelding hi.
Pasian in thuman mite pilna guan a, midikte a hu hi.
Amah'n thutang mitecing a, amah a itte a kem hi.
Tua hileh thuman le thutang a hoih le a kilawm na theiding hi.
Tua ciangin mipil na suakding a, na pilna hangin nuam na sading hi.
Na thungaihsut theihna le na thutelna in nangmah hong hu in,
a sia in na gamtatkhakding hong kemding a, kampauna tawh buaina a piangsak thei mi,
nuntakna manin a nungta lo, mawhna khuamial sungah a gamta,
a sia in gamtatding nuam a sa, a sia-a gamtatnaah a lungkim mahmah,
mi lungsim kawi, muan theih lohding mite panin nang hong kemding hi.
Tua ahih manin mihoihte' gamtat bangin na gamtading a, thuman mite' gamtatna na zuiding hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh mi thuman, miginate, hih i leitungah tengin omding uh a,
ahi zongin Pasian in leitung panin migilote lawnkhia in, singkung zungbawh bangin mawhneite botkhiading hi.
Kata aw, kong thuhilhte mangngilh kei inla, kong thugente phawk tawntung in.
Kong thuhilhte in na khan hong sausakding a, hong daupaisakding hi.
Tua hileh, Pasian' mai le mite' maiah maipha ngahin na maa vangding hi.
Na lungsim khempeuh tawh Topa muang inla, nang' theihna suang kei in.
Na hihna khempeuhah amah phawk in. Tua hileh lampi man amah in hong lakding hi.
Nangmah a pilin kingaihsun tawm kei inla, Topa zahtakin a sia peel in.
Na neihsa le na anpalte tawh Topa zahtak in.
Tua hileh na ansalte an tawh kidimding a, beel dimletin leenggahzu na neiding hi.
Kata aw, Topa' thuhilhna limtakin ngai in, hong tainate thudon in.
Pilna nei in thu a thei mipa, a lungdam mi ahi hi.
Pilna nei leeng ngun sangin hoihzaw a, kham sangin zong manpha zaw hi.
Pilna in khan hong sausak a, hauhna le pahtawina zong hong piathuah lai hi.
Pilna in nuntakna hong nuamsak a, lungmuang takin hong omsak den hi.
Topa'n pilna tawh leitung bawl a, a theihtelna tawh vantung a bawl hi.
Ama pilna in guntuite luangsak a, meiite in leitungah guah zusak hi.
Tuate pen nang a dingin nuntakna hiding a, na hoih nadingin kizepna hiding hi.
Tua hileh lungmuang takin na nungtading a, puknading thu bangmah om loding hi.
Launa om loin nuamtakin na lumding a, zan tawntung lungmuang takin na ihmu theiding hi.
Migilote tungah huihpi bangin siatna a tun ciangin, nang na lunghihmawhnading bangmah om loding hi.
Na hihzawhding ahih nakleh midangte' kitangsapna huh tawntung in.
A ngongtat thei mite engkha kei inla, amau' gamtat bangin gamtakha kei in.
Topa'n migilote' innsung samsia a, thuman mite' innsung thupha a pia hi.
Amah'n mi kihisakte bangmahin sim lo a, a kiniamkhiatte tungah maipha a pia hi.
Tate aw, napa uh' hong hilhnate ngai unla, thu na teltheih nadingun limtakin ngaihsun un.
Kei zong tapa khat neihsun ka hi a, naupangno khat ka hih lai in
Pilna deih in; mi lianin hong bawlding hi. Limtakin pom in; pahtawina hong ngahsakding hi.
Pilna in pahtawina le minthanna nangma tungah hong tungsakding hi,” hong ci hi.
Kata aw, ka thugente limtakin zui in. Tua hileh na khansauding hi.
Na pilnading lampi kong hilhzo a, na gamtatnading zia kong genzo hi.
Hong kihilhnate lencip inla, khahsuah kei in. Na nuntaknading ahih manin limtakin zui in.
Migilote tawh kikhawl kei inla, amau' gamtatnate zui kei in.
Amau' gamtat bangin gamta peuhmah ke'n! Gitlohna peel in! Paisan inla, na maban sem in.
Gitloh gamtatna, annek bangin nuamsa uh a, ngongtatna, tui dawn bangin a ngaihsun uh hi.
Kata aw, ka thugente don inla, ka kammalte ngai in.
Na kiang panin paikhiasak kei inla, na lungsimah ciamteh in.
Kisuanna nei hetloin om liuliau inla, maizumin kuncip kei in.
Na khatpeuh na sepna thu theitel in. Tua hileh na nasep peuhpeuh maavangding hi.
Siatna peelin a manin gamta inla, thuman lampi panin themcik zong pialkha kei in.
Kata aw, ka pilna le ka thumuhnate, limtakin ngai in hong za in.
Numei paktatte' kampau khuaizu bangin khum mahmahin a thugente uh a neel dakdak hangin,
a tawpnaah lungkhamna le natna simloh nangma tungah bangmah dang hong guan lo hi.
Tate aw, tu in ka thugente limtakin hong ngai unla, ka thugente mangngilh kei un.
Tua bang numei tawh kinehkha kei unla, a inn gei nangawnah paikha kei un.
Tua ciangin, “Bang hangin thu thei hoh lo a, hong kihilhna mang hoh lo ka hi hiam?
Na zi' tungah citak inla, amah bek itin nei in.
Pasal dang tawh va vakzau in kongzing lakah va mawhkhading hi.
Na zi pen nangma ading bek hi a, midangte tawh na neihkhawmding hi lo hi.
Tua ahih ciangin na zi tawh lungkim inla, na tenpih numei tawh lungdam in.
Kata aw, bang hangin numei dang lunggulhding a, numei dangte' ngaihbaanna iplahding na hi hiam?
Kata aw, na lawmte khatpeuh in sum leitawi a lak ciangin a lohzawh kei leh ama tangin a lohsak dingin kam na ciamkha hiam?
Na kampauna hangin nang hong kimanin, na thuciamna hangin na awkkha hiam?
Ihmumu kei inla, om mawkmawk kei in.
Thadahpa aw, miksite kiangah pai inla, amau' nuntakzia va en in.
Amaute'n a ukding le a makaiding kuamah nei lo napi in,
khuakhal sungin a nekding uh, tuk hun sungin kaikhawm khol uh hi.
Thadahpa aw, bang tanvei lumlumding a, cik ciangin thokhiading na hi hiam?
Tawmkhat sung mengme lai ning, na cih kikalin
zawnna le cihmawhna in migilo gutate bangin nang hong sugawp pakding hi.
Miginalo pa, a gilo pa, thuzuau genin vak kawikawi a,
A lungsimah thusia bekbek ngaihsun niloh a, a omna peuhah buaina a piangsak hi.
kihihsakna, zuauthu genna, mawhnei lo mi thahna,
thusia bawlding ngaihsutna, gamtatsiatding a manlangte,
zuauthu gen teci man lote, le kitotna a piangsakte ahi hi.
Amau' hong thugente phawk tawntung inla, na lungsimah ciamteh niloh in.
Amau' melhoihna iplahkha kei inla, amau' hong zawlmitna khenglahkha kei in.
Na ang sungah meikuang pom lecin na puan kang loin omding ahi hiam?
Mei-am tungtawnin pai lecin na khe kang loin omding ahi hiam?
amah kiman leh a zah sagihin kilohsak a, a neih khempeuh a piak kul hi.
Mawhna a bawl mi in satgawpna thuakding a, a min sia in mindai paisuakding hi.
Kata aw, ka thugente ciamteh inla, kong sawl thute khempeuh mangngilh ngei kei in.
Kong hilhnate kem tawntung inla, na lungtang tungah gelh in.
Pilna na sanggamnu dingin nei inla, thumuhna na lawm it pen dingin nei in.
Khatvei, ka omna innah, ka tawlet panin ka khuadak a,
tua hun pen nitak nitum khit zawh, khuamui hun laitak ahi hi.
Mihon omna van zuakna phual, lamdung citeng, kongkiu khatpeuhah mi ngakin om niloh hi.

“Tuni in biakpiakna ka bawl a, nekding sa tampi ka nei hi.
Ka nekpih dingin nang ka hong zong a, tu in kong mu petmah hi.
Ka lupna tungah a nop mahmah dingin, Egypt gam puan hoihpente ka phahzo hi.

Ka tate aw, kei' lam hong nga unla, ka thugente hong ngai un.
Tua bang numeite' zolna mang kei unla, tua bangte tawh khialkha kei un.
Ngai un! Pilna in hong sam a, thungaihsut theihna hong kiko hi lo ahi hiam?

khuapi lutna lampi geiah, mi omna kongpi tualah hong kiko a,
Ngaihsut kicing nai lote aw, na lungsim uh khanghamsak un. Mihaite aw, thu ngaihsun un.
Ngai un, thu manpha kong gending hi; ka gen khempeuh thuman vive ahi hi.
Ka thugente a man bekbek hi a, zuauthu ka deih kei hi.

Thungaihsun theite a dingin telnop mahmah a, thu mutheite a dingin siang mahmah hi.

Kei hong itte ka it a, kei hong zong peuhmahte in hong mu uh hi.

Zuaugenna tawh hauhnate beimang pak a, sihna khuk sung hong tunpih hi.
Mimawhte thukawi in gamta uh a, midikte a manin gamta uh hi.
Migilote in thusia bekbek deih uh a, a lawmte nangawn zah tuan lo uh hi.
A simthamin letsong piakna in hehna damsak a, puannuai tawi in sinsona daisak hi.
Thutangin na a kisep ciangin midik khempeuh lungdam a, ahi zongin migilote lungkham hi.
A kilawm gamtatna pan a pialkhia mite misi honte lakah a tung hi.
Midikte' thuak dingin a bawlsak uh gimnate pen migilote mah in lehthuak zawsop uh hi.
A phun hat zi gilo tawh tenkhop sangin gam simthamah khat guak tangten' hoihzaw hi.
Thuman thutakin gamta tawntung lecin na khan sau in pahtawina na ngahding hi.
Kampau a ki-ipzote lungkhamna tawh kipelh hi.
Mi kihisak i cihte pen kilian sakin a kiphasak mite ahi hi.
Mi thadahpa in na sem nuam lo ahih manin amahmah a kithattawm ahi hi.
A man lo tecite mangthangding uh a, thuman tecite' kam kizazading hi.
Kiniamkhiat-a Topa zahtakna thaman in hauhna, minthanna, le khansauna ahi hi.
Migilote' lampiah thang kisiahin so kidawh a, mipilte in tua lampi pelh uh hi.
Mihaute in mizawngte uk a, leitawi a late pen a piate' sila a suak hi.
A cingh mi in mizawngte an pia a, amah in thupha ngahkik hi.
Mi kiphasakte hawlkhia lecin kitotna le kisimmawhna bei pahding hi.
Kamsiamna in kumpipa' lawm hong suaksak a, ahi zongin Topa'n lungsim takpi a deih hi.
Topa'n thuman mite kem a, ahi zongin thuzuau gente a lawnthal hi.
Naupangte a hai gamtat a ngeina hi a, deihtakin pangbetna in mihoih suaksak thei hi.
Na lungsim uhah ciingin zang thei le-uhcin, na lung uh dam tawntungding hi.
Thuhilhna le pilna thu nam sawmthum hih laiah note a dingin ka gelh a,
A hehbaih mite tawh kipawl kei unla, a lungtom mite tawh kikhawl kei un.
Midangte' leiba lohsak dingin kamciamin leiba tavuan lakha kei un.
A leiba lohsakzo kei le-uhcin na lupna nangawn uh hong kidawhkhiatsakding hi.
Na pu na pate' phuhsa gisuang cikmah hunin khin kei un.
A nasepnaah a siam mahmah mi na theikha uh hiam? Amah'n mi mawkmawkte' na sem loding a, kumpite' na semding hi.
Miliante tawh an nekhawm dingin na tut uh ciangin na tutpihpa limtakin en un.
An a ngaklah thei mi na hih khak uhleh zong limtakin kidawm un.
Hong thangsiahna hi khatheiding ahih manin tua anlimte lunggulh pah lua kei un.
Hauhnop man bekin sum' sila suak kei unla, a man loin gamtakha kei un.
Na ngahsa uh sumte mitphiat kalin beimang thei a, muvanlai bangin thakhatin leengmang thei hi.
A cil tentan mite' an neksak kei unla, a anlimte uh duhgawhkha kei un.
Mihaite pil hopih kei un; amaute in a manphatna phawk thei lo uh hi.
Tanglai gisuang khin kei unla, tagahte' leitang va keek kei un.
Amaute a pawlpihpa pen Topa hi a, note' langkhatah amaute panpihding hi.
Hong kihilhnate zui unla, pilna thu hong kigente ngai un.
Naupangte satding lunghiang kei un; satna hangin si loding hi.
Ciangduai tawh sat le-uhcin nuntaklawh zawding uh hi.
Kata aw, mipil suak lecin ka lungdam mahmahding hi.
Thuman na gen ciangin ka nuam mahmahding hi.
Mawhnei mite engkha kei inla, Topa zahtakna zom paisuak in.
Tua bang hi lecin lametna om a, cithei in na khansauding hi.
Zu nenete tawh kikhawl kei inla, a uisante tawh kithuahkha kei in.
Thuman, pilna, siamna, thungaihsut theihna lei in; zuakkhiat dingin tuate pammaih lua hi.
Ta hoih a neipa a lung damding a,ta pil a neipa ata' tungah lungkimding hi.
Na nu le napa a kipak nadingin gamta inla, na pianna nu lungdamsak in.
Kata aw, ka thugente ciamteh inla, keima gamtat bangin nang zong gamta in.
Gutate bangin nang hong buksim a, mi tampi tak siasak uh hi.
Kuate in gal nei a, kuate in dahna thuak hiam? Thu om lopi in kuate liam a, thu om lopi in kuate a mit san gega hiam?
Zu ne-a a tut khote zu a nenete ahi hi.
Na mitah na lamdangdang hong suakding a, hoihtakin na pau thei nawn keiding hi.
Migilote eng kei inla, amaute tawh kikhawl kei in.
Amaute'n tatsiatding bek ngaihsun uh a, thusia bekbek genin nei uh hi.
Pilna tawh inn kilam a, ngaihsut siamna tawh inn kip hi.
Thungaihsut theihna inn sungah a hoih a manpha nate a dimtakin om hi.
Thahatna sangin pilna hoihzaw a, thakhauhna sangin thutheihna hoihzaw hi.
Geel siamna tawh galte kizo a, ngaihsut siamna tawh gualzawhna kingah hi.
Thusia lamsang a deih mite thusia bawl mi kici hi.
Haksatna na tuah ciangin na lung a kiat leh a ginalo mi na hi hi.
Kata aw, khuaizu khum ahih manin ne in. I kamah khuailuzu khum mahmah hi.
Migilote' gamtat bangin thuman mite' omna sugawp kei inla, amau' tenna inn luhgawp kei in.
Migilote' hangin lung nuammawh kei inla, amaute eng kei in.
Amaute'n mai lamah lametding bangmah nei lo a, amaute' meivak kisukmitsakding hi.
Kata aw, Topa le kumpipa zahtak khawm inla, amau a langpangte tawh kipawlkha kei in.
Mimawh kimlai a diksak thukhenpa leitung a mi khempeuh in mudahin phuisamding hi.
A mawh mi gim a pia thukhenpa ahihleh thupha kipia in daupaiding hi.
A mantakin dawnkikna pen lawm taktak hihna lim ahi hi.
Tua bang ka muh ciangin thu ka lungngaingai a, thu manpha khat ka mukhia hi.
Tawmkhat ihmutna, tawmkhat lusukna, tawmkhat sung na sep lohna, khutzepin ommawkna hangin
i tungah zawnna hong tung a, cihmawhna in hong khuhcip hi.
Judah kumpi Hezekiah' lai-atte in a teikhiat uh Solomon' paunak dangte:
Ngun a ek teng paikhia lehang sikseekpa in na hoihpi piangsak thei hi.
Kumpipa kiang pan migilote nilkhia lehang thumanin ama ukna kip thei bek hi.
Kumpipa maiah na om ciangin milian kineih kei inla, miliante' tutnading munah tukha kei in.
Thu khatpeuh na theih ciangin thukhen zum tun pah kei in. Na vengpa in nang' khialhna hong laktel kik leh nang bang lawh nawnding na hi hiam?
Tua hikeileh amah hehin nang hong maizumsakding a, na minsiatna bei ngei nawn loding hi.
Na vengte' innah hawh mun lua kei in. Hong cimtakin hong mudah khading hi.
Leilu lam huih in guah a zuksak bangin gensiatna in hehna piangsak hi.
Sakolte satding kisam a, late kamkaih kisam a, mihaite zong satding a kisam ahi hi.
Mihaite' thudotna dawngdawng lecin nang zong amau mah bangin a hai na hi hi.
Thadahpa in, “Lampiah humpinelkai om! Kongzingah humpinelkai om!” ci in lumlum hi.
Kongkhak pen kawmhek tungah a kiheihei lel bangin mi thadahpa a lupna tungah kiheihei hi.
A vengte a khem khit ciangin ka ciamnuihna hi, a cipa pen
sihtheihna gu a baang thaltang tawh a kappa tawh kibang hi.
Sing om kei leh mei mit a, gensiatna om kei leh kitotna bei hi.
Meihol in mei-amding piangsak a, sing in mei kuangsak a, migilo in kitotna piangsak hi.
Tungtham beka kam khum pauna pen cimbeng kizut leibeel tawh kibang hi.
Ama hoih lohna a ip nop hangin mi khempeuh in ama gitlohna thei veve hi.
Suangtum le sehnel gik mahmah a, ahi zongin mihaite' piansak lungkhamna gikzaw lai hi.
Hehna le sinsona siahuai a, ahi zongin hazatna siahuaizaw lai hi.
Itna i seel bawl sangin a langtangin taina hoihzaw hi.
Inn panin gamlapiah a zinkhia mipa a bu panin a leengkhia vasa tawh kibang hi.
Sathau namtui le paknamtui in lung nuamsak a, lawmte' limbawlna in tha hatsak hi.
Sik in sik mah hiamsak thei a, mi in midang pilsak thei hi.
Theikung acingpa in a theigah ne a, a tapa a kempa in pahtakna ngah hi.
Mihingte' lungsim pen misite' gam tawh kibang a, tamlua cih hun nei thei lo hi.
Ngun le khamte meikhukah kize-et a, mihing ahihleh phatna tawh kize-et hi.
Na tuuhonte hoihtakin thei inla, na bawnghonte hoihtakin kem in.
Na keelnawite ahihleh na innkuan annekding, le na nasem numeite' nuntak nadingin kicingding hi.
Kuama delh lohpi in migilote taimang a, mithumante ahihleh humpinelkai bangin a hang uh hi.
Hau napi in lungsimkawi mi hihna sangin zawng napi in paubaan neih lohna hoihzaw hi.
Mizawngte a uk migilopa pen humpinelkai gilkial le vompi halungvei tawh kibang hi.
Thumanin a gamta mite lungmuangin omding uh a, a zuautat mite ahihleh pukding uh hi.
Mi khat tai in thuhilh lecin tungthama phatna sangin a tawpnaah lungdamzawding hi.
A huaiham mi in kitotna piangsak a, Topa a muang mite mihau hiding hi.
Ei le ei kimuanna haina hi a, mipilte' hilhna zuihna pen lungmuanna ahi hi.
Kihilh napi in a mang nuam lote bawlphat zawh nawn loh dongin kisiading uh hi.
A man lopi in mi khat mawkphatna pen a awk nadingin thangsiahna ahi hi.
Migilote amau mawhna sungah awkcip a, midikte ahihleh suakta in lungdam uh hi.
Kumpipa in mizawngte' thu a manin khensak leh a ukna kip tawntungding hi.
Ciangduai le tai-na in pilna guan a, a kikhahkhongta in a nu maizumsak hi.
Nata thuhilhin tai lecin ama hangin na kipakding a, na lung hong kimsakding hi.
Thu ngaihsun loin a pheng paupau mipa sangin mihaipa a dingin lametna omzaw lai hi.
A heh pahpahte in kitotna piangsak a, a heh baihte khial thei tawntung hi.
A kiphasakte in niamkhiatna thuakding a, a kiniamkhiatte in pahtawina ngahding hi.
Midangte kihtakna in hong lunghimawhsak a, Topa muanna in hong lungmuangsak hi.
Midikte in migilote mudah uh a, migilote in midikte mudah uh hi.
Pilna thu ka thei kei a, Pasian' thu ka theih om lo hi.
Vantungah kua kahto a, leitungah kua hong kumsuk kik ahi hiam? Kua'n a khut sungah huihte lomcip a, puan tawh tuite tuncip ahi hiam? Kua'n leitung bulpite phut kip ahi hiam? Tua bang mi na theih ngei leh a tapa' min bang ahi hiam?
Pasian aw, thu nih kong ngen hi. Ka sih ma in tuate hong pia in.
Haulua leng nang hong nialin, “ Topa i cih kua ahi hiam?” kong ci khading a, zawnglua leuleu leng mi' na guksakin ka Pasian' min kong daisak khazelding hi.
Mihoih pha mahmahin a kingaihsun, a kiliansak mahmah mi pawlkhat om hi.
Ka theihzawh hetloh a lamdang mahmah thu thum om a, eh! li hi zaw:
Leitung mi khempeuh in a thuakzawh loh thu thum, eh! thu li om a,
Ngalvangte: A thahat lo ganhing hinapi in suang lakah a kuading bawl uh hi.
Kauphete: Kumpi nei lo napi in a kituak diamdiamin hontat thei uh hi.
Innhikte: Khut sunga tawizawh ganhing hilel napi in kumpi inn sungah tengzo uh hi.
A gamtatna i et ciangin a thupi suak mahmah thum, eh! li om hi.
Humpinelkai: Ganhing lak pan a hatpen kuamah a kihta lo.
Kumpipa Lemuel, a nu in a thuhilhna:
Kong it mahmah kata aw, thu ngenngenin kong neih ka tapa na hi hi. Nangma tungah bang teng hong gending ka hi hiam?
A si dekdekte, khamtheihzu pia inla, a lungkham mahmahte, leenggahzu pia in.
Amaute nesak lecin a zawnna uh mangngilhin, a lungkhamna uh phawk nawn loding uh hi.
A pasal in muang mahmah a, a innsung uhah annek kitasam ngei lo uh hi.
Amah'n samul le khau zongin thanuam takin na sem hi.
Amah'n sumbukte' van pua teembaw bangin gamlapi panin an hong ciahpih hi.
A nik singtenin a puanban zial a, thalawp takin na a sem hi.
Amah'n a nasepte a manphatna thei a, zankim zankhang dongin nakpitakin na a sem hi.
Amah'n khau kheekin a puanding gantawm hi.
A innkuan buppi puanlum guanzo ahih manin phalbi tunding lunghimawh lo hi.
Amah'n a puanding khuitawm a, saihadial puansan vive a silhzo hi.
Amah'n puan khui in kawnggakte zong bawl a, sumbukte tungah tuate a zuak hi.
Amah a tha hatin zong kizahtak a, mailam hun ading a lung patau lo hi.
Amah'n a pilna tawh thu gen a, kam khum takin pau hiathiat hi.
Amah'n a innkuansung kisapna teng sem a, a tawntungin manlah den hi.
A tate in amah it mahmah uh a, a pasal in zong pakta mahmah a,
Jerusalem khua sungah kumpi a sem, David' tapa, Thugen Siampa' thugente:
Thugen Siampa in hih bangin ci hi: A mawknapi, a mawknapi, na khempeuh a mawknapi.
Gimpi-a nisa thuakin nasepnaah mihing in bang noptuam ngah ahi hiam?
Khang khat bei in khang khat hong tung a, ahi zongin leitung kibangbang niloh hi.
Ni hong suakin ni tum a, a suakkik dingin tum zel hi.
Thugen Siampa kei pen Jerusalem khuaah Israel kumpipa ka hi ngei hi.
A kawisate kimamsak thei lo a, a om lopi a omin kiseh thei lo hi.
Pil semsem lehang kilunghimawh semsem a, tam thei semsem lehang hong gimsak semsem zawsop hi.
Nuihna pen haina ahihna, nopna pen bangmahin a kiman lohna ka mukhia hi.
Tua singnote tui piak nadingin tuikhukpi zong ka bawl hi.
Tua ciangin, “Mihaite tungah a piangding thute kei' tungah zong hong piangding ahih manin, ka pil mahmah manin bang phattuamna ngah ka hi hiam?” ka ci a, “Bangmah ngah kei ing, themkhat zong ngah kei ing,” ci in ka kidawng hi.
Tua ahih ciangin hih leitungah nakpitakin na ka sepna ka kisik hi.
Mi khat in hih leitungah lunghimawhin thatang sanin na a sepnaah bang phattuamna ngah ahi hiam?
Pasian kihel loin kua in an ne in nuamsa theiding ahi hiam?
Na a sem mipa in a sepsa khempeuh thamanin bang ngah ahi hiam?
Pasian in eite' manlahpih dingin hong piak nasep ka thei hi.
Tua tham loin, hih leitungah gitlohna in thuman thutang a suankhiatna zong ka mu hi.
A hinglai mite sangin a si khinsa mite hamphazaw ka sa hi.
Nuntakna sungah a mawknapi ahi thudang khat ka mu leuleu hi.
Mi khat in tapa ahi a, sanggam ahi zongin nei lo napi in, a tawntungin na semin a neihsa tawh lungkim hun nei thei lo hi. Kua a dingin gimpi in na sem a, a ututinta hoh lo ahi hiam? Hih zong a mawknapi mah, a dahhuai nuntakna khat ahi hi.
Mi khat sangin mi nih hoihzaw hi; amau' sepna thaman a tamzaw ngah uh hi.
Khua a dam ciangin mi nih lumkhawm leh khua lum hi; khat guak bangci khualum theihding ahi hiam?
Na thuciamna bangin na tunsak keiding le thu ciam vet kei zaw in.
Gam khat peuhpeuh in lo khawhna lamsang a lunghimawh kumpi khat kisam hi.
A dahhuai mahmah thu in: I suah hun lai-a mah bang teekteekin i ciahkikding hi. A mawknapiding a i sepnaah bang phattuamna ngah ihi hiam?
Pasian in lungdamin omsak ahih manin a nuntak tomlam phawkin nei kha loding hi.
Hih leitung a mihingte tungah a man hetloin hong kibawlna ka phawk hi.
Tua ahih manin mihaipa sangin mipilpa a hamphat zawkna bang om tuan ahi hiam? Mihaipa in nuntaknading zia a theih hangin bang phatuam tuan ahi hiam?
Sauvei kinial lehang a mawkna hi semsem a, a phattuamna om lo hi.
Niliim bangin a pai hanhan, a mawknapi hih nuntak tom sungah mihing ading a hoihpen kua in theiding ahi hiam? Ama sih khit ciangin leitungah bang piangding cih kua in gen thei ahi hiam?
Mipilte dahna lakah omtual a, mihaite nopna lakah omtual hi.
Mihaite in pahtawinala hong sak sangin mipilte' hong taina hoihzaw hi.
Thu khatpeuh a kipatna sangin a tawpna hoihzaw a, kiphatsakna sangin lungduaina hoihzaw hi.
Heh pahpah kei in; hehna a haihuai ahi hi.
“Bang hangin nidang lai in hih sangin hoihzaw tham ahi hiam?” ci in dong kei in. Tua bangte pil thudotna hi lo hi.
Pilna pen hauhna zahin hoih a, mihingte a dingin phattuamna ahi hi.
Pasian' sepsate ngaihsun dih in. Pasian in a kawi-a a bawlsate kua in mamsakkik thei ahi hiam?
Tua ahih ciangin hoihlua kei inla, lah sia lua kei in. Bang hangin nang kisiasak tawmding na hi hiam?
Gilo lua, hau lua kei in. Bang hangin khansih laizangding na hi hiam?
Khuapi a uk mihing sawm sangin pilna in mi khat hatsak zaw hi.
Mi' gen khempeuh thudon kei in. Na nasempa' hong samsiatna na zakhading hi.
Nang zong midang na samsiat zelzelna teltakin na kithei hi.
Mihing nuntakna kua in theikhia zoding ahi hiam? Eite a dingin thuk lua a, telhak lua hi.
Kumpipa' hong sawl bangin gamta inla, Pasian' tungah thu mawk ciampak kei in.
Na puante siangsakin paaksak tawntung inla, na sam gumsak ngei kei in.
Hih leitungah a thuman lo gam ukte' piansak ka muhte:
Mihaite, zalianpi kipia a, mihaute kiniamkoih suk hi.
Sakol tungah silate tuang a, miliante, sila bangin a khe-un pai uh hi.
Mipilte' kampauna in pahtawina ngahsak a, mihaite' kampauna in amau mah siasak hi.
Khuavak hoih mahmah a, i mit in nitaang a muh ciangin nuam mahmah hi.
Note kilunggimsak kei unla, na pumpi uh gentheisak kei un. Bang hang hiam cih leh na khangno hunsung uh sauvei loding hi.
Solomon'la ngaih pente:
Na muk tawh nong tawp a, na hong itna leenggahzu sangin khumzaw hi.
Ngaihno aw, hong gen dih in. Koi laiah na tuucingding a, sunin koi laiah khawlding na hi hiam? Bang hangin tuucing dangte lakah nang hong zong kawikawi masa seding ka hi hiam?
Nungak khempeuh lakah a ngaihbaang pen nungak aw, a mun thei lo na hi hiam? Tuuhonte zui in na keelte hong khah inla, tuucingpa' puanbuk geiah hongcing in.
Ngaihno aw, Faro' sakoltal in sakolpite a delh bangin nang hong kidelh hi.
Nangma a dingin kham khainiang bawlin na kizepnading zong ngun tawh bawl ni.
Ka kumpipa a lupna tungah a om laitakin ka paknamtui hong kizel hi.
Ka angah ka ngaihno hong lup laitakin myrrh paknamtui bangin namtui viauviau hi.
Ka ngaihno pen Engedi gam leenggui loah a palh lihleh pak hoihte tawh kibang hi.
Ngaihno aw, na mel hoih a, na mit zong ngaihbaang hi.
Ngaihno ngingei aw, na etlawm a, na ngaihhuai hi.
Annekna phualah hong paipih inla, itna mai tawh hong en in.
Lungzuang, duangvul ka hih manin leenggahkeu tawh hong vak inla, epelgah tawh hong thadimsak in.
A veilam baan hong khamsak a, a taklam khutin kei hong kawi hi.
Phalbi vengta a, guah zu nawn lo hi.
Khuasung cingin a pai kawikawite ka tuak a, “Ka ngaihno na mu uh hiam?” ci in ka dong hi.
Myrrh paknamtui le saledi pak namtui a kihel tawh a kibang, sumbuk a paknamtui om khempeuh a kihal khin a khu tawh a kibang, gamlak a hong khuto henhan bang ahi hiam?
Sing hoihpen tawh a kibawl luai in Kumpi Solomon hong kizawng hi.
Ngaihno aw, na ngaihbaang mahmah a, kawkbaannading na nei kei hi.
Ka lawmnu, ka naunu, a ki-umcip huan hi a, a kinei tuam tuinak ahi hi.
Ka puante suah khinzo ing. Ka puante silhkikding ka hi hiam? Ka khete sil khinzo ing; ninsakkikding ka hi hiam?
Ka ngaihno in kongkhak hong len khin napi hong taisan kik hi.
Nungak lak aa hoihpen aw, na ngaihno a bangci hiam, hong gen dih in. Tua bangin kong gen liangding uh bangzahtakin lamdang ahi hiam?
Nungak lak a hoihpen nu aw, na ngaihno, koiah pai hiam? Na ngaihno koi lam pai hiam? Amah hong zonpih nung.
Na lu khuhna puan sung panin na kho hong san lihleh hi.
Kumpi-zi sawmguk, kumpi zineu sawmgiat, simzawh lohin nungak tampi om khading a,
Zing khuavak tawh a kibang hih nungak kua ahi hiam? Amah melhoih mahmah a, nitaang, khataang, a bang hi.
Hong ciahkik in, hong ciahkik in, Shulam numei aw. Nang kong muh theih nadingun hong ciahkik in, hong ciahkik in. Shulam nungak, khanglui lai-a a lamte bangin bang hangin hong mu nuam na hi uh hiam?
Itluat aw na ngaihbaang a, na mel kong muh nuam zungzung hi.
Ka ngaihno a' ka hi a, amah in kei hong deih hi.
Ngaihno aw, gamlakah paikhia in leenggui loah va giak ni.
A veilam khut hong khamsak a, a taklam khutin hong kawi hi.
Jerusalem nungakte aw, ko' kingaihna nong suknawi loh nadingun kei tungah hong kiciam un.
Gamlak panin a lawmpa tawh khut kilensa in a hong paikhia kua ahi hiam? Nangmah na pianna mun, na nu in hong neihna mun, epel kung nuai panin nang kong phong hi.
Sanggam numeino khat ka nei uh a, a nawite neu mahmah hi. Tangval khat in hong hel zenzen leh ka sanggamnu uh bangci huhding ka hi uh hiam?
Bang hangin note hong kisat theih nadingin lehdo teitei na hi uh hiam? Israel aw, na lutang khempeuh liamma dim a, na lungsim le na ngaihsutna gim mahmah hi.
Topa'n hih bangin ci hi: “Note' biakpiakna a tampite pen kei' tungah bang hi leltak ahi hiam? Tuutalte le ganhing thaute' sathau tawh meihal biaknate ka khamta hi. Bawngtalte, tuunote, le keelte' si tawh kei ka lungkim kei hi.
Kei' maiah a kilaak dingin na hong pai uh ciangin hih bangin ka huangsung na tuatcil gawpna uh kua'n hong deihding ahi hiam?
Note' Khadet nite le na pawite uh ka mudah hi. Tuate pen kei a dingin vangikpi khat suakkhin a, tuate khempeuh ka puakna in ka gim hi.
Note kisil tawm unla, a siangtho in kibawl un. Keima muhnaah na gamtat siatnate uh paikhia in, siatna na bawlte uh khawl un.
Note'n utna lungsim nei in thu na man' nak-uhleh lei pana piang agah hoihte na neding uh hi.
A thutak, thutang tawh a kidim ngeisa khuapi, bangci-a a paktat numei tawh kibangta ahi hiam? Ama sungah thumanna om ngei napi in tu in mi thatte bek a omta hi.
Note tungah na kong semding a, meikhukah haltui bangin na saam-ek teng uh tuikhia sakin, na kihelpih na nin khempeuh uh ka lakhiading hi.
Judah gam le Jerusalem tawh kisai thu Amoz' tapa Isaiah' muhna hih bang ahi hi:
Jakob' suanlekhakte aw, hong pai un; Topa ' khuavak sungah gamta ni.
a sang, a kilaamto, Lebanon mual taamtak kung khempeuh, Bashan mual tawsaw kung khempeuh;
a lian mual sang khempeuh le a sang mualneu khempeuh;
tausang khempeuh le a muanhuai kulhte khempeuh;
Tarshish teembaw khempeuh le teembaw hoih khempeuh a niamkoih hunding ni khat a nei hi.
Milimte khempeuh mangthang khinding hi.
Mihingte muanin nei nawn kei un. Amaute leltak banga simthamding ahi hiam?
mi vanglianpa le galkap pa, thukhenpa le kamsang pa, aisanpa le upa pa,
Amaute' ulian dingin naupangte ka bawlding a, naungekte in amaute ukding uh hi.
Topa'n thupang dingin ama panmun hongla a, ama mite' thu a khen dingin ading hi.
Ka mite sucipin mizawngte na gawina uh bang na cihnopna uh a hiam?” Vanglian Topa Pasian in ci hi.
Topa'n Jerusalem numeite' lutang meima sakin Topa'n amau' lutang kolhsakding hi.
Tua ciangin Topa'n khebuh hoihte, lutuam le khade lim tawh a kibang kizepnate;
bilbah tualte, taaute, le mai sitnate;
lukhute, banbulhte, kawngtente, paknamtui bungte, le a kivom aite;
min gelhna zungbuhte le nakbuhte;
pawipuante, puanza neute, puanpite le khutkhai ipte;
puanza neu vang siseihte, saihadial puansungsilhte, dialkhipte, le kikhuhna puante lakhiading hi.
Ka leenggui lo a dingin ka hih nai loh ka hihding a kilawm bang omlai ahi hiam? Leenggah hoihgahding ka lamet laitakin bang hangin gam leenggah honggah mawk ahi hiam?
Mi khempeuh a niamin kikoih suk hi. A kiphasak mite kiniamkhiat suk hi.
Amau' mitah pil kisa a, amau' muhnaah siam a kisate in gimna ngahta hen!
Leenggahzu tampi a dawnte, khamtheih zunek a hatte,
mimawhte sumgolh tawh khah a, midikte a mawhsakte in gimna ngahta hen!
Tua ciangin, “Kua sawlding a, eite a dingin kua va paiding ahi hiam?” Topa' cihna aw ka za hi. Tua ciangin ke'n, “Hih laiah kei om ing! Kei hong sawl in,” ka ci hi.
Tua ciangin keimah in, “ Topa aw, bang tanvei sawtding ahi hiam?” ka ci hi. Amah'n, “Khuapiah a teng kuamah om loin hawm suakin, innteah kuamah om loin, leitang pen gamkhing suak kiuhkeuhin,
Topa'n gamlapiah mite khinkhia in, leitungah a kinusia mun tampi a om dong, hiding hi.
Topa'n Ahaz kiangah thu genkik a,
Ahih hangin Ahaz in, “Ka ngen keiding hi; Topa ka ze-et keiding hi,” ci hi.
Tua ciangin Isaiah in, “David' innkuan aw, ngai un! Mite na lunggim sakna uh kicing sa lo a, ka Pasian zong lunggimsak lai na hi uh hiam?
“Tua ni ciangin mi khat in bawngla khat le tuu nih bang bek suahtakzoding a,
Topa'n kei tungah thu hong genkik leuleu a,
Note kikhawmin thu na vaihawm uh hangin a mawkna suakding a, thu khat peuhpeuh na gen uh hangin kip loding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh kote tawh Pasian hong omkhawm hi.
“Hih mite' vaihawmna pawlpih kei un. Amau' kihtakte kihta kei unla, lau kei un.
Ka nungzuite aw, Pasian in kei tungah hong piak hih thute, limtakin kemin koihcing un.
Jakob' innkuante' kiang panin a maitang a seel Topa ngakin amah ka muangding hi.
Amaute'n note kiangah, “Phun suausuau in a pau mualmual vankah theite le aisan theite kiangah thu dong un. Mite'n amau' pasiante thu dongin, mihingte' thu pen misite dotding mah hi lo ahi hiam?” hong ciding uh hi.
Galkap hangte' khedap khempeuh le si a baang puan khempeuh mei in kicihding hi.
Topa'n Jakob tungah thu khat khah a, Israel tungah thu hong tungding hi.
Amaute a satpa' lamah Israel mite kihei lo a, Vanglian Topa zong lo uh hi.
Gimpiak ni hun, gamlapi panin huihpi hong nun' ciangin note in bangcihding na hi uh hiam? Huhna ngenin kua kiangah taiding a, na neihsa uh koi laiah koihding na hi uh hiam?
Assiriate pen ka hehna mite gimpiak nadingin molhtum le ciangkhutin ka zat ahi hi.
Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Ka galkapmangte, kumpi vive hikhin hi lo ahi hiam?
Kalno khuapi pen Karkhemish khuapi tawh kibang hi lo ahi hiam? Hamath khuapi pen Arpad khuapi tawh kibang hi lo ahi hiam? Samaria khuapi pen Damaskas khuapi tawh kibang hi lo ahi hiam?
Samaria le a milimte tungah ka bawl bangin Jerusalem le a milimte tungah bawl loding ka hi hiam?” ci hi.
Amah a liktopa pen molhtumin a zangding bangkeek, sing ahi lo mipa pen ciangkhut bangin a liktoding bang keekin, phuk nadingin amah a zangpa tungah, hei, kihisak theiding ahi hiam? Singat tem zong amah a zangpa tungah kiliansak theiding ahi hiam?
Jakob innkuan a omlaite a vanglian Pasian kiangah ciahkikding hi.
Amah'n tulak singte hei tawh phukding a, Lebanon mual a singkung liante tawh pukkhawmding hi.
Amah'n thuman le thutak tawh ama mite ukding hi.
Amoz' tapa Isaiah in Babylon siatnading tawh kisai a thumuhnate:
A kimu mi peuhmah kithatding a, a kiman mi peuhmah namsau tawh siding hi.
“Nang Khuavakta, Zingsol, Babylon kumpipa aw, vantung panin nang bangci kiat na hi hiam? Minamte a niam koihpa ahi nangmah leilak dongah hong bangci kiphukpai ahi hiam?
Meiite' tung pekah ka kahtoding a, Sang Penpa bangin ka kibawlding hi,' na ci hi.
Ahih hangin nang pen Leinuai thuk penna Leihawm sungah hong kikoih sukding hi.
leitung pen sehnel gam suaksakin, khuapite a susiapa, thong sungah a kikhum mite innah a ciahsak lopa hihpa hi lo ahi hiam?' hong ciding uh hi.
“Minam dangte' kumpite khempeuh amau hankhuk sung ciat uhah a minthangin lum uh hi.
Vanglian Topa kiciam khin a, “Ka geelsa bangin piangding a, ka ngimnasa bangin kipding hi.
Vanglian Topa'n ngim khin ahih manin kua in phiatzoding ahi hiam? Ama khut kizan khin ahih manin kua in kaiton kikzoding ahi hiam?
Kumpi Ahaz a sih kumin thu hong tung a,
Filistia mite in a hong sawl kamtaite mi khatpeuh in bangci dawnding ahi hiam? “ Topa'n Zion kipsak khin a, gimna a thuak ama mite in tua sungah bukna mu uh hi,” ci in a dawngding uh hi.
Tua ni ciangin Jakob' liatna beiding a, ama hauhna khempeuh mangthangding hi.
Ah, mi tampite' kikona, tuipi ging bang!ah, minamte' otna, tui lianpi ging bang!
Nail guntuite keuding a, guntui kangcipin keuding hi.
Anthul khau ciingin na a semte le patpuan a gante lungkhamding uh hi.
Gam sung makaite kisusiacipding a, a kicial nasemte dahding uh hi.
Zoan uliante hai cihtakin hai uh a, Faro' mipil thu lamlakte in thu haihuai gen uh hi. Nang in Faro' tungah, “Mipil pa' tapa ka hi hi; tanglai kumpite' tapa ka hi hi,” bangci in ci theiding na hi hiam?
Tua ahih kei leh Egypt kumpipa Faro aw, na mipilte koiah om ahi uh hiam? Vanglian Topa'n Egypt gam gimpiakding a ngimna thu, na mipilte in nangma tungah hong genthei khading hi.
Tua ni ciangin hih tuipi gei-a teng mite in, ‘En un, eite' lametna, Assiria kumpipa' kiang panin eite hong honkhia dingin i belh mite' tungah hih bang piang khinta hi. Eite bangci suahtakding ihi hiam?' ciding uh hi,” a ci hi.
Edom gam tawh kisai thu hih bangin gen hi: Seir mual tung panin khat in kei hong sam a, “Galvilpa aw, tuzan bangci hiam? Galvilpa aw, tuzan bangci hiam?” hong ci hi.
Tema gam a teng mite aw, a dangtakte tui puak unla, galtaite an tawh dawn un.
Maangmuhna Kuam tawh kisai thu hih bangin gen hi: Kikona tawh a kidim, a gamlum khuapi, lungdamin a diang khua aw, note khempeuh, innkhumzangah na kah toh uh bang na cihnopna uh ahi hiam? A kithat nangma mite pen namsau tawh a kithat hi lo a, galsung a si hi lo uh hi.
Note hong uk mite tai uh a, thal zat kul loin amaute kiman hi. Gamlapiah na tai uh hangin hong kimu note khempeuh hong kiman hi.
David khuapi mun tampi tak a siatna mu in, bual nuainung tuite na cingkik a,
nangmah in Jerusalem innte a phazah simin, kulhpi siate puahna dingin innte na phel hi.
Hih laiah nangma ading hankhuk a to, a sangna munah hankhuk a bawl, na omnading suang a khuak mipa aw, nang in hih laiah bang hih a, vuiding kua nei na hi hiam?
“Tua ni ciangin Hikiah' tapa ahi ka nasempa Eliakim ka samding a,
Tuipi gei-a teng mite aw, Tarshish khuaah tai in kap un!

Tarshish teembaw hawlte aw, na muan uh khuapi kisiata ahih manin thumin kap un.

Kei vaiphei..zomi kahi lou kuki kahie
Kuki is name give to all of us by bengal. Yes, for Bengali people we  were all known as kuki. Zomi name or group was formed in Myanmar by paite ( know as tedim in Myanmar) though there might be some similarities vaiphei are ethnically distinct from paite, tedim (zomi). Their language, flag everything is same, vaiphei have different language and no such flag.
Zomi nam was formed by paite ( also known as tedim in Myanmar) vaiphei were not part of it when it was formed.

I'm learning several languages on Duolingo. My grandson asked if he could learn Zumi, as many of his classmates, here in Jenks,OK,are Zumi. Let me go on to say, this suburb of Tulsa, OK (population approximately 5,000 Zumi) is a highly rated school district with many helpful programs for Zumi children and their parents. They even have their own translator, who parents can call for questions or concerns. I sent my grandson to school today with a word written on a card,  it says : zingpah. He's eager to say it to his new friends today!
If anyone is interested in getting their children into a five star school, Jenks will welcome you! their are several inexpensive apartments in Tulsa which are in Jenks school district. (Jenks housing is more expensive). If you come to live in Tulsa, be SURE you get a home in Jenks school district! There are Zumi churches in Tulsa too. Welcome! Thank you for your video!

Identity i cih pen Absolute Truth hilo hi, A hun leh a mun tawh kikhel thei den ahih manin Identity politics kimawl pen lauhuai leh buaina hong tun thei ding hi.

Zomi Tangthu by Dr. Gin Khan Khual — a compelling sermon on Zomi identity, history, and true meaning of belief. Dr. Khual discusses the origins of the Zomi people from ancient Zo roots, how Zomi history began, the evolution of Zomi identity, and how their faith and culture have spread from early civilization (including mentions of Zo roots possibly tied to ancient Chinese regions) through Myanmar, India, and across the world.

In the diaspora, we unfortunately don’t always have easy access to this pure product. Therefore, this video’s purpose, is to demonstrate the ease with which one can make Zomi at home, regardless of geographical location, using one main ingredient. The palm nut fruit cream is readily accessible, and available as a canned product in most African stores worldwide.

My Dear I am watching from Richmond Hill ga 👍
Zomi in Ewe simply means  hot pressed oil.so whether the salt or not since it is   extracted with by fire it's called zomi. However some people  extract the palm oil using the cold press method ....... mostly the cold pressed it not seasoned with salt and onion. You can also add some slices of  onions to it the next time you make  it( after you have added the salt).And also you could  have gotten alot of  oil  if you had chilled  the palm paste before  adding  the water. Traditionally  the palm paste is mostly  left in a very  cold place over night as it helps to intensify the flavour in the palm.

A  (78 )vei na  ZO MI  NAM  NI.
Tukum 2026 kum pen koi koi ah ki bawl Tek in ahi zongin Lamka. leh Malaysia  ah nopcit takin ki bawl zihziah in lungkim huaimahmah hi. Mundang te ah ahih leh phawkna Ciang tawhki bawl bek hi. Tuapen khua Hun hoihloh hang ahihmanin lungdam huai veve hi. Zominamni akibawlna keimuhna teng ahih leh Malaysia, Lamka, Aizawl, Singapore, Rangoon, hin bang aa zominamni  ih bawl lohna te ah  aom koten zong akibawl na kamuh uh Ciang na  a Ng tang mahmah hi ingh.(Zomite) ihpasian in Mai nawt dingleh akithu tuak diam diam dingin thupha hongpia kimciat tahen.
Zominamni lambangpaakding Lia leh taang ihkim na m aw. Tuam pupa ten mabangpatsa khangsawn ten giabangzun lenge.
Tha ngah hang ei. Zomite Topan thupha hong peta hen.

Journey into the heart of one of Asia’s most remarkable indigenous communities. ZOMI ORIGIN uncovers the ancient roots, migration paths, cultural identity, and enduring spirit of the Zomi people—told through history, legend, research, and lived experience.
Long before the India–Myanmar border was drawn, Zogam already existed. The Zomi people were living on these ancestral hills, building villages, preserving culture across what is now divided by an international line.

Israel's ambassador to Australia Hillel Newman was asked several questions about Australian aid worker Zomi Frankcom, who was killed by an IDF strike in Gaza, in a National Press Club address. He refused to make a direct apology for her death.
Zomi's brother Mal Frankcom has told the ABC he is still seeking accountability for his sister's death after two years of no answers.
Zomi Frankcom died in a strike, along with six others, including British, US and Canadian charity workers.
On Oct. 7, the Zomi community in Australia held its new year celebration, known as Khuado Pawi. The Zomi ethnic group comes from northern Chin State. It holds Khuado Pawi each year to pray for a good harvest and for the health of its community. This year, prayers were made for Myanmar's permanent representative to the U.N. Kyaw Moe Tun, to remain in his position representing the National Unity Government (NUG) at the international level.
Israel has apologised for an airstrike that killed seven aid workers in Gaza including Australian Zomi Frankcom, claiming it was a ‘grave mistake’.
A friend of Australian aid worker Zomi Frankcom, who was killed while working in Gaza by a reported Israeli air strike, says the woman was "huge-hearted" and "relentless" in her efforts to help others.

We are not Kuki Zo, We are Zomi Zo
@bmuanngaihte  We are Same. We are Kuki We are Zomi. There no much Difference. Even in Our Dialect in Thado 'Zo' or 'Zou' means Hill Areas or Hilly and 'Mi' means Human or People. So Zomi means Hilly People or in our Dialect 'Thinglhang Mi' . The main Reason why 'Let us Call Ourselves KUKI' is it has a Larger Scope. Most People apart from Our Community knows us as Kuki. Not only Thadou even Simte Zou Vaiphei Paite Gangte Kom Hmar Chiru etc. fought the British for 3 years & they name us Kuki, they wrote our History as Kuki Rebellion 1917-1919. The day we throw away The name Kuki is the day we lost Our History. Before 97 we lived together our mindset was One, even in Kuki-Naga Conflict many Ngaite Guite Hangshing were killed by Nscn-IM. In simple way among ourselves in our dialect We are Zomi we can agree with that but internationally we are KUKI just like in Germany, in their Own dialect they call themselves Deutsch People or Deutschland but in international we know them as German People or Germany. We Can call Ourselves Zomi but we also should agree that we are Kuki too, this will be the only way to heal our Society💓
But Zomi is not under Kuki ..Zomi is Zomi.. we are struggling for that too,its gonna be hard and tough we forseen that , possibly bunch of discrimination we might face but we ought to stand up and be recognised from all through that. Because we are not STUPID.
Longlive zomi ❤❤❤
We ,Zomi,are absolutely not a Kuki but I respect your opinion..We might be facing bunch of discrimination as per  Zomis,but we still keep on struggling for that as nothing comes easy as it seems to rise but we ought to face every obstacles,got recognised as well like others oneday but till then we ain't back down.. Zomi is not under Kuki and Zomi is not same with Kuki.Zomi is ZOMI . *(Conversation over)*peep
